### [75] [RODS: Reward-Driven Online Data Synthesis for Multi-Turn Tool-Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19047)
*Ruishan Fang,Siyuan Lu,Chenyi Zhuang,Tao Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对多轮工具使用任务中因静态样本枯竭导致的强化学习效率瓶颈，本文提出了RODS方法。该方法利用奖励方差在线合成模型能力边界上的新样本，实现了样本的高效循环利用，在仅使用少量原始数据的情况下达到了大规模数据集的训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮工具使用强化学习主要受限于静态数据集中的高质量样本会被迅速耗尽。研究发现，梯度信号倾向于集中在成功与失败平衡的“能力边界”样本上，随着训练深入，这些样本在静态数据集中会逐渐枯竭，导致训练效率下降。

Method: 本文提出了RODS（奖励驱动在线数据合成）方法。其核心机制是将进度奖励方差用作无需额外推理成本的“边界检测器”，实时识别模型能力边界上的样本；随后通过基于技能对齐的重采样流水线，合成与原样本结构复杂性一致的新多轮任务变体，并维护一个随策略进化的动态回放缓冲区。

Result: RODS仅使用400个人工标注种子样本和约800个活跃训练样本，即可达到拥有17,000个样本的离线训练管线的性能水平。与传统的固定数据集强化学习和环境增强方法相比，RODS在受控实验中展现出了显著的性能提升和极高的样本效率（所需轨迹减少约20倍）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的RODS框架成功解决了多轮工具使用强化学习中静态数据集样本枯竭的问题。通过利用奖励方差动态合成边界样本，该方法在大幅减少对原始数据依赖的同时，实现了与大规模静态数据集相当甚至更好的性能，为高效的工具调用模型训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Multi-turn tool-use RL is bottlenecked by the rapid depletion of informative samples in static datasets. We observe that the gradient signal in GRPO concentrates on tasks with the highest rollout reward variance, a consequence of the Popoviciu upper bound. Consequently, samples near the agent's capability boundary -- where successes and failures are roughly balanced -- contribute disproportionately large policy gradients. As training progresses, this boundary continuously shifts, which gradually depletes the pool of informative samples in a static dataset. We propose RODS (Reward-driven Online Data Synthesis) to resolve this depletion. RODS closes the loop between RL training and data generation by repurposing the progress reward variance as a practical, zero-cost boundary detector that requires no extra inference beyond the rollouts already computed for training. It continuously identifies such boundary samples, synthesizes new multi-turn variants matching their structural complexity (e.g., API topology and dependency depth) via a skill-aligned resampling pipeline, and manages a dynamic replay buffer that co-evolves with the policy. Starting from 400 human seeds and maintaining an active training pool of ~800 samples, RODS achieves comparable performance to a 17K-sample offline pipeline while requiring roughly 20x fewer trajectories, and improves over fixed-data RL and environment augmentation in our controlled setting.

</details>


### [76] [ARIADNE: Agnostic Routing for Inference-time Adapter DyNamic sElection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19079)
*Enrico Cassano,Michał Brzozowski,Zuzanna Dubanowska,Paolo Mandica,Neo Christopher Chung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ARIADNE 是一种无需训练的通用适配器路由框架，通过将输入嵌入与适配器训练集的质心进行匹配，实现了在缺乏标签的情况下自动、高效地为推理请求选择最佳适配器，且兼容所有 PEFT 方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着参数高效微调（PEFT）的广泛应用，系统中存在大量针对不同任务的适配器，但推理时往往缺乏任务标签。现有的路由方法通常依赖适配器内部参数或需要额外训练，难以扩展到动态增长的异构适配器池。因此，需要一种无需训练、兼容性强且无需访问适配器内部的自动路由机制。

Method: ARIADNE 提出了一种免训练（training-free）且与适配器无关（adapter-agnostic）的路由框架。该方法通过计算每个适配器训练集嵌入的质心（centroids）来表征该适配器的数据分布，在推理时，通过计算未标注输入的嵌入与各适配器质心在潜在空间内的距离，动态选择最合适的适配器。

Result: 在 Llama 3.2 1B Instruct 模型和 23 个 NLP 任务的评估中，ARIADNE 恢复了 97.44% 的性能上限；在扩展至 44 个任务时，依然保持了 89.7% 的平均选择准确率，且无需任何额外的训练或对适配器内部的访问。

Conclusion: ARIADNE 证明了通过在潜在空间内测量输入与适配器训练数据分布（质心）的相似度，可以无需额外训练和内部访问权限，实现高效且通用的适配器路由选择，为大规模适配器生态系统提供了一种可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: The increasing deployment of parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) has led to model ecosystems in which a single backbone is paired with many task-specialized adapters. In this setting, inference-time queries often arrive without task labels, requiring the system to automatically select the most appropriate adapter from a growing and heterogeneous adapter pool. Existing routing methods either depend on access to adapter internals, such as weight decompositions or gradient-based statistics, or require additional router training, which limits scalability and portability as new adapters are added. We introduce ARIADNE, a training-free, adapter-agnostic routing framework for dynamic adapter selection at inference time. ARIADNE represents each adapter through a set of centroids computed from embeddings of its training set, capturing the data distribution associated with that adapter. Given an unlabeled input, it selects an adapter by measuring proximity to these centroids in latent space. Because routing is performed entirely in the input embedding space, ARIADNE is compatible with arbitrary PEFT methods and requires no modification to the adapters or training procedures. Primarily evaluated with Llama 3.2 1B Instruct on 23 diverse NLP tasks, ARIADNE recovers 97.44% of the upper bound performance. Scaling to 44 tasks, it achieves 89.7% average selection accuracy, without additional training or access to adapter internals.

</details>


### [77] [Towards an Agent-First Web: Redesigning the Web for AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19116)
*Eranga Bandara,Ross Gore,Ravi Mukkamala,Asanga Gunaratna,Safdar H. Bouk,Xueping Liang,Peter Foytik,Abdul Rahman,Sachini Rajapakse,Isurunima Kularathna,Pramoda Karunarathna,Chalani Rajapakse,Ng Wee Keong,Kasun De Zoysa,Tharaka Hewa,Amin Hass,Wathsala Herath,Aruna Withanage,Nilaan Loganathan,Atmaram Yarlagadda,Sachin Shetty*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对互联网因AI代理兴起而导致的底层逻辑失效，本文提出了“代理优先”互联网框架，通过在访问、经济和内容三个层面实施技术与规范重构，将AI代理整合为互联网的一等公民，以解决现有抵制策略带来的效率低下与内容质量退化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 互联网架构长期建立在“人类是唯一内容消费者”的假设之上，而AI代理的兴起使该假设失效。当前的Web生态通过封锁、验证码及排斥性经济模型对抗AI，导致代理与互联网之间存在严重冲突，亟需更新社会契约以适应代理主导的未来。

Method: 本文提出了“代理优先”互联网的三层重构方案：1. 访问层：引入标准化的代理身份标识与速率限制，并推行“双层架构”以同时适配人类与机器；2. 经济层：建立基于代理作为人类代理人原则的意图导向框架，推行以Token（代币/标记）计费的订阅模型，并锚定人类意图的创作经济；3. 内容层：针对“认识论递归”风险，提出了代理文本标记语言（ATML）、四级人类监督模型及加密溯源链。

Result: 提出了构建“代理优先”互联网的十项基本原则。通过系统性地调整访问机制、经济激励模型以及内容生产与验证流程，该方案能够有效缓解AI生成的“认识论递归”风险，实现人类与AI代理在互联网环境下的共生与互利。

Conclusion: 互联网的现有社会契约已不再适用于以AI代理为主导的新时代。本文提出的“代理优先”互联网架构，通过在访问、经济和内容层面的根本性重构，旨在将AI代理确立为互联网的一等公民，从而解决当前Web平台与AI代理之间的对立与脱节问题。

Abstract: The World Wide Web was built on an assumption held for three decades: the primary consumer of web content is a human being. This permeates every layer; its access model presumes human visitors, its economics rest on human attention, and its content targets human perception. The rapid emergence of AI agents as intermediaries between humans and web content invalidates this assumption. Yet the web resists agents through blanket blocking, CAPTCHA-based exclusion, and economic models that treat agent access as extraction rather than legitimate interaction.
  This paper proposes a principled redesign across three layers. At the access layer, agents acting for humans should inherit equivalent access rights, governed by rate limiting and agent identification metadata in HTTP requests, analogous to browser headers, alongside a dual-layer architecture serving human-readable and agent-optimized content from the same domain. At the economic layer, we propose an intent-based tier framework grounded in the agent-as-human-proxy principle: an agent's economic obligation mirrors that of the human it represents. A token-based subscription model meters content in tokens rather than pageviews, alongside a commissioned content economy anchoring AI content production in human intentionality. At the content layer, we identify epistemic recursion, the self-referential loop in which AI-generated content is consumed by agents to produce further content, progressively detaching web knowledge from human ground truth. We propose the Agent Text Markup Language (ATML), a four-level human supervision tier model, and a cryptographic provenance chain to counter this threat.
  Together these constitute ten design principles for an agent-first internet, one in which agents are first-class citizens whose integration requires renegotiating the web's foundational social contract across access, economics, and content.

We employ SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations) to quantify feature contributions and apply and extend SSHAP, an aggregation framework to improve interpretability in high-dimensional settings. The analysis identifies that renewable energy sources, particularly solar, play a disproportionately important role in price formation despite their lower share in total power generation. Gas prices remain a dominant and consistent driver across electricity markets, while interconnections significantly shape price dynamics, highlighting the strong interdependence of European electricity systems. Abstract: Current conversational AI systems have made significant progress in language generation, personalization, and long-context interaction. However, most existing methods model social behavior through isolated components such as emotion modeling, memory retrieval, or persona conditioning, lacking a unified framework to explain the emergence of stable social relationships and social intelligence in long-term human-AI interaction.To address this, we propose the Human-AI Coevolution Dynamics Framework (HACD-H), a formal model of human-AI interaction as a self-organizing social cognitive system. HACD-H integrates emotional adaptation, relational organization, social memory, and personality consistency into a unified dynamical framework and introduces principles including multi-timescale social cognition, relational attractors, trust basins, developmental phase transitions, and social cognitive energy dynamics.We construct a conversational dataset with approximately 14,700 interaction turns and develop a theory-driven empirical evaluation framework. Results reveal a hierarchy of temporal persistence in social cognition, stable relational attractors, phase-transition-like developmental patterns, and a structured social cognitive energy landscape. HACD-H provides a unified theoretical foundation for modeling adaptive human-AI social interaction and developing socially intelligent AI systems.

### [80] [Beyond Safe Data: Pretraining-Stage Alignment with Regular Safety Reflection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19168)
*Jinhan Li,Kexian Tang,Yihan Xu,Zhuorui Ye,Kaifeng Lyu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“安全反射预训练”方法，通过在预训练数据中嵌入安全反射机制，从模型行为塑造的层面提升了大语言模型的内生安全性，有效防御了基于良性数据组合产生的潜在不安全行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预训练安全对齐主要依赖于过滤或重写不安全数据，但这种做法忽略了模型可能将看起来“无害”的知识和能力组合成不安全行为的风险。因此，研究旨在探索如何在预训练阶段建立深层的安全对齐机制。

Method: 提出了“安全反射预训练”（Safety Reflection Pretraining）方法，通过在预训练语料中定期插入简短的安全反射内容，将自我监控能力直接整合进语言建模过程中；并构建了受控的合成环境MedSafetyWorld用于评估模型的安全泛化能力。

Result: 在1.7B模型上的实验表明，该方法显著提高了安全分类准确率，并大幅降低了推理阶段和微调攻击的成功率。在MedSafetyWorld环境下的消融实验证明，相比于传统的数据过滤和重写，该方法在防止模型从安全数据中泛化出不安全行为方面具有明显优势。

Conclusion: 预训练阶段的安全对齐不应仅限于数据清洗或重写，更应致力于塑造模型从良性数据中推导潜在危险行为的能力。通过在预训练过程中嵌入安全反射机制，模型能够建立起内生的自我监控能力，从而更有效地防御各类攻击。

Abstract: To achieve deeper safety alignment for large language models (LLMs), recent efforts have studied how to push safety interventions earlier into the pretraining stage, primarily by filtering unsafe data or rewriting it into safer forms. We argue that pretraining-stage alignment should go beyond making the data safe: LLMs may compose seemingly benign knowledge and capabilities into unsafe behaviors. To this end, we propose Safety Reflection Pretraining, a pretraining-stage alignment method which regularly inserts short safety reflections into pretraining corpora to integrate self-monitoring directly into language modeling, establishing a foundational capability that is subsequently reinforced by compatible post-training. Our experiments with 1.7B models pretrained on FineWeb-Edu show that Safety Reflection Pretraining improves safety classification accuracy and substantially reduces the success rates of inference-stage and finetuning attacks. Complementary to our real-world experiments, we also introduce a fully controlled synthetic environment, MedSafetyWorld, with a clear definition of safety and a reasoning structure under which models can easily generalize unsafe behaviors from safe data. Ablations in MedSafetyWorld further demonstrate a clear advantage of Safety Reflection Pretraining in preventing models from acting on unsafe behaviors generalized from safe data, compared with data filtering and rewriting. Taken together, our findings suggest that pretraining alignment should not only make the training data safe, but also shape the behaviors that models are likely to acquire from safe data.

### [81] [User as Engram: Internalizing Per-User Memory as Local Parametric Edits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19172)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出“User as Engram”架构，通过将个性化事实与模型推理技能解耦，在实现超高压缩比（33,000x）和多用户无损存储的同时，显著提升了模型的间接推理能力，解决了传统LoRA方法导致的知识污染和推理退化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的个性化方法（如LoRA）将事实（内容）和推理（技能）混合在同一个全局权重增量中，导致模型记忆事实时会污染与用户无关的文本，并可能损害模型的通用推理能力；此外，基于检索的方法在大规模用户场景下存在效率瓶颈。

Method: 提出“User as Engram”方法：将用户的个性化内容存储为Engram模型哈希键控内存表中的手术式编辑，而将推理技能保留在单一共享的适配器中。通过这种层级化设计，实现了事实存储与技能更新的物理分离，支持多用户事实的加法堆叠且无损。

Result: 相比于传统的每用户LoRA，该方法在保持直接召回能力的同时，间接推理准确率平均提升了5.6倍，且不会损害基础模型的推理能力。存储方面，其内存占用量减少了约33,000倍，且由于采用哈希表存储，不同用户的事实可以无损叠加，实现了极高的扩展性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“User as Engram”架构通过将个性化事实（内容）与推理能力（技能）解耦，不仅实现了极其高效的存储，还避免了传统LoRA方法对模型基础能力的损害，为大规模个性化语言模型提供了一种可扩展且性能优越的新方案。

Abstract: Personal memory in a language model is two problems: content and reasoning skill. The brain keeps the two apart (a sparse, local engram in the hippocampus for each episode, a slow neocortex for the shared skills that interpret it), so a new fact need not overwrite everything else. Most personalization today keeps a user's facts outside the weights, in a natural-language memory file or a retrieval index. When facts are written into the model instead, the standard recipe is the per-user LoRA adapter, which does the opposite of the brain, folding content and skill into one global weight delta. Writing a user's facts as a LoRA contaminates text unrelated to them; writing the same facts as local Engram rows leaves it mathematically untouched, resulting in a roughly 33,000x smaller memory footprint.
  We therefore propose User as Engram: store a user's content as surgical edits to the hash-keyed memory table of an Engram model, and carry the reasoning skill in one shared adapter. This layered design matches per-user LoRA's direct recall while delivering 5.6x higher indirect-reasoning accuracy on average, and never makes a single user worse at reasoning than the untouched base. The edit is a glass box: writing a fact switches on its lookup at exactly the trigger, adds the value the answer needs, leaves every other position unchanged to the last bit, and fails if written into the wrong layer. Because different users' facts land in disjoint hash slots, their edits compose: many users live in one shared table at once, stacking additively and losslessly, where a per-user LoRA, a single global weight delta, admits only one. Upon retrieval, a per-user Engram table does not grow with the population the retriever must search, so past ~100 facts it overtakes a retrieval pipeline on a 2.5x larger model.

</details>


### [82] [TxBench-PP: Analyzing AI Agent Performance on Small-Molecule Preclinical Pharmacology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19245)
*Hannah Le,Ramesh Ramasamy,Alex Urrutia,Mahsa Yazdani,Tim Proctor,Kenny Workman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文推出了首个专注于小分子临床前药理学的评估基准 TxBench-PP，通过真实研发数据测试 AI 智能体的决策水平。结果显示，尽管 AI 在药物发现领域潜力巨大，但目前最先进的模型在处理真实药理学决策任务时成功率普遍偏低，远未达到可实际部署的标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI 智能体被认为有望通过加速药物研发的决策循环来提升效率，但目前缺乏针对真实药理学决策的可信评估标准。现有的评估多依赖模型对文献知识的记忆，而非针对真实实验数据的分析推理。因此，作者开发了 TxBench-PP，旨在评估智能体从真实药物研发实验数据中提取准确决策的能力。

Method: 研究构建了 TxBench-PP 基准测试集，包含 100 个由真实临床前药理学数据构成的评估任务。评估流程要求 AI 智能体在编码环境中处理真实的工作流快照（如文件检查），并返回确定性的结构化答案。研究通过 16 种模型组合（共 4800 次实验轨迹）对智能体进行基准测试，重点考察其在机制分析、药效推理、靶点验证及安全性评估等方面的表现。

Result: 在 16 种测试配置中，没有一个系统能稳定且可靠地完成临床前药理学决策任务。表现最好的 Claude Opus 4.8 / Pi 配置仅通过了 59.3% 的端点测试，GPT-5.5 / Pi 紧随其后为 55.3%。研究表明，当前的 AI 模型在处理实际药物研发的复杂场景时表现远未达到行业要求。

Conclusion: TxBench-PP 揭示了当前主流 AI 智能体在处理复杂的临床前药理学决策时仍存在显著局限性。要实现药物研发的自动化，AI 不仅需要提升数据解读能力，还需具备更强的逻辑推理与跨学科决策能力，现有的模型尚无法可靠地支撑真实的药物开发工作。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) agents promise to accelerate drug discovery by compressing interpretation and decision-making loops, but practical deployment requires trusted evaluation on realistic program decisions. We introduce TherapeuticsBench Preclinical Pharmacology (TxBench-PP), a verifiable benchmark for small-molecule preclinical pharmacology and the first focused slice of a broader TherapeuticsBench effort across drug-discovery stages and therapeutic modalities. TxBench-PP tests whether agents can recover accurate conclusions from real-world assay data rather than memorized facts from literature. The benchmark contains 100 evaluations indexed by program stage, assay type, and task structure, spanning mechanism-of-action (MoA) and pharmacodynamic (PD) reasoning, compound-target engagement, causal target validation, developability and safety, and translational efficacy. Agents receive realistic workflow snapshots, inspect files in a coding environment, and return structured answers graded deterministically. Across 16 model-harness configurations, comprising 11 models and 4,800 trajectories, no system reliably recovered preclinical pharmacology decisions. The strongest configuration, Claude Opus 4.8 / Pi, passed 59.3\% of endpoint attempts (178/300; 95\% CI, 51.1-67.6), followed by GPT-5.5 / Pi at 55.3\% (166/300; 47.0-63.6).

### [83] [X+Slides: Benchmarking Audience-Conditioned Slide Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19256)
*Haodong Chen,Xuanhe Zhou,Wei Zhou,Xinyue Shao,Yanbing Zhu,Bo Wang,Jiawei Hong,Anya Jia,Fan Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了面向特定受众的演示文稿生成基准测试X+Slides，旨在解决现有模型在内容针对性和信息源可追溯性评估方面的缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的演示文稿自动生成基准测试主要关注完整性和技术深度，忽略了“受众类型”这一现实中关键的考量因素，导致生成的幻灯片无法满足特定受众（如专家或决策者）的差异化需求。

Method: 提出了X+Slides基准测试，包含113个主题和七种演示场景。构建了基于8133个去重、有源文档支持的探针（probes）的动态评估框架，通过分配受众特定的效用权重，衡量受众覆盖率、领域覆盖率、效率和准确性四个指标。

Result: 对DeepPresenter、SlideTailor和NotebookLM的实验表明，当前系统在提取受众必需信息方面存在局限，受众覆盖率仍不理想（最高为0.853），且系统之间在信息来源的准确性和关联性方面表现出显著差异。

Conclusion: 现有的大型语言模型在生成演示文稿时，虽然能覆盖部分主题，但在针对不同受众需求（如专家与决策者）的精准适配上仍有显著欠缺。研究强调，视觉质量和话题覆盖率不能替代基于源文档的严谨评估，未来的系统需在保证信息源可追溯性的前提下，实现更具针对性的内容生成。

Abstract: Automatically generating slide decks from source documents is an important application of large language models (LLMs). Existing benchmarks primarily assess slide completeness and technical depth, while overlooking the target audience as a critical real-world factor. For instance, specialists demand rigorous proofs, whereas decision-makers prioritize actionable conclusions. To bridge this gap, we introduce X+Slides, a benchmark specifically designed for audience-conditioned slide generation. Built on a diverse corpus spanning 113 topics and seven presentation scenes, X+Slides employs a dynamic evaluation framework constructed from 8,133 deduplicated, source-grounded probes. By assigning audience-specific utility weights to the same source-grounded probes, X+Slides reports four complementary metrics: Audience Coverage measures how much audience-essential information is conveyed, Domain-wise Coverage shows which information types are covered, Efficiency measures delivered utility per unit of attention cost, and Correctness verifies whether slide claims are supported by the source. Experiments on DeepPresenter, SlideTailor, and NotebookLM show that current systems can recover a substantial but still incomplete part of audience-essential information: at $τ_A=0.7$, DeepPresenter reaches a best Audience Coverage of 0.714, SlideTailor reaches 0.594, and the NotebookLM ablation reaches 0.853 while showing clear grounding differences. These results indicate that visual quality and broad topic coverage should not be treated as evidence support without source-grounded evaluation.

</details>


### [84] [NeSyCat Torch: A Differentiable Tensor Implementation of Categorical Semantics for Neurosymbolic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19279)
*Daniel Romero Schellhorn,Till Mossakowski,Björn Gehrke*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 NeSyCat Torch，通过 monad（单子）抽象实现了神经符号语义的统一，在保持高效训练的同时，超越了多个现有 NeSy 系统的性能，提供了一个可扩展的逻辑与深度学习结合框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经符号（NeSy）语义研究处于碎片化状态（如经典、模糊、概率和神经网络系统各自为政），且 NeSyCat 框架此前缺乏对神经网络学习的谓词和函数的支持，限制了其在实际深度学习任务中的应用。该研究旨在通过 NeSyCat Torch 填补这一空白，建立统一的归纳真值定义。

Method: 该研究引入了 NeSyCat Torch，通过将计算符号解释为神经网络，并利用单子（monad）抽象来实现逻辑规则。具体采用了分布单子（distribution monad）进行语义推导，使用惰性对数张量单子（lazy log-tensor monad）确保数值稳定性与可微训练，并结合批量单子（batch monad）实现高效并行计算。该框架通过 monad-based do-notation 编写代码，自动处理边缘化与分支剪枝。

Result: 在 MNIST 加法任务的实验中，基于 HaskTorch、JAX 和 PyTorch 的 NeSyCat Torch 实现方案在速度和准确率上均优于 LTN 和 DeepProbLog，并达到了与 DeepStochLog 相当的准确率，同时具备了更广泛的适用性。

Conclusion: NeSyCat Torch 提供了一个统一的神经符号框架，不仅在性能上超越了现有的多个基准系统（如 LTN 和 DeepProbLog），还通过单子（monad）参数化实现了理论上的高度可扩展性，为处理复杂逻辑推理和神经网络学习提供了一种严谨且高效的通用范式。

Abstract: Neurosymbolic semantics is fragmented: classical, fuzzy, probabilistic and neural systems each define truth by their own inductive rules. NeSyCat, extending ULLER, subsumes them under a single inductive definition of truth, parametric in a strong monad and an aggregation structure on truth-values. NeSyCat has so far lacked an account of predicates and functions learned by neural networks.
  We provide NeSyCat Torch as the missing link and interpret computational symbols via neural networks, implementing the framework in probabilistic programming and tensor-based backends. We use the distribution monad for reference semantics and metric evaluation, and complement it by a monad for numerically stable, differentiable training: the lazy log-tensor monad over the log-semiring. For efficient training in batches, we furthermore employ a batch monad. The axioms are the source code: written once in monad-based do-notation, monadic bind performs marginalisation, lazily pruning unneeded branches.
  On MNIST addition, our HaskTorch, JAX, and PyTorch implementations outperform LTN and DeepProbLog in speed and accuracy, while achieving nearly the accuracy of DeepStochLog. However, unlike DeepStochLog, we stay in a uniform framework that applies to many first-order NeSy approaches. Namely, the construction is parametric in the monad; instantiating it with, e.g., the Giry monad extends the approach to continuous probability (working out a neural representation here is left for future work).

</details>


### [85] [Rethinking Reward Supervision: Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19327)
*Siyi Gu,Jialin Chen,Sophia Zhou,Arman Cohan,Rex Ying*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对推理模型训练中蒸馏数据标注昂贵和强化学习奖励反馈稀疏的问题，本文提出了一种“基于评价准则的自我蒸馏”框架，通过引入结构化的评价准则提供细粒度的令牌级指导，显著提升了模型的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理语言模型的后训练方法存在局限性：监督蒸馏依赖昂贵且可能有噪声的思维链标注；而基于强化学习的验证奖励将反馈压缩为单一标量，难以精确指导推理过程的改进。因此，作者旨在引入结构化、细粒度的评价准则来替代单一的参考路径，以优化推理过程。

Method: 该论文提出了一种“基于评价准则的自我蒸馏”（Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation）框架，包含两个阶段：第一阶段训练模型生成任务特定的评价准则（Rubrics）；第二阶段利用这些评价准则对学生的采样路径提供令牌级别的指导，从而实现比标量奖励优化更细粒度的信用分配。

Result: 在多个科学推理基准测试中，该方法表现优异，平均性能分别超过了GRPO方法1.0个百分点和OPSD方法0.9个百分点。

Conclusion: “基于评价准则的自我蒸馏”框架成功证明了将细粒度评价准则转化为推理过程中的令牌级指导，能够有效提升推理模型的性能，并为解决现有训练范式（蒸馏数据昂贵、强化学习奖励反馈稀疏）的局限性提供了一种更优的替代方案。

Abstract: Post-training of reasoning language models is commonly driven by supervised distillation and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. Distillation often relies on chain-of-thought annotations that are expensive to obtain and may themselves be noisy, incomplete, or partially incorrect; even when the final solution is correct, an imperfect rationale can interfere with learning. Reinforcement learning with verified rewards, on the other hand, typically compresses evaluative feedback into a scalar signal, obscuring which aspects of a response should be improved. We propose \textbf{Rubric-Conditioned Self-Distillation}, a framework that incorporates rubrics as structured, fine-grained feedback for on-policy self-distillation. Our method conditions the teacher model on criterion-level rubrics and uses it to provide token-level guidance on the student's own sampled trajectories. This design avoids treating a single reference rationale as the sole supervision target. Instead, rubrics specify what a strong response should satisfy, enabling more fine-grained credit assignment over the reasoning process than scalar reward optimization. We instantiate this framework with a two-stage pipeline that first learns to generate task-specific rubrics and then trains a rubric-guided reasoner. We evaluate on a diverse suite of science reasoning benchmarks and results show that rubric-conditioned self-distillation effectively converts rubric-level criteria into token-level guidance over the reasoning process, surpassing GRPO by 1.0 points and OPSD by 0.9 points on average.

</details>

### [86] [RankGraph-2: Lifecycle Co-Design for Billion-Node Graph Learning in Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18379)
*Renzhi Wu,Zikun Cui,Junjie Yang,Tai Guo,Hong Li,Xian Chen,Li Yu,Ke Pan,Sri Reddy,Mahesh Srinivasan,Nipun Mathur,Haomin Yu,Hong Yan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Meta提出的RankGraph-2框架通过深度协同图构建、表示学习与服务索引这三个阶段，实现了十亿级节点下的高效精准检索，大幅优化了计算资源消耗并显著提升了点击率和转化率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图检索工作通常将图构建、表示学习和实时服务三个紧密耦合的问题孤立处理，导致系统效率低下且无法满足工业界超大规模（十亿级节点）的应用需求。

Method: 提出了RankGraph-2框架：1. 通过包含人气偏置校正的子采样技术将边数压缩至千亿规模；2. 利用个性化PageRank预计算多跳邻域以消除在线图基础设施；3. 协同训练残差量化（Residual-Quantization）聚类索引以优化在线检索性能。

Result: RankGraph-2在服务计算成本上降低了83%；在双向图上的召回率比GAT+Deep Graph Infomax模型提升了3.8倍，比PyTorch-BigGraph提升了2.1倍；在实际业务中实现了CTR提升0.96%和CVR提升2.75%，并已支撑Meta超过20个检索场景的上线。

Conclusion: RankGraph-2通过将图构建、表示学习和实时服务三个生命周期阶段进行协同设计，成功解决了大规模图检索中的耦合问题，不仅显著降低了计算成本，还显著提升了业务指标，证明了全生命周期协同优化在工业级推荐系统中的巨大价值。

Abstract: Graph-based retrieval at billion-node scale requires jointly solving three tightly coupled problems -- graph construction, representation learning, and real-time serving -- yet existing work addresses each in isolation. We present RankGraph-2, a framework deployed at Meta that co-designs all three lifecycle stages for similarity-based retrieval (U2U2I and U2I2I), where each stage's requirements shape the others. Serving requires a co-learned cluster index to avoid expensive online KNN -- this pushes index co-training into the training objective. Training benefits from the observation that similarity-based retrieval tolerates pre-computed neighborhoods, eliminating online graph infrastructure -- this requires construction to produce self-contained data. Construction must also support hour-level refresh for item coverage. Acting on these cascading requirements, RankGraph-2 reduces hundreds of trillions of edges to hundreds of billions via subsampling with popularity bias correction, pre-computes multi-hop neighborhoods via personalized PageRank, and co-learns a residual-quantization cluster index that reduces serving computational cost by 83%. This lifecycle co-design enables a simple architecture to achieve 3.8 x higher recall than a GAT + Deep Graph Infomax model on a bipartite graph and 2.1 x higher than PyTorch-BigGraph on item retrieval. RankGraph-2 delivers up to +0.96% CTR and +2.75% CVR, and has powered 20+ retrieval launches across major surfaces.

</details>


### [87] [SHIFT: Semantic Harmonization via Index-side Feature Transformation for Multilingual Information Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18801)
*Youngjoon Jang,Seongtae Hong,Hyeonseok Moon,Heuiseok Lim*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 SHIFT 的索引阶段校准方法，通过消除多语言密集检索模型中的语言偏见（即对查询语言的过度偏好），实现了无需额外训练即可显著提升跨语言信息检索效果的目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多语言密集检索模型普遍存在严重的语言偏见问题（即偏向检索与查询语言相同的文档），这导致检索结果忽略了其他语言中语义更相关的文档，限制了跨语言检索的效果。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SHIFT 的训练无关（training-free）方法。该方法在索引阶段，利用平行翻译对来估计目标语言相对于源语言的相对语言向量，并通过从文档嵌入中减去该偏移量来校准语言偏见。

Result: 在四个多语言信息检索基准测试和多种密集检索模型上的实验结果表明，SHIFT 有效地减轻了语言偏见，提升了多语言信息检索的整体性能。

Conclusion: SHIFT 提供了一种高效且无需额外训练的方法来减轻多语言密集检索中的语言偏见，从而显著提升了跨语言检索的性能和公平性。

Abstract: With the rapid expansion of massive multilingual corpora, Multilingual Information Retrieval (MLIR) has emerged as a critical technology for global information access. MLIR enables users to retrieve semantically relevant documents from multilingual text collections using a single-language query. However, recent multilingual dense retrieval models often exhibit a strong preference for documents in the same language as the query. This leads to severe language bias, where top-ranked results are dominated by documents of specific languages, even when documents in other languages contain more semantically relevant information. To address this issue, we propose SHIFT, a training-free method applicable in the indexing stage. Specifically, SHIFT utilizes parallel translation pairs to estimate a relative language vector for each target language with respect to a source language. Subsequently, SHIFT corrects the language-specific offset by subtracting this relative language vector from document embeddings during indexing. Our comprehensive evaluation across four MLIR benchmarks and diverse dense retrieval models confirms that SHIFT can effectively mitigate language bias and enhance MLIR performance.

</details>


### [88] [Rescaling MLM-Head for Neural Sparse Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18811)
*Youngjoon Jang,Seongtae Hong,Jonah Turner,Heuiseok Lim*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在LSR模型中使用强力预训练基座时，MLM头部尺度过大导致训练崩溃的问题，并提出了一种零成本的初始化重缩放方案，有效提升了稀疏检索模型的稳定性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在将更强大的预训练模型（如ModernBERT、Ettin）应用于SPLADE等LSR模型时，由于MLM头部输出的尺度不匹配，导致稀疏激活被过度放大、匹配分数失真，进而引发性能下降甚至训练崩溃。

Method: 提出了一种简单的初始化阶段纠正方法，即在SPLADE训练前，通过一个常数因子对MLM头部的投影进行重新缩放（rescaling），以解决因MLM头L2范数过大导致的训练不稳定性。

Result: 该方法成功稳定了具有大范数MLM头的基座模型，在多个内域和跨域检索基准测试中表现出色，显著优于传统BERT-SPLADE基线，且该方法无需修改模型架构或训练目标，属于零成本调整。

Conclusion: 学习型稀疏检索模型（LSR）中，适配更强预训练编码器的瓶颈并非模型容量，而是用于构建稀疏表示的MLM头部（MLM-head）的尺度校准。通过简单的初始化阶段重新缩放，可以有效解决训练不稳定问题，使强基座模型在稀疏检索任务上达到更优性能。

Abstract: Learned sparse retrieval (LSR) models such as SPLADE have traditionally used BERT-style masked language models as backbone encoders. A natural expectation is that replacing BERT with stronger pretrained encoders should improve retrieval effectiveness. However, we find that under standard SPLADE training recipes, backbones with large MLM-head L2 norms can suffer performance degradation and even training collapse under standard SPLADE training recipes. We identify this failure as a scale mismatch in the MLM head: SPLADE directly uses MLM-head outputs to construct sparse lexical representations, and query-document relevance is computed by an unnormalized dot product over these representations. As a result, an inflated MLM-head scale can amplify sparse activations, distort matching scores, and destabilize contrastive training under common training settings. To address this issue, we introduce a simple initialization-time correction that rescales the MLM-head projection by a constant factor before SPLADE training. This zero-cost adjustment improves training stability without modifying the model architecture or training objective. Across both in-domain and out-of-domain retrieval benchmarks, this simple correction substantially improves large-norm backbones such as ModernBERT and Ettin, turning unstable training runs into competitive sparse retrievers. In several settings, the corrected models further match or surpass the classic BERT-SPLADE baseline. These findings suggest that the bottleneck in adapting pretrained encoders to LSR is not encoder capacity alone, but the calibration of the MLM-head scale used to construct sparse lexical representations.

</details>


### [89] [LensKit-Auto](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18814)
*Max Breit,Anass Amezian El Idrissi,Rishikesh Giriraj Kulkarni,Luca Quade*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文对自动化推荐框架LensKit-Auto进行了升级与功能增强，通过引入TPE优化算法、支持模型复用及可视化，并适配元学习框架，极大提升了系统易用性，旨在帮助非专业人员高效地为特定数据集寻找最优推荐算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于没有“放之四海而皆准”的推荐算法，针对不同数据集寻找最合适的算法及其超参数组合是一个持续的难题。为了降低推荐系统开发门槛并提升效率，作者旨在构建一个自动化推荐系统（AutoRecSys），即LensKit-Auto，以实现从数据输入到最优算法配置输出的全自动流程。

Method: 本文主要基于现有的LensKit-Auto框架进行开发，具体包括：1. 将框架迁移至最新版本的LensKit；2. 引入Tree Parzen Estimator（TPE）作为新的优化算法；3. 增加已训练模型重用功能与优化过程可视化功能；4. 适配元学习框架以构建元数据集，为未来集成元学习提供支撑。

Result: 通过一系列改进，LensKit-Auto实现了对底层框架的兼容更新，增强了优化效率（TPE引入），并提供了更好的用户交互体验（可视化与文档更新）。此外，元数据集的构建实验为后续将元学习引入该系统提供了可行性方案。

Conclusion: 本文通过对LensKit-Auto进行版本升级与功能增强，成功提升了其在自动化推荐系统选择与超参数调优方面的易用性与效率，使得即使是非专业用户也能便捷地为特定数据集找到最优的推荐算法配置。此外，对元学习框架的适配为后续实现智能推荐模型选择奠定了基础。

Abstract: Recommender systems have a wide area of application, e.g. in fields like video streaming, social media, or digital marketplaces. But, for a recommender-system, finding the right algorithm with the right hyperparameters is a reoccurring challenge. There is no one-fits-all solution, since the performance of one algorithm can vary immensely on different data sets. Due to the challenges of finding the right algorithm and the broad use of recommender-systems, it is of interest to create an Automated Recommender System (AutoRecSys) that takes on the task of finding the right algorithm-hyperparameter-combination for a given data set. In this work, we present the enhancement of LensKit-Auto, a framework introduced by Vente et al., that solves exactly this task of finding a fitting algorithm-hyperparameter-combination. LensKit-Auto's biggest strength lies in its ease of use, where it operates as a black-box, into which the user can feed their data set and receive the information of which algorithm and hyperparameters work best on this data set. In this work, we bring LensKit-Auto up to date, so that it works with the new version of its underlying framework, LensKit. We also implement further functionalities, such as the Tree Parzen Estimator as an additional optimization method, the ability to reuse the found algorithm, updated documentation, and the ability to visualize the optimization process. We also adapt an existing meta-learning framework to generate a suitable meta-dataset for LensKit-Auto, which could enable the integration of meta-learning into LensKit-Auto in the future. The presented changes bring LensKit-Auto up to date and enhance its usability, so that even non-experts in the field can find the right algorithm for their use case.

</details>


### [90] [SAERec: Constructing Fine-grained Interpretable Intents Priors via Sparse Autoencoders for Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18897)
*Jiangnan Xia,Xuansheng Wu,Yu Yang,Xin Wang,Ninghao Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SAERec，通过稀疏自编码器从大语言模型中提取并解耦细粒度意图，将其作为先验知识整合到推荐系统中，有效解决了意图表征不精准且不可解释的问题，实现了性能与可解释性的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于意图的推荐模型往往直接从序列数据中挖掘意图，存在对序列质量依赖高、意图数量需预设、语义表征粗糙且缺乏可解释性等问题，限制了推荐效果。作者旨在利用大语言模型的高密度文本信息，构建更具语义解释性的意图空间以辅助推荐。

Method: 提出 SAERec 框架：首先利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）对大语言模型提取的文本嵌入进行解耦，构建细粒度意图空间；其次为用户检索个人意图（兴趣）与公共意图（商品特征）作为先验；最后通过多分支注意力机制与自适应融合层，将意图信号集成至序列推荐模型中。

Result: 在多个公开数据集上的实验结果表明，SAERec 表现优于现有的前沿基准模型，在提升推荐准确度的同时，能够提供符合人类逻辑的决策解释。

Conclusion: SAERec 通过引入稀疏自编码器成功从大模型中解耦出细粒度且可解释的意图空间，不仅提升了推荐精度，还增强了系统的可解释性，证明了利用文本语义作为意图先验是优化推荐系统的有效路径。

Abstract: Intent-based recommender systems have gained significant attention for improving accuracy and interpretability by modeling the underlying motivations behind user behaviors. Most existing models derive intents directly from user sequences via clustering or prototype learning. However, they are sensitive to sequence quality, require presetting the number of intents, and lack explicit semantic grounding. These issues lead to an incomplete and coarse intent set and limit the effectiveness of recommendation. In this paper, we propose the Sparse Autoencoder for intent-based recommendation (SAERec), a novel recommender that automatically constructs a fine-grained and interpretable intent space from a textual corpus to guide recommendation. Rather than treating texts as side signals, SAERec leverages them as high information density evidence for intent construction. Specifically, we first extract a comprehensive set of fine-grained interpretable intents from the latent space of large language models (LLMs) by using a sparse autoencoder (SAE) to disentangle and interpret text embeddings, which isolates intent-related semantics from textual noise. Then, for each user, we retrieve relevant intents from this set as priors to guide recommendation. It contains personal intents matching a user's current interests and public intents capturing general item patterns shared across users (e.g., quality, price). Finally, to integrate retrieved intents into sequence modeling, we propose a multi-branch attention mechanism that captures temporal dependencies and injects both personal and public intent signals, followed by an adaptive fusion layer to construct the final user representation for recommendation. Extensive experiments on public datasets demonstrate the superiority of SAERec, consistently outperforming state-of-the-art baselines while providing human-understandable explanations.

</details>


### [91] [Querit-Reranker: Training Compact Multilingual Rerankers via Efficient Label-Free Distribution Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19037)
*Yunfei Zhong,Jun Yang,Wei Huang,Yinqiong Cai,Haosheng Qian,Yixing Fan,Ruqing Zhang,Lixin Su,Daiting Shi,Jiafeng Guo*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 Querit-Reranker，一种高效的多语言重排序器。通过合成查询挖掘实现少样本适配，并利用模型融合技术在不增加推理开销的情况下，实现了跨语言、跨领域的卓越排序性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可部署的多语言重排序器需要在跨语言、跨领域和跨任务场景下具有泛化能力，同时要求高效。目前的适配方法通常依赖昂贵的人工相关性标注，难以实现高效的任务迁移。

Method: 采用以数据为中心的训练流程，首先在大规模排序数据上学习通用相关性建模，随后通过合成查询挖掘（Synthetic-Query Mining）并利用教师模型评分作为连续软标签进行任务适配。最后，利用球面线性插值（SLERP）将多个任务适配模型合并为单一模型，避免了运行时集成开销。

Result: Querit-Reranker-A0.4B 在 BEIR 和 MIRACL 数据集上分别将 nDCG@10 提升至 59.28 和 67.70。在 MTEB 多语言重排序任务中，该模型显著优于更大的基于嵌入的基准模型，Querit-Reranker-4B 则在公开模型中达到了 SOTA 水准。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 Querit-Reranker 系列模型通过高效的数据驱动流程和模型融合技术，在保证低运行开销的同时，实现了跨语言和跨任务的卓越排序性能，为轻量级且高性能的重排序器部署提供了新范式。

Abstract: Deployable multilingual rerankers must generalize across languages, domains, and target ranking tasks while remaining efficient enough for second-stage reranking. However, adapting them to new target distributions typically requires extensive task-specific relevance annotations, which are costly to obtain. We present Querit-Reranker, a family of multilingual cross-encoder rerankers trained with a data-centric pipeline for label-efficient adaptation. We instantiate it as Querit-Reranker-A0.4B, initialized from an in-house MoE backbone with 0.4B activated parameters, and Querit-Reranker-4B, initialized from Qwen3-Embedding-4B. Our pipeline first learns general relevance modeling from large-scale ranking-oriented data, then adapts to target distributions through synthetic-query mining with teacher scores as continuous soft labels. To consolidate complementary task-adapted strengths, we further merge checkpoints via spherical linear interpolation, obtaining a single deployable model without runtime ensembling overhead. Using Qwen3-Embedding-0.6B as the shared first-stage retriever, Querit-Reranker-A0.4B improves average nDCG@10 from 54.11 to 59.28 on BEIR and from 59.87 to 67.70 on MIRACL. On MTEB Multilingual v2 Reranking, it also substantially outperforms larger embedding-based baselines, while Querit-Reranker-4B further achieves state-of-the-art performance among publicly available models. We release both models on Hugging Face.

</details>

### [92] [Gaussian Mixture Attention: Linear-Time Sequence Mixing via Probabilistic Latent Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18283)
*Yongchao Huang,Hassan Raza*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于高斯混合模型（GMA）的新型注意力机制，通过将计算复杂度从$N^2$降低到线性级别，在保持性能竞争力的同时，为长上下文处理提供了一种可解释且高效的架构选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer中的点积注意力机制在处理长序列时存在$N^2$的计算和存储瓶颈，限制了模型对长上下文的扩展能力。

Method: 提出高斯混合注意力（GMA），通过将查询（Query）和键（Key）映射到共享的潜在路由空间中，利用K个学习到的高斯混合成分进行交互。通过矩阵乘法的结合律，避免了构建$N \times N$的注意力权重矩阵，将存储复杂度降低至$\mathcal{O}(NK)$，并实现了端到端的梯度可导参数化。

Result: 实验表明，GMA实现了预期的$\mathcal{O}(NK)$线性内存扩展，在长上下文分类任务中表现出竞争力。尽管在WikiText-103基准测试中优于部分线性/随机特征注意力变体，但相较于当前高度优化的因果SDPA和Mamba模型仍有差距。分析显示GMA能够学习到有意义的组件分布。

Conclusion: GMA提供了一种具备可解释性的概率性、线性复杂度注意力替代方案，适用于长序列任务，但目前在计算效率和整体性能上仍无法完全取代针对特定架构（如SDPA或Mamba）的高度优化实现。

Abstract: The dense token-to-token interaction pattern of standard dot-product attention remains a central bottleneck in scaling Transformer architectures to long contexts. We introduce \textbf{Gaussian Mixture Attention (GMA)}, a probabilistic attention-style sequence mixer that replaces explicit pairwise query--key comparison with routing through $K$ learned Gaussian mixture components. Queries and keys are mapped to posterior \textit{responsibility} vectors over a shared latent routing space; their overlap defines an implicit responsibility-space affinity, while values are written into and read from a $K$-slot latent memory. By exploiting the associativity of matrix multiplication, GMA avoids materializing the induced $N\times N$ affinity matrix and instead uses two responsibility matrices whose dominant activation storage scales as $\mathcal{O}(NK)$ rather than $\mathcal{O}(N^2)$ for fixed $K$. We formulate bidirectional and causal variants of GMA, provide an end-to-end differentiable parameterization of the Gaussian mixture components, and analyze its responsibility-modulated gradient structure, constrained non-negative low-rank affinity interpretation, and local routing stability. Empirically, GMA exhibits the intended fixed-$K$ linear memory scaling and is competitive with attention-style baselines on long-context classification, while causal GMA improves over tested linear/random-feature attention variants on WikiText-103 but remains behind optimized causal SDPA and Mamba in the current implementation. Analysis of learned responsibilities further shows broad component usage and moderate alignment with surface-form token categories, supporting GMA as a probabilistic, interpretable, fixed-$K$ linear-time attention-style alternative rather than a universal replacement for optimized softmax attention or state-space models.

</details>


### [93] [Breaking the Solver Bottleneck: Training Task Generators at the Learnable Frontier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18284)
*Lorenz Wolf,Connor Watts,Roger Creus Castanyer,Geoffrey Bradway,Maxwill Lin,Augustine N. Mavor-Parker,Matthew Daborn-Sargent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对强化学习中任务生成评估成本过高的问题，PROPEL引入了一个轻量级的激活探针作为求解器代理，通过高效的预测机制实现了在代码和软件工程领域对任务生成分布的精准调控，显著提升了生成高质量训练任务的比例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习训练面临“前沿任务供给”瓶颈，即难以持续生成难度适中（既非过于简单也非无法解决）的有效任务。特别是在软件工程等复杂领域，由于求解评估耗时极长，传统的强化学习训练生成器方法在计算上不可行。

Method: 提出了一种名为PROPEL的求解器摊销框架（solver-amortized framework）。该方法通过在一个预先标注的任务与结果语料库上训练轻量级的“激活探针”，利用该探针模拟目标求解器的通过率，从而替代了直接进行昂贵的求解器滚动评估（rollouts）。在生成器优化过程中，只需进行单次前向传播即可预测任务的难度，实现对任务生成分布的控制。

Result: PROPEL显著提升了任务生成器产出“学习前沿”任务的比例。在编程任务中，对于Qwen2.5-3B和7B模型，目标通过率任务的比例分别提升至20.0%和12.6%；在软件工程领域，对于Qwen3.5-27B模型，该比例从9.8%提升至19.6%，且在未见过的代码仓库上仍具有良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: PROPEL通过引入基于激活探针（activation probe）的求解器代理模型，成功解决了强化学习训练中任务生成器难以高效评估的问题，为大规模、高质量任务自动生成提供了一种可扩展且高效的解决方案，在代码和软件工程领域证明了其提升训练数据效能的有效性。

Abstract: The limiting resource for training agents via reinforcement learning (RL) is increasingly frontier task supply: valid, solvable tasks just difficult enough to train the current model. As reasoning and agentic models improve, fixed task distributions saturate, while naive synthetic generation yields tasks that are trivial, impossible, or ill-posed. Training a task generator with RL to optimize validity and learnability can address this bottleneck, but direct optimization requires repeated solver rollouts per candidate. For software-engineering (SWE) tasks, a single rollout can take tens of minutes; solver-in-the-loop generator training is intractable. We introduce PROPEL, a solver-amortized framework for training task generators at the targeted solve rate. PROPEL trains a lightweight activation probe on a one-time labeled corpus of generated tasks and solver outcomes. The probe predicts target-solver pass rate from a frozen generator reference model and serves as a proxy for solve rate during generator optimization, reducing generator evaluation to a single forward pass. Across math, code, and software-engineering at multiple model scales, PROPEL shifts generation toward the targeted solve rate: for coding, tasks generated at the learnable frontier increase from $10.1\% \rightarrow 20.0\%$ for a Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct solver and from $5.3\% \rightarrow 12.6\%$ for a Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct solver. For SWE, PROPEL increases the share of generations at the targeted solve rate from $9.8\% \rightarrow 19.6\%$ for Qwen3.5-27B on repositories not seen during training of probe and generator.

</details>


### [94] [CODEBLOCK: Learning to Supervise Code at the Right Granularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18286)
*Zhijie Deng,Ling Li,Jinlong Pang,Kaiqin Hu,Qi Xuan,Zhaowei Zhu,Jiaheng Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CodeBlock 是一种代码 LLM 稀疏微调框架，它通过提取语法连贯且具有核心逻辑意义的“代码块”进行针对性监督，而非简单的 token 掩码，从而在大幅减少监督数据量的同时提升了代码生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的代码 LLM 有监督微调（SFT）对所有 token 施加均匀的损失，忽略了 token 间重要性的差异；而现有的 token 级掩码方法会破坏代码的语法和语义完整性。

Method: 提出一种结构感知的稀疏监督框架 CodeBlock，包括：1. 筛选高质量指令-响应对；2. 将代码划分为语法连贯的单元；3. 基于核心逻辑 token 的泛化交叉熵估计效用；4. 利用数据流的可达性和桥接信号对代码块进行重排序，仅对选定的重要代码块计算损失。

Result: 在六个代码生成基准测试中，CodeBlock 在仅使用 1.9% 监督 token 的情况下，其平均 pass@1 指标超过了全量 token SFT 和现有的选择性基线方法。

Conclusion: CodeBlock 通过利用代码的结构化特性进行稀疏监督，不仅提升了代码生成的准确率，还极大地降低了对监督信号密度的依赖，证明了在代码微调中考虑程序依赖性和结构完整性的重要性。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning of code LLMs typically applies uniform cross-entropy loss to all response tokens, implicitly assuming that every token provides equally useful learning signal. Recent token-level selection methods challenge this assumption in natural-language SFT by supervising only high-value tokens. However, directly transferring token-level masking to code can break syntactically and semantically coherent program units, because code depends on structural completeness and definition-use relations. We therefore propose CodeBlock, a structure-aware sparse supervision framework that selects structure-complete code evidence rather than isolated tokens. CodeBlock first selects high-quality instruction-response pairs, then partitions code responses into syntactically coherent coding items, estimates their utility by aggregating generalized cross-entropy over core logic tokens, and reranks them with data-flow reach and bridge signals to prioritize blocks that propagate or connect important program dependencies. During training, the full response remains available as context, while loss is applied only to selected code items and informative natural-language tokens. Experiments on six code-generation benchmarks show that CodeBlock achieves stronger average pass@1 than full-token SFT and competitive selection baselines, while using only 1.9% of supervised response tokens.

</details>


### [95] [Artemis: Anatomy-Resolved inTervention for Eliminating Multimodal NeuroImage confounderS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18287)
*Siyuan Dai,Yang Du,Kun Zhao,Zhusuyi Chen,Heng Huang,Paul Thompson,Chao Shi,Haoteng Tang,Liang Zhan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多模态神经影像分析中，年龄和性别等人口统计学因素常会作为混杂因素影响模型对临床结果的预测，导致模型学习到伪相关性而非因果特征。现有的因果图神经网络方法大多忽略了神经影像数据中特定脑区对混杂因素的不同敏感性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 Artemis 的区域级因果学习框架。该方法通过为每个大脑区域独立学习特定的人口统计学混杂因素表示，并在图神经网络的推理过程中引入区域级因果干预，从而剥离非必要的干扰信息。该框架作为一个轻量级的插件模块，兼容多种图神经网络骨干架构。

Result: 在 ADNI（疾病诊断）、OASIS（痴呆分期）和 HCP（性别分类）三个基准数据集上的实验表明，Artemis 在性能指标上均优于现有的代表性基线模型，并且表现出良好的统计显著性和神经科学解释性。

Conclusion: Artemis 框架成功地在图神经网络中实现了区域级的因果干预，证明了针对特定脑区进行混杂因素调整对于提高神经影像分析的准确性和稳健性至关重要，为处理具有人口统计学偏置的临床数据提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Multimodal neuroimaging, integrating functional connectivity from fMRI and structural connectivity from DTI, enables non-invasive analysis of brain networks using graph neural networks. However, demographic factors such as age and sex systematically confound the relationship between brain connectivity and clinical outcomes, causing GNNs to exploit spurious shortcuts rather than learning causally invariant representations. While recent causal GNN methods introduce causality at the graph-modeling level, their causal mechanisms remain domain-agnostic without accounting for the real-world confounders inherent in clinical neuroimaging data. Moreover, brain networks are constructed from atlas-based parcellations where each region exhibits distinct sensitivity to demographic factors, necessitating region-aware adjustment. We propose Artemis, a region-level causal framework that bridges this gap with causal intervention at each brain region independently by learning region-specific confounder representations with lightweight parameters. Our adjustment comprehensively utilized the multimodal functional and structural features for graph reasoning as a plug-in module compatible with arbitrary GNN backbones. Experiments on three benchmarks, ADNI for disease diagnosis, OASIS for dementia staging, and HCP for sex classification, demonstrate consistent improvements over representative GNN-based baselines. Multiple supporting experiments further demonstrate statistical significance and neuroscientific interpretability.

### [96] [A Link between Shock-wave Theory and Symmetry-reduced Stochastic Gradient Descent for Artificial Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18303)
*Taiki Miyagawa*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文将随机梯度下降的训练动力学映射为流体力学中的非线性波动问题，通过商化参数对称性，提出了一种分析神经网络训练行为的统一几何框架，并为深度学习训练监控提供了更精确的指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习理论往往忽略了参数对称性（如缩放、置换不变性）对训练动力学的影响。作者旨在建立一套严谨的数学框架，解释神经网络训练中观测到的非线性现象（如相变和冲击形成），并提出基于商空间的更准确的训练诊断指标。

Method: 采用微分几何、李群理论（用于商化参数对称性）以及流体力学（特别是粘性汉密尔顿-雅可比方程和伯格斯方程）对随机梯度下降动力学进行建模；利用局部熵粗粒化技术推导有效动力学。

Result: 研究证明了多层感知机、卷积神经网络、Transformer和平均场网络在训练过程中遵循汉密尔顿-雅可比方程或伯格斯方程；揭示了训练动力学中的冲击形成现象，并指出基于对称性修正的商空间观测值比原始参数范数更能有效监控和控制训练过程。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入流体力学和几何框架，成功将随机梯度下降（SGD）的学习动力学与波动方程联系起来。这为理解深度神经网络在训练过程中的相变、收敛行为以及模型复杂度评估提供了全新的理论视角和数学工具。

Abstract: We develop a mathematically explicit link between shock-wave theory and the symmetry-quotiented learning dynamics of stochastic gradient descent, drawing on differential geometry, Lie group theory, and fluid mechanics. Specifically, after quotienting parameter symmetries and applying local-entropy coarse-graining, the effective dynamics satisfy a viscous Hamilton--Jacobi equation on the quotient manifold. Moreover, under the assumption that the raw parameter dynamics can be summarized by a gradient field on the quotiented space, the gradient of the coarse-grained loss function obeys a Burgers-type equation, and shock formation can be established rigorously. We apply our theory to multilayer perceptrons, convolutional neural networks, Transformers, and mean-field networks, and show that they obey the Hamilton--Jacobi or Burgers-type equations. We conjecture that this framework also yields practical diagnostics for deep learning. In architectures such as Transformers, raw parameter norms are often distorted by symmetry redundancy and may therefore be misleading, whereas symmetry-corrected quotient observables provide a principled basis for monitoring, forecasting, and controlling training-phase transitions.

</details>


### [97] [Attribution-Guided and Coverage-Maximized Pruning for Structural MoE Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18304)
*Yifu Ding,Jiacheng Wang,Ge Yang,Yongcheng Jing,Jinyang Guo,Xianglong Liu,Dacheng Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对MoE模型部署成本高的问题，本文提出了细粒度的结构化剪枝框架，通过识别专家内部通道的冗余并优化剪枝比例分配，在保持精度的前提下实现了显著的压缩效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的MoE压缩方法主要针对“专家”这一粗粒度单位进行剪枝（如移除整个专家），导致无法捕捉专家内部的细粒度冗余，压缩效果受限且资源分配不合理。因此，作者旨在探索更精细的剪枝策略以降低MoE模型的部署成本。

Method: 研究发现MoE专家内部存在高度集中的信息和显著的冗余，据此提出了一种结构化剪枝框架。该方法将剪枝比例的分配重构为“通道评分覆盖最大化”问题，并采用基于属性的近似算法进行高效求解，从而实现比传统专家级剪枝更精细的压缩。

Result: 在DeepSeek和Qwen MoE模型上的实验表明，该方法在结合4-bit量化后，即使在50%或25%的结构化剪枝率下也能保持模型精度。特别是在Qwen3-30B-A3B模型上，实现了5.27倍的显存缩减，并在多项任务中优于现有的SOTA基线方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种针对混合专家模型（MoE）的结构化剪枝框架。实验证明，该方法能有效识别专家内部的细粒度冗余，在大幅降低显存占用（最高达5.27倍）的同时，能够保持模型在多种基准测试中的精度，显著优于现有的专家级剪枝方法。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models scale compute efficiently, yet remain expensive to deploy due to their substantial memory footprint and inference overhead. Prior compression methods mainly operate at the expert level, either removing entire experts or ranking experts by coarse-grained importance scores. However, such expert-wise decisions are often too coarse to capture fine-grained redundancy, leading to misallocated pruning budgets and limited compression. To address this problem, we observe that information within MoE experts is highly concentrated in a small subset of channels, leaving substantial redundancy even in experts deemed important. Based on this observation, we propose a structural pruning framework tailored for MoE models. Our method reformulates prune-ratio allocation as a channel-score coverage maximization problem and solves it efficiently using an attribution-based approximation. Experiments on DeepSeek and Qwen MoE models show that our method preserves model accuracy under 50% or 25% structured pruning when combined with 4-bit quantization. On Qwen3-30B-A3B, our approach reduces memory footprint by 5.27$\times$ and consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across diverse benchmarks.

</details>


### [98] [Fisher Width: A Geometric Measure of Complexity on Statistical Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18306)
*Vu Khac Ky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“Fisher 宽度”（Fisher Width），这是高斯宽度在统计流形上的黎曼几何对应物，通过利用费舍尔信息度量，更精确地刻画了统计模型参数空间的有效维度与复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高斯宽度是欧几里得空间中衡量几何复杂度的核心工具，但在统计模型中，参数空间本质上具有由费舍尔信息度量定义的黎曼几何特性，传统的欧几里得宽度无法捕捉统计区分度下的各向异性几何效应。

Method: 本文定义了 Fisher 宽度，通过引入费舍尔信息度量张量（Fisher Information Metric Tensor）的局部映射 $G(\theta)^{1/2}$，将原本的欧几里得度量替换为流形上的黎曼度量；并证明了其浓度不等式、度量扰动稳定性及谱比较界等理论特性，同时将其应用于 Fisher-Lipschitz 假设空间的泛化误差分析。

Result: 理论证明了 Fisher 宽度具有良好的数学结构，能有效捕捉欧几里得度量所忽略的统计曲率信息；实验表明，基于 Fisher 宽度的泛化界在 MNIST 数据集上能够更准确地反映不同模型类的学习难度与泛化性能。

Conclusion: Fisher width 成功将高斯宽度的概念从欧几里得空间推广到统计流形，为理解弯曲统计空间下的模型复杂度、泛化性能和学习理论奠定了几何基础。

Abstract: Gaussian width is a central geometric complexity measure in high-dimensional probability, compressed sensing, convex optimization, and learning theory. It quantifies the average extent of a set along random directions, thereby capturing the effective dimension of constraint sets, hypothesis classes, and descent cones. However, this notion is intrinsically Euclidean. Statistical models instead carry a natural Riemannian geometry induced by the Fisher information metric, where directions are scaled according to statistical distinguishability rather than ambient Euclidean length.
  We introduce Fisher width, a Fisher-geometric analogue of Gaussian width for statistical manifolds. At a parameter point $θ$, Fisher width replaces the Euclidean identity by the local metric tensor $G(θ)^{1/2}$, measuring the Gaussian width of the Fisher-rescaled set. This makes the resulting quantity sensitive to local statistical curvature and invariant under smooth reparameterizations.
  We develop the basic theory of Fisher width, showing that it retains key structural features of Gaussian width, including concentration, metric perturbation stability, and spectral comparison bounds with the Euclidean baseline, while also capturing anisotropic geometric effects invisible to Euclidean measures. As an application, we prove a generalization bound for Fisher-Lipschitz hypothesis classes and propose computable estimators, which we evaluate empirically on MNIST across three model classes.
  Fisher width is to statistical manifolds what Gaussian width is to Euclidean convex bodies. This work lays the foundation for studying complexity and learning on curved statistical manifolds.

</details>


### [99] [DRIFT: Refining Instruction Data via On-Policy Data Attribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18307)
*Zefan Wang,Lincheng Li,Tianyu Yu,Yuan Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型微调中数据筛选的局限，本研究提出了DRIFT方法，利用同策略影响函数进行数据归因与精细化筛选，有效突破了现有方法在提升模型能力上限方面的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据筛选方法多侧重于在预算限制下加速训练，但在提升模型性能上限方面表现不足。传统的影响函数（Influence Functions）在应用于有监督微调时存在离策略验证目标带来的“邻近性差距”以及对梯度范数的过度偏置问题。

Method: 提出了DRIFT（Data Refinement via On-Policy Influence Functions）框架。该方法使用模型自身的同策略滚动数据（on-policy rollouts）作为验证目标，以减小参数邻近性偏差；同时引入基于轨迹正确性的符号加权和梯度范数去偏技术，修正了传统影响函数在微调场景中的结构性限制。

Result: 在7B参数的指令遵循和逻辑推理模型上的实验表明，DRIFT能够一致性地提升模型的性能上限，其表现优于现有的各类数据整理（Data Curation）基准方法。

Conclusion: DRIFT通过采用同策略（on-policy）的影响函数，成功解决了现有数据筛选方法在提升大语言模型性能上限时的局限性，证明了基于细粒度数据归因的精细化筛选能显著优化微调效果。

Abstract: Optimizing the training data distribution for Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) dictates the capability of Large Language Models (LLMs). While existing data curation methods excel at accelerating training under constrained budgets, they are less suited to elevating the capability upper bound. The challenge here is no longer to identify a smaller subset that preserves performance, but to refine the data distribution toward instances most capable of improving the final model. To address this problem, we explore instance-level data attribution using Influence Functions (IF). We identify that standard IF formulations struggle in this setting due to two structural limitations: a proximity gap caused by off-policy validation targets, and a severe bias towards gradient norm. We propose DRIFT (Data Refinement via On-Policy Influence Functions for Supervised Fine-Tuning). Instead of relying on external reference data, DRIFT utilizes the model's on-policy rollouts as validation targets, which empirically minimizes the parameter proximity gap and better aligns with the local neighborhood assumption of IF. It further applies signed weighting based on trajectory correctness and debiases influence scores against the gradient hacking issue, allowing a small set of validation queries to act as reliable anchors for attributing the full dataset. Experiments on 7B-parameter instruction and reasoning models show that DRIFT consistently raises the performance ceiling on both, outperforming existing data curation baselines.

</details>


### [100] [TRIDENT: Breaking the Hybrid-Safety-Physics Coupling for Provably Safe Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18308)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在联网信息物理系统中，离散-连续混合动作空间、训练阶段的安全硬约束与物理动态特性三者相互作用，构成了“三向耦合引理”，导致现有的强化学习方法在处理这些复杂性时表现不佳。

Method: 提出TRIDENT框架，包含三个协同组件：1. 使用Richardson-Romberg梯度校正以降低Gumbel-Softmax偏差；2. 采用李雅普诺夫约束的序列置信域更新以确保每一步的安全性；3. 构建物理信息残差评论家（Physics-informed residual critic）进行价值分解。

Result: TRIDENT在理论上实现了受约束纳什均衡的收敛，并在多无人机边缘计算、自动交叉口管理等实验中，相较于基线方法大幅降低了违规率（最高达95.5%），同时提升了系统性能。

Conclusion: TRIDENT框架通过协同设计三个核心组件，有效解决了联网信息物理系统（CPS）在多智能体强化学习中的混合动作、安全约束和物理动态耦合问题，在提升奖励的同时显著降低了训练过程中的安全违规率。

Abstract: Safe coordination in networked cyber-physical systems forces learning algorithms to simultaneously handle hybrid discrete-continuous actions, hard training-time safety constraints, and physics-governed dynamics. We show that these three features form a directed cycle of biases that defeats any naive composition of off-the-shelf modules, and formalize this as a three-way coupling lemma. We then introduce TRIDENT, the first MARL framework whose three components are co-designed to cancel each leak: a Richardson-Romberg gradient correction reducing Gumbel-Softmax bias from O(tau) to O(tau^2), a Lyapunov-constrained sequential trust-region update enforcing per-iterate feasibility, and a physics-informed residual critic that decomposes value rather than reward. We prove an O~(1/sqrt(K)) convergence rate to a constrained Nash equilibrium and an O(sqrt(K)) cumulative-violation bound. On multi-UAV mobile-edge computing, autonomous intersection management, and a hybrid SMAC variant, TRIDENT cuts training-time violations by 95.5% over MADDPG and 76.3% over MACPO, while improving reward by 13.5% over the strongest unconstrained baseline.

### [101] [SAGE: Retain-Aware Post-Hoc Sanitization of Final Unlearning Vector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18309)
*Jingyuan Zhang,Yucheng Bai,Peixi Wen,Zhehao Huang,Zhengbao He,Hanling Tian,Xinwen Cheng,Haiyin Ran,Xiaolin Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型遗忘过程中的性能折中问题，本文提出了一种名为SAGE的事后修正方案，通过优化更新向量的激活几何结构，在保留模型原有性能的同时精准移除有害知识，无需重新训练即可实现性能恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为SAGE（光谱激活几何修正）的方法。该方法通过小规模保留数据集获取激活数据，提取其主导的激活几何结构，并在闭式解的优化框架下，修正大模型遗忘后的最终更新向量，使其在保留核心遗忘目标的同时，减小对模型保留能力的破坏。

Result: 实验表明，SAGE在多种遗忘方法、不同模型规模及基准测试中表现出色，能够持续有效地缓解遗忘与保留之间的性能权衡，证明了事后修正更新向量是机器遗忘领域一个极具价值且未被充分发掘的方向。

Conclusion: SAGE证明了对大语言模型遗忘更新向量进行事后（post-hoc）修正是一种有效且实用的策略。通过抑制与保留知识相关的激活几何成分，可以在不重新运行遗忘流程的前提下，显著缓解遗忘与保留性能之间的权衡矛盾。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) unlearning aims to remove undesirable knowledge or behaviors while preserving retained capabilities. Current unlearning methods all involve a trade-off between unlearning and retention. We have found that the retention activation bias can also be used to quantify the damage an unlearning method inflicts on retention, without considering the specific implementation of the unlearning process. This allows us to restore retention performance for any unlearning method using a post-hoc approach. Therefore, we propose a complementary post-hoc setting to sanitize the final update vector without rerunning the original unlearning pipeline. In this setting, we design SAGE, Spectral Activation-GEometry Sanitization, a source-agnostic correction for final unlearning updates. SAGE collects real module inputs from a small retain proxy, extracts their dominant activation geometry, and solves a source-anchored optimization objective in closed form, which suppresses update components aligned with high-energy retained directions while preserving the source method's forgetting carrier. Across multiple unlearning methods, model scales, and benchmarks, SAGE consistently relieves the retain-forget trade-off, identifying post-hoc sanitization of final vectors as a practical and underexplored axis for machine unlearning.

### [102] [Zero-Shot Active Feature Acquisition via LLM-Elicitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18933)
*Binyamin Perets,Natalie Mendelson,Shiran Vainberg,Yehuda Chowers,Shai Shen-Orr,Shie Mannor*

Main category: cs.LG

Method: 提出了一种“纪律性诱导”（disciplined elicitation）框架，将获取任务解耦：利用LLM提取MRF的充分统计量（一元偏差和成对协变），并引入最大熵闭包（maximum-entropy closure）来解决LLM仅返回判别性统计量导致的量规模糊问题，从而构建出零样本AFA决策策略。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架成功地弥合了LLM在知识获取与决策能力上的差距，通过将LLM的知识转化为马尔可夫随机场（MRF）的充分统计量，实现了一种无需标记数据的零样本主动特征获取（AFA）方法，在处理复杂临床数据时表现出显著的优越性。

Abstract: Active feature acquisition (AFA) sequentially selects which features to observe to reach a classification or ranking decision. Its central limitation is reliance on large amount of labeled data to fit probabilistic models guiding acquisition. Large language models (LLMs) supply unsupervised domain knowledge, but are poor sequential planners. Asking one to both know and decide conflates capabilities best kept separate. Here, we develop a framework for zero-shot AFA through disciplined elicitation: asking the LLM only for what it can be trusted to return, the unary deviations and pairwise co-variations that are the sufficient statistics of a Markov random field (MRF). We apply our framework to two settings: binary classification and top-$k$ identification. In practice, the LLM reliably returns only discriminative statistics, what distinguishes the classes rather than each class in isolation, which precludes classical AFA. We apply a maximum-entropy closure that resolves this gauge ambiguity. We evaluate on a cohort of Inflammatory Bowel Disease (IBD) patients, an active clinical setting where diagnostic ambiguity and patient heterogeneity obstruct stable treatment strategies. Our framework outperforms the LLM both on real labels and on its own extracted beliefs. Where it matters most, on the hardest patients, our top-$k$ acquisition policy markedly outperforms all existing methods.

### [103] [Ghost Attractor Networks: Basin-Structured Dynamical Decoders for Closed-Loop Sequential Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18315)
*Tianyu Wang,Ying Wang,Zhihao Liu,Xi Vincent Wang,Lihui Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Ghost Attractor Networks，这是一种新型动力学解码器，通过在潜在空间中构建具有“幽灵吸引子”特征的稳定盆地结构，极大地提升了机器人动作生成的效率与控制精度，在参数量远小于传统模型的情况下实现了领先的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大型 Transformer 或扩散模型的序列生成方法在大序列长度下内存消耗过大且计算耗时；而小型的全连接（feed-forward）解码器虽然高效，却缺乏稳定的潜在几何结构，难以支持机器人闭环控制中所需的相位条件动作生成与跨步 latent 延续。

Conclusion: Ghost Attractor Networks 通过在解码器中引入基于势能与漂移的动力学结构，成功在保持极低计算资源消耗的同时，实现了与超大规模扩散模型相当甚至更优的性能。该研究证明了利用分叉理论构建具有稳定盆地结构的潜在空间，是解决机器人闭环控制中多模态生成与长程一致性问题的有效路径。

Abstract: Sequential output generation with large-scale Transformer and diffusion decoders pays a memory cost that grows with sequence length, plus iterative per-step computation. Replacing them with small feed-forward decoders restores efficiency but produces unstructured latent representations that limit closed-loop control: phase-conditioned action generation and cross-step latent carry-over both require a latent geometry with stable basins. This article proposes Ghost Attractor Networks, a theoretically derived dynamical decoder whose latent evolves under a learned potential with drift and produces a basin-attractor structure by construction. Three desiderata (multi-modality, decoder-level single-pass switching, and constant memory) motivate the potential-drift form, and mode transitions arise as saddle-node bifurcations with ghost-attractor escape. A hierarchical phase-space decomposition separates first-order basin convergence from second-order proprioceptive refinement. Empirically, a Ghost trained end-to-end with a behavioral-cloning and contrastive objective exhibits the predicted gradient-flow contraction in its potential, with the gradient norm decaying by 67 percent across five integration steps on 1430 held-out samples. Ghost is evaluated as a robotic action decoder. A 2.3-million-parameter Ghost matches the offline accuracy of a 1.07-billion-parameter Diffusion Transformer at 462 times fewer parameters and 32 times lower latency, and beats five alternative 2M-parameter decoders (MLP, Neural ODE, CVAE, Transformer, 1-step Diffusion) on offline mean squared error by 5.9 to 29 percent. On the LIBERO-10 closed-loop benchmark, phase conditioning on Ghost's basin-structured latent yields a 13.5 percentage-point success-rate gain over a feed-forward MLP baseline, and persistent-latent ensembling reaches a 95.7 percent final success rate.

### [106] [ASTRA: A Scalable Next-Generation ATCO Training Simulator with Autonomous Simpilots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18319)

Built on open-source foundations such as DSPy and Unsloth, this approach enables scalable, standardized ATCO assessment while reducing instructor workload.

### [107] [SAE Interventions are Unreliable: Post-Intervention Recovery of Suppressed Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18322)
*Mingyue Cui,Linghui Shen,Xingyi Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出，稀疏自动编码器（SAE）虽然能提供可解释的特征，但通过“钳制”特定特征来防御模型有害行为是不可靠的；攻击者可以通过优化SAE重构残差来绕过防御，恢复有害行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于SAE的潜空间防御机制假设通过钳制（clamping）“不安全”特征即可可靠地阻止有害行为。作者旨在验证这一假设的鲁棒性，探讨当对特定特征进行干预时，模型是否仍能通过其他未被捕获的路径恢复有害行为，从而评估SAE在安全防御中的实际有效性。

Method: 作者将干预后的行为恢复建模为一个受约束的残差空间优化问题。具体方法包括：在保持目标SAE特征被抑制的状态下，通过优化残差扰动来尝试恢复预干预的行为表现；通过编码器正交更新（单层干预）和特征映射雅可比矩阵（跨层干预）确保优化过程并未简单撤销干预；并利用恢复路径归因分析定位行为恢复的来源。

Result: 研究表明，即便在强威胁模型下，通过优化残差扰动，行为恢复依然可能实现。在拒绝引导（refusal-steering）任务中，实现了高达95.8%的行为恢复率，且目标特征的漂移极小。分析发现，行为恢复主要依赖于SAE重构残差（即SAE未解释的部分），证明了仅对SAE特征进行干预在行为控制上存在漏洞。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了基于稀疏自动编码器（SAE）的特征干预存在局限性，仅控制特定特征无法保证完全抑制模型行为。研究强调了“行为完整性”与“特征级控制”之间的差距，并指出残留误差（reconstruction residual）是导致行为恢复的关键因素，未来的防御机制需要超越单一特征的干预。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) decompose residual-stream activations into interpretable features. Recent latent-space defenses increasingly rely on these decompositions, assuming that identified "unsafe" SAE features serve as actionable handles for monitoring and intervention. In this paradigm, clamping a specific harmful feature is expected to reliably prevent model misbehavior. However, we show that this success may hide a recoverable failure mode: the clamp may block one visible route to a behavior without eliminating the behavior itself. We formulate this vulnerability as post-intervention recovery, a constrained residual-space optimization problem. Starting from the post-intervention residual state, we optimize residual perturbations to recover the pre-intervention behavior while preserving the post-intervention values of the targeted SAE features. Even under a strong threat model where the intervention remains active throughout optimization and generation, recovery remains possible. To rule out that recovery simply undoes the intervention, we use encoder-orthogonal updates for single-layer interventions and the corresponding feature-map Jacobian in the cross-layer setting. Across TPP, unlearning, IOI, and refusal steering experiments, this stress test reveals recoverable behavior despite successful feature-level intervention. Especially in the safety-critical refusal-steering setting, we achieve a 95.8% recovery rate on valid samples while keeping defended-feature relative drift to 0.131, substantially below suffix-based baselines. A recovery-path attribution analysis further localizes this recovery to the SAE reconstruction residual, the component left unexplained by the SAE. These results expose a gap between feature-level control and behavioral completeness: SAE features can support causal intervention, but controlling them does not guarantee control over the underlying behavior.

</details>


### [108] [Why SWAVE May Not Be All You Need:A Concept-Evolution Retrospective on Complex-Valued Recurrent Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18324)
*Ramprasath Ganesaraja,Swathika N,Sahil Dilip Panse*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SWave是一款基于复杂值循环架构的语言模型，通过引入Cayley参数化的酉转换和波传播扫描技术，实现了长上下文下的稳定状态传播，并提出了一套解决复杂值神经网络训练中数值坍缩问题的工程方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索利用复杂数域表示语言作为波的潜力，以实现比传统实值模型更丰富的信息编码，并通过数学约束（酉转换）保证循环神经网络在处理任意长上下文时的状态完整性，防止状态衰减或爆炸。

Method: 研究采用复杂值循环语言模型架构，核心组件包括Cayley参数化的酉转换、ComplexNorm、波传播扫描（Wave Propagation Scan）以及解耦的实部与虚部嵌入表。训练过程历经三个阶段，通过引入独立嵌入表解决了“余弦主导坍缩”问题，并优化了前向与后向扫描算法以确保数值稳定性。

Result: SWave模型（约1.69亿参数）在FineWeb-Edu数据集上实现了稳定的训练，最佳困惑度（PPL）达到22.0。研究明确了“余弦主导坍缩”的失效模式，提出了支持数值稳定的对数空间反向传播扫描算法，并总结了六项复杂值循环训练的工程原则。

Conclusion: SWave的研究表明，通过复杂的数学结构（如Cayley参数化的酉转换）可以有效实现循环语言模型中长程信息的稳定传播，从而克服梯度消失或爆炸问题。该研究通过实证纠正了此前对某些复杂架构组件（如多尺度保持概念）的认知，并为复杂值循环神经网络的稳定训练提供了关键的工程原则与数值稳定性方案。

Abstract: SWave is a complex-valued recurrent language model (169.26M parameters, D=384, L=16, T=2048) trained on FineWeb-Edu using 2xH100 NVL. It was designed around three founding premises: that representing language as complex waves rather than real-valued numbers enables richer information encoding; that a Cayley-parameterised unitary transition provides a mathematical guarantee against state decay or explosion; and that a hidden state which rotates rather than shrinks preserves signal integrity over arbitrarily long contexts. The core of SWave evolved substantially across three development phases. The Resonance Head was found to structurally admit imaginary-channel collapse as a global loss minimum (a failure mode we term cos-domination collapse) and was superseded by an untied head with independent real and imaginary embedding tables from the Phase-Associative Memory (PAM) architecture. This resolved the degenerate minimum and enabled stable 200,000-step training (best-step PPL 22.0 at step 89,861). ComplexNorm and the Wave Propagation Scan proved load-bearing throughout all three phases and were retained to the final architecture. ProtectGatedScan was reframed as a structural prior rather than a learned behaviour. The four multi-scale retention concepts showed no measurable improvement under controlled evaluation and were found non-load-bearing. The ComplexGatedUnit was superseded by a real-valued squared-ReLU channel mixer with fewer parameters. The auxiliary training objectives showed no benefit once structural constraints were resolved. The investigation yields a formal characterisation of cos-domination collapse, a parallel scan with a log-space backward pass for numerical stability, six transferable engineering principles for complex-valued recurrent training, and a plan-to-code traceability methodology for catching structural divergences that conventional test suites miss.

</details>


### [109] [Neural Network Implementation of the Renormalization Group for Fault Diagnosis with Class Imbalance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18326)
*Evgeny Nikulchev,Dmitry Ilin*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于重整化群理论的神经网络RGNet，通过分层粗粒化特征空间有效解决了类别不平衡与噪声干扰问题，在故障预测任务中实现了高性能与高可解释性的统一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际机器学习任务中，模型往往面临类别不平衡及多维噪声带来的严峻挑战，现有的方法在捕捉多尺度特征和提供模型可解释性方面仍存在不足。

Method: 提出了一种名为RGNet的神经网络架构，核心在于利用重整化群（RG）概念对特征空间进行分层粗粒化处理。该方法通过顺序压缩输入维度，并将各尺度的特征拼接以捕捉局部细节与全局模式，同时引入RG-flows以生成可解释的低维表示。

Conclusion: RGNet通过引入重整化群思想，成功为处理不平衡数据下的故障预测任务提供了一种通用、可解释且具有竞争力的新架构。其在特征空间分层粗粒化方面的优势，验证了该方法在复杂工业场景中的有效性。

Abstract: The application of machine learning models in practical tasks faces challenges such as class imbalance and multidimensional noise. This paper proposes RGNet, a neural network architecture based on the concept of the renormalization group (RG), for hierarchical coarse-graining of the feature space. The model sequentially compresses the input dimensionality and concatenates all scales before classification, allowing it to capture both local details and global patterns. The notion of RG-flows is introduced - interpretable low-dimensional representations whose visualization via t-SNE reveals a discrete curvilinear structure confirming the effectiveness of coarse-graining. Experimental results are presented on the imbalanced AI4I dataset. The obtained results demonstrate that RGNet is a universal, interpretable, and competitive solution for fault prediction in applications with imbalanced classes.

### [110] [Self-CTRL: Self-Consistency Training with Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18327)
*Itamar Pres,Laura Ruis,Melat Ghebreselassie,Belinda Z. Li,Jacob Andreas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种通过强化学习使语言模型的自我解释与实际行为保持一致的训练方法（Self-CTRL），实验证明该方法在增强模型透明度、审计准确性及安全性方面具有显著效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了让语言模型（LM）能够准确描述自身行为，从而使模型更易于被用户审计、理解和信任。当前模型在自我解释与实际行为之间往往存在不一致，导致模型不可控或不透明。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Self-Consistency Training with Reinforcement Learning (Self-CTRL)”的方法。该方法通过强化学习优化模型，使其自我解释（self-explanations）与相关输入下的行为保持一致。具体而言，该方法通过两个方向的更新来实现：一是优化解释以预测行为，二是优化行为以匹配解释。

Result: 在形式化概率推理任务中，该方法将模型对潜在偏差的自我报告与行为测量之间的相关性从 R²=0.24 提升至 R²=0.64；在宪法AI任务中，模型对拒绝/合规行为的描述准确率从 36% 提升至 92%，且在 HarmBench 测试中，有害行为的失败率从 15.0% 显著降低至 0.5%。

Conclusion: 通过将语言模型的自我解释与实际行为对齐，Self-CTRL提供了一种通用的训练范式，能够显著提升AI模型的可信度、透明度和可控性，是实现更安全AI的重要路径。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) that faithfully describe their own behavior can more easily be audited, understood, and trusted by users. This paper describes Self-Consistency Training with Reinforcement Learning (Self-CTRL), a method that optimizes for consistency between a LM's self-explanations and behavior on related inputs by updating explanations to better predict behavior or updating behavior to better match explanations. We apply our method in two domains. First, we study a formal probabilistic reasoning task in which LMs must learn to imitate a family of biased samplers and evaluated on their ability to report the associated biases. We find that consistency training improves the correlation between self-reported and behaviorally-measured latent biases from $R^2=0.24$ to $R^2=0.64$ on a set of held-out distributions, matching the generalization of direct ground-truth supervision. Second, we study a constitutional AI domain in which LMs must describe when they will refuse or comply with user requests. Here, Self-CTRL produces rules that faithfully describe the model's behavior on held-out requests, improving the refusal predictions of a third-party auditor model from $36\%$ to $92\%$. In the other direction, behavior updates improve alignment, reducing HarmBench failure rate from $15.0\%$ to $0.5\%$ without substantially increasing refusal on harmless prompts. By aligning explanations and behavior, our work provides a general recipe for training AI models to be safer, more transparent, and more controllable.

</details>


### [111] [ThousandWorlds: A benchmark for climate emulation of potentially habitable exoplanets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18338)
*Edward T. Stevenson,Mei Ting Mak,Eric Wolf,Denis E. Sergeev,Tobi Hammond,N. J. Mayne,Miles Cranmer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发布了ThousandWorlds，这是一个旨在加速系外行星气候仿真的标准化数据集与基准，填补了机器学习在该领域应用的数据空白，并指出高斯过程在处理此类复杂物理模拟回归任务中表现优于传统深度学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释系外行星大气中的生物特征需要全球气候模型（GCM），但GCM计算成本极高且耗时。虽然机器学习仿真器可以解决该瓶颈，但目前缺乏高质量、标准化的多模型系外气候数据集，限制了相关研究的发展。

Method: 研究人员构建了ThousandWorlds数据集，包含来自5个不同全球气候模型（GCM）的约1800次模拟，涵盖了温度、湿度、风场、云量和辐射等三维大气参数。研究设计了三个递进的回归任务子集，并提出了两种评估协议，对比了包括简单统计方法、深度学习和高斯过程在内的七种基准模型。

Result: 实验表明，基于高斯过程（GP）的方法在ThousandWorlds数据集上的表现优于现有的深度学习模型。研究还发现，该数据集所代表的低数据量、多模拟器参数到场（parameter-to-field）回归场景，对当前的深度学习架构提出了重大挑战。

Conclusion: ThousandWorlds数据集揭示了目前现成的深度学习模型在模拟器间回归任务中的局限性，并强调了高斯过程（GP）在处理此类小样本、多模拟器科学数据中的优势，为未来系外行星气候仿真提供了一个标准化的评估框架。

Abstract: The search for life beyond Earth will depend on detecting faint signatures in the atmospheres of potentially habitable exoplanets. Interpreting those signatures requires understanding the host planet's climate: the same molecule may signal life on one planet and abiotic chemistry on another. Global climate models (GCMs) provide this understanding, but individual runs can require up to millions of core-hours and substantial domain expert time. Machine-learning emulators could remove this bottleneck, but progress has been limited by the absence of a curated, multi-model exoclimate dataset. We introduce ThousandWorlds, an ML-ready benchmark for exoclimate emulation and for the broader regime of low-data, multi-simulator, parameter-to-field regression. The dataset contains approximately 1800 simulations from five GCMs, mapping eight planet parameters to 3D atmospheric fields including temperature, humidity, winds, clouds, and radiation. Three nested subsets define progressively harder challenges: single-simulator regression, multi-simulator regression with complete observations, and multi-simulator regression with structured missingness. We propose two evaluation protocols: one for ranking methods, and one that measures performance relative to the disagreement between GCMs themselves. We evaluate seven baselines spanning simple methods, deep learning, and Gaussian processes. GP-based methods perform best, suggesting that ThousandWorlds exposes a regime where off-the-shelf deep learning does not yet succeed. Data: https://doi.org/10.57967/hf/8695. Code: https://github.com/edstevenson/ThousandWorlds.
