### [153] [Contextualizing Biological Language Models across Modalities via Logit-Space Contrastive Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18703)
*Yanjun Shao,Yundi Chen,Yashvi Patel,Aurelien Pelissier,María Rodríguez Martínez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LOGICA 是一种通过在输出 Logit 空间进行对比学习来实现上下文条件化预测的新框架，它在保留生物语言模型原生概率接口的同时，显著提升了变体评分和药物抗性预测的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生物语言模型大多在未标记的大规模语料上预训练，缺乏对特定生物环境（如相互作用伙伴、药物干预等）的条件化能力。而现有的上下文匹配方法往往通过潜在空间池化或任务头扭曲了模型原生的概率接口，限制了其在变体评分和机制解释上的应用。

Method: 提出了一种名为 LOGICA（Logit-space Contrastive Alignment）的框架。该方法使用门控跨模态适配器（gated cross-modal adapters），直接在预训练模型的输出 Logit 空间进行对比学习，将上下文信息转化为标记（token）的对数似然分数，无需共享的分词器或解码器。

Result: LOGICA 在蛋白质-配体结合、TCR-肽活性以及药物抗性预测等任务上均超越了现有的对比学习和条件掩码语言模型基准。特别是在单突变药物抗性预测中，将 AUC 从基准的约 0.55 提升至约 0.65。

Conclusion: LOGICA 证明了在输出 Logit 空间而非潜在空间进行对比学习，是实现上下文条件化生物序列预测的有效途径。该框架在保持预训练模型原生概率接口的同时，有效提升了复杂生物任务的预测性能，且具有良好的可解释性。

Abstract: Pretrained biological language models expose per-token probability distributions through masked-token prediction, providing the likelihood interface central to sequence design, variant scoring, and mechanistic interpretation. Yet these distributions are learned from broad unlabeled corpora and are not naturally conditioned on task-specific biological contexts such as interaction partners, cellular environments, or therapeutic interventions. Existing contextual matching methods often distort this interface through pooled embeddings, contrastive latent spaces, or task-specific prediction heads. We introduce LOGICA (Logit-space Contrastive Alignment), a framework for context-conditioned prediction that performs contrastive learning directly in output-logit space. Using gated cross-modal adapters compatible with each model's native token head, LOGICA preserves the pretrained likelihood interface and converts contextualized token log-likelihoods into matching scores. Alignment is defined through context-sensitive token probabilities rather than proximity in a shared embedding space, enabling learning from sparse paired data across models with distinct vocabularies, without a shared tokenizer or decoder. LOGICA is particularly effective for mutation-local variant ranking, where comparisons reduce to context-conditioned likelihoods of mutant tokens at perturbed sites. Across protein--ligand binding, TCR--peptide activity, and drug-conditioned resistance prediction, LOGICA improves over prior state-of-the-art methods, including matched latent-contrastive and conditional MLM baselines, while retaining a token-level interface for interpretation and generation. On held-out-gene single-mutation drug-resistance prediction, LOGICA improves AUC from near-random latent-space baselines of $\sim$0.55 to $\sim$0.65.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 理论上，作者提供了在凸、强凸及非凸设置下的收敛性保证，证明了 Cond-DP 可以显著提升私有线性回归的收敛速度。实证结果表明，在多种数据集和模型架构下，Cond-DP 在标签差分隐私设置中均优于现有的先进基准方法，表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: Cond-DP 成功利用公共特征的结构信息改善了差分隐私回归的优化过程，证明了在隐私约束下，通过预处理优化景观可以显著提升收敛速度和模型性能，为标签差分隐私场景下的回归任务提供了一种高效且稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: We study differentially private (DP) regression in settings where each data sample includes public, non-sensitive features -- common in applications such as recommendation and advertising systems. While such label-DP or semi-sensitive-feature settings have been primarily explored in the context of classification, effective approaches for regression remain underexplored. We introduce Cond-DP, a conditioned variant of DPSGD that leverages the structure of public feature matrices to improve optimization under privacy constraints. Motivated by the observation that these public features often exhibit rapidly decaying spectra, Cond-DP incorporates a data-driven conditioning matrix to reshape the optimization landscape and accelerate convergence. We provide convergence guarantees for convex, strongly convex, and non-convex settings, and recover standard DPSGD as a special case when the conditioning matrix is the identity. We show how to construct an effective conditioning matrix for Cond-DP directly from public features, enabling provably faster convergence than DPSGD in private linear regression without incurring additional privacy cost. Empirically, Cond-DP with this conditioning matrix consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across a wide range of datasets and model architectures under label DP, demonstrating strong and robust performance in practice.

*Jiale Linghu,Hao Dong,Yangshuai Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Photonic quantum machine learning offers a route to trainable physical representations built from phase, interference and measurement. However, its role in scientific machine learning remains largely unexplored. Physics-informed neural fields provide a natural setting, because differential equations require trial spaces that preserve phase, frequency and derivative structure. Here we introduce a photonic quantum neural field in which coordinates become trainable optical phases, are mixed by multi-photon Fock-space interference and are decoded from photon-number measurements. The photonic circuit is optimized as the neural-field representation itself, not as a fixed feature map or hardware accelerator. Photonic measurement is therefore a trainable representation on which the physics-informed residual is minimized. Across seven elliptic, wave, nonlinear dispersive and inverse PDE benchmarks, we observe a phase-complexity transition: classical coordinate and Fourier-feature networks suffice in smooth regimes, whereas the photonic field is most accurate when residual derivatives amplify phase mismatch. In the hardest regimes it gives the lowest errors, with margins reaching an order of magnitude and about one quarter of the trainable parameters of classical baselines. Frozen and shuffled controls, together with noise stress tests, attribute this gain to learned interference and stable Fock-probability readout under compound perturbations. These results identify photonic quantum measurement as a representation-learning principle for scientific machine learning.

Abstract: Identifying Pareto optimal solutions is critical to support multi-objective decision-making. We benchmark TTPFTS against state-of-the-art fixed-budget Pareto Set Identification algorithms on synthetic environments. Next, we demonstrate its practical utility in a challenging multi-objective molecular discovery setting by efficiently exploring an ultra-large synthesis-on-demand molecular library. Furthermore, we introduce a novel uncertainty quantification metric that estimates our algorithm's confidence in the predicted Pareto set. Motivation: 传统的基于帧的视频处理在实时应用中功耗较高且对环境适应性有限，本研究旨在通过结合脉冲神经网络（SNN）的高能效特性与事件相机（DVS）的时空处理优势，探索一种更高效、低功耗的人体跌倒检测解决方案。

Result: 实验结果表明，该混合模型在多个数据集上均表现优异，在跌倒检测任务中实现了高准确率，并显著降低了计算能耗，优于传统的机器学习模型。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了混合脉冲神经网络（SNN）与卷积神经网络（CNN）架构在处理基于事件的视觉数据方面的有效性，表明该方法在保持高准确率的同时，能够显著提升边缘设备上复杂任务（如跌倒检测）的能效。

Abstract: This work presents the development of hybrid models that integrate spiking neural networks (SNNs) with components of convolutional neural networks (CNNs) to learn from simulated event-based camera data (Dynamic Vision Sensor, DVS) generated from conventional smartphone videos. Aimed primarily at human fall detection, the approach leverages the energy efficiency and spatio-temporal processing capabilities of SNNs by converting video frames into event-based data. The proposed models are evaluated through simulations on multiple datasets, comparing their performance to that of traditional machine learning models. Results demonstrate significant gains in efficiency without sacrificing accuracy, underscoring the potential of combining SNNs and DVS technology for complex tasks in real-world environments.

### [158] [Learning from Own Solutions: Self-Conditioned Credit Assignment for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18810)
*Yingyu Shan,Yuhang Guo,Zihao Cheng,Zeming Liu,Xiangrong Zhu,Xinyi Wang,Jiashu Yao,Wei Lin,Hongru Wang,Heyan Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SC-GRPO 是一种改进的推理任务强化学习算法，通过利用自条件轨迹产生的 KL 散度作为梯度权重，实现了对关键推理步骤的自动信用分配，显著提升了模型性能且无需额外依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法（如 GRPO）在推理任务中对所有 token 赋予统一权重，导致计算资源浪费，且现有信用分配方法过度依赖外部教师（蒸馏）或过程奖励模型，限制了纯 RLVR 设置下的适用性。

Method: 提出 SC-GRPO（Self-Conditioned GRPO）算法。该方法观察到对模型进行验证轨迹的条件化会产生原分布与条件分布间的 KL 散度，利用此 KL 散度作为 GRPO 梯度计算中的乘法权重，实现对关键推理步骤的自动加权，从而避免了对外部教师模型或过程奖励模型的依赖。

Result: 在涵盖数学、代码及代理任务的五个基准测试中，SC-GRPO 表现显著优于 GRPO（提升 8.1%）和 DAPO（提升 5.9%），且在分布外（OOD）任务中表现更佳，性能甚至超越了在线策略蒸馏（OPD）。

Conclusion: SC-GRPO 证明了通过自条件（Self-Conditioned）产生的 KL 散度可以有效衡量各 token 的贡献度，无需外部教师或额外监督，为纯强化学习环境下的 LLM 推理任务提供了一种高效且高性能的信用分配机制。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has driven substantial progress in training LLMs for reasoning tasks, but representative methods such as GRPO assign uniform credit across all tokens, wasting gradient on routine tokens while under-crediting pivotal reasoning steps. Existing token-level credit assignment methods require resources beyond the model's own rollouts. GRPO variants rely on process reward models or ground-truth answers. Knowledge distillation assigns credit through per-token divergence but requires external teachers (On-Policy Distillation) or privileged information (On-Policy Self Distillation). However, these dependencies limit applicability in the pure RLVR setting. We observe that conditioning the model on its own verified trajectories induces a measurable per-token KL divergence between the original and conditioned distributions, and prove that distilling from a self-teacher constructed by verified trajectories leads to infeasible weighted-average solutions when multiple verified trajectories exist. We propose SC-GRPO (Self-Conditioned GRPO), which uses KL divergence mentioned before as a multiplicative weight on GRPO gradients. Across five benchmarks spanning math, code, and agentic tasks, SC-GRPO consistently outperforms 8.1% over GRPO and 5.9% over DAPO with stronger OOD performance. Moreover, SC-GRPO achieves higher performance than OPD.

### [159] [GateMem: Benchmarking Memory Governance in Multi-Principal Shared-Memory Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18829)
*Zhe Ren,Yibo Yang,Yimeng Chen,Zijun Zhao,Benshuo Fu,Zhihao Shu,Bingjie Zhang,Yangyang Xu,Dandan Guo,Shuicheng Yan*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验表明，在多样的基线模型和主干模型中，没有方法能同时实现强大的实用性、稳健的访问控制和可靠的遗忘。长上下文提示在治理得分上表现最佳但成本极高，而基于检索和外部记忆的方法虽然降低了成本，但往往会导致未经授权或已删除信息的泄露。

Conclusion: 当前的记忆体代理（Memory Agents）在处理多主体共享记忆时，仍远未达到可靠部署的标准，现有方法难以在实用性、访问控制和遗忘机制之间取得平衡。

Abstract: Memory benchmarks for LLM agents largely assume single-user settings, leaving shared assistants for hospitals, workplaces, campuses, and households understudied. In these deployments, multiple principals write to a common memory pool and query it under different roles, scopes, and relationships, so memory quality requires governance as well as recall. We introduce GateMem, a benchmark for multi-principal shared-memory agents. GateMem jointly evaluates utility for legitimate long-horizon requests with state updates, access control across contextual authorization boundaries, and agent-facing active forgetting after explicit deletion requests. It spans medical, office, education, and household domains, with long-form multi-party episodes, incremental memory injection, hidden checkpoints, structured judging, and leak-target annotations. Across diverse baselines and backbone models, no method simultaneously achieves strong utility, robust access control, and reliable forgetting. Long-context prompting often yields the best governance score at high token cost, while retrieval-based and external-memory methods reduce cost yet still leak unauthorized or deleted information. These results show current memory agents remain far from reliable shared institutional deployment.

### [160] [RouteJudge: An Open Platform for Reproducible and Preference-Aware LLM Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18774)
*Guannan Lai,Haoran Hu,Han-Jia Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 LLM 路由评估框架 RouteJudge 和配套工具箱 ORBIT，通过引入在线成对偏好评估和标准化开发流程，解决了 LLM 路由策略难以量化评估及开发流程不统一的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 评估多关注模型层面的回答质量，缺乏针对“路由策略（Router）”决策质量的有效评估机制。同时，路由算法的研究缺乏标准化的开发、评估与集成工具，难以进行跨研究的公平对比。

Method: 1. RouteJudge：通过在线匿名成对比较收集用户对路由决策的偏好数据，支持成本感知和任务感知的多维度分析。2. ORBIT：一个模块化工具箱，提供统一的基准测试加载、路由实现、预算感知评估及方法对比接口，标准化了从开发到在线评估的全流程。

Abstract: We present RouteJudge, an online pairwise preference evaluation framework for LLM routing systems, with a public platform available at https://routejudge.cn. Different from model-level response evaluation, RouteJudge focuses on router-level decision quality. For each user query, multiple routing strategies independently recommend candidate models under the same model pool and budget constraints. The selected model responses are then presented to users through anonymous pairwise comparisons, and the resulting user preferences are attributed back to the routing strategies behind the compared responses. Each evaluation record stores the query, routing decisions, model responses, preference labels, cost, latency, and task metadata, enabling preference-aware, cost-aware, and task-conditioned analysis of LLM routers. To support the continuous expansion of routing methods in RouteJudge, we further release ORBIT (Optimal Routing and Budgeted Inference Toolbox), a modular and extensible toolbox that standardizes the end-to-end workflow of LLM routing. ORBIT provides unified interfaces for benchmark loading, query representation, router implementation, budget-aware evaluation, and method comparison, allowing researchers to develop and evaluate routing algorithms under consistent protocols. It also serves as the submission and integration layer for RouteJudge: researchers can implement routing methods within ORBIT, validate them on existing routing benchmarks, and submit compatible routers for online preference-based evaluation. The code of ORBIT is available at https://github.com/AIGNLAI/LAMDA-ORBIT.

### [161] [REVES: REvision and VErification--Augmented Training for Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18910)
*Yuanxin Liu,Ruida Zhou,Xinyan Zhao,Amr Sharaf,Hongzhou Lin,Arijit Biswas,Mohammad Ghavamzadeh,Zhaoran Wang,Mingyi Hong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为REVES的两阶段迭代框架，通过将推理过程中的“近失”中间步骤转化为纠错训练数据，优化了大语言模型的测试时推理能力，在编程、数学和逻辑推理任务中显著优于传统的多轮强化学习方法，且在小模型上实现了高效的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型推理优化主要关注单步目标，这与测试时顺序修订的推理范式存在不匹配；而现有的多轮强化学习方法直接对长轨迹进行优化，忽略了对推理过程中产生的“高质量错误（即近失答案）”的学习价值，导致训练效率低下且难以有效提升模型的自我纠正能力。

Method: 本文提出了一种两阶段迭代框架（REVES）：1. 数据/提示增强阶段：将成功纠正路径中的中间步骤（近失答案）拆解为“修订”与“验证”提示；2. 策略优化阶段：通过离线策略学习，集中训练模型识别错误并实现答案转换。这种方法避免了传统强化学习对长视野轨迹的直接优化，降低了计算开销。

Result: 在LiveCodeBench基准测试中，该方法比RL基准提升了6.5个百分点，比标准多轮训练提升了4.0个百分点；在圆堆积任务中，以较小的4B模型规模达到了与大规模演化搜索系统相当的SOTA性能；在数学推理及约束满足问题（如n-queens、数独）上也表现出极强的泛化纠错能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的REVES框架通过两阶段迭代策略，成功克服了传统多轮强化学习在处理推理任务时的效率瓶颈。该方法证明了利用“近失（near-miss）”中间步骤进行纠错训练，能显著提升大语言模型在编程、数学及逻辑约束任务中的推理与自我纠正能力，且在小参数模型下展现了卓越的性能。

Abstract: Test-time scaling via sequential revision has emerged as a powerful paradigm for enhancing Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning. However, standard post-training methods primarily optimize single-shot objectives, creating a fundamental misalignment with multi-step inference dynamics. While recent work treats this as multi-turn reinforcement learning (RL), conventional approaches optimize over the multi-step trajectories directly, failing to further exploit the high-quality mistakes in intermediate steps that model can learn from correcting them. We propose a two-stage iterative framework that alternates between online data/prompt augmentation and policy optimization. By converting the intermediate steps (``near-miss'' answers) in the successful recovery trajectories into decoupled revision and verification prompts, our approach concentrates training on both effective answer transformation and error identification. This approach enables efficient off-policy data generation and reduces the computational overhead of long-horizon sampling compared to standard multi-turn RL. On LiveCodeBench, using publicly available test cases as feedback, we observe gains of +6.5 points over the RL baseline and +4.0 points over standard multi-turn training. Beyond coding, our approach matches the previously reported SOTA result on circle packing while using the smallest base model (4B) and far fewer rollouts than the much larger evolutionary search systems. Math results under ground-truth verification further confirm improved correction ability. It also generalizes to out-of-distribution constraint-satisfaction puzzles such as n\_queens and mini\_sudoku, where correctness is defined entirely by problem constraints. Code is available at https://github.com/yxliu02/REVES.git.

</details>


### [162] [Online Distributional Prediction via Latent Cluster Geometry Under Drift and Corruption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18778)
*Navyansh Mahla,Prateek Chanda,Ganesh Ramakrishnan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对非平稳流数据，本文提出了一种基于潜在聚类几何的非参数化在线分布预测方法，利用Gibbs后验平均和重启机制，成功在对抗性干扰和数据漂移环境下实现了Wasserstein后悔的次线性界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的在线学习多集中于点估计，而许多实际应用需要预测完整的概率分布。在数据存在非平稳漂移（drift）和对抗性干扰（adversarial corruption）的情况下，如何进行分布预测并获得理论保证是一个挑战。

Method: 提出了一种基于潜在聚类几何的在线分布预测框架，利用Gibbs准后验对配置进行平均，并采用可逆跳跃MCMC（Reversible-jump MCMC）处理变维后验采样。同时，为了应对数据漂移，引入了重启机制（Restarted variant）以实现局部化的准贝叶斯更新。

Result: 理论分析证明，在有界支撑、稳定的潜在几何结构、预测映射正则性等假设下，该方法能实现累积Wasserstein后悔的次线性增长。其误差界限分解为PAC-Bayesian复杂度、干扰敏感的后验扰动项和动态最优传输项。

Conclusion: 该研究通过在非平稳数据流和对抗性干扰下实现次线性的累积Wasserstein后悔，证明了所提出的非参数化、基于潜在聚类几何的分布预测方法的有效性。该方法无需预设参数模型即可处理复杂的数据分布动态变化。

Abstract: Online learning in non-stationary streams is often formulated as tracking a point estimate, but many applications require predicting the full data-generating distribution. We study online distributional prediction under drift and adversarial corruption. Our approach represents each candidate law through a latent cluster geometry: a variable-size configuration of centers that organizes probability mass and induces a predictive distribution. A Gibbs quasi-posterior over these configurations yields an online predictor by posterior averaging, and the resulting variable-dimensional posterior can be sampled with reversible-jump MCMC. The method therefore avoids specifying a parametric streaming law while retaining a structured latent space for uncertainty, regularization, and comparison.
  We evaluate performance by cumulative Wasserstein-1 regret against the time-varying true law. The analysis separates two effects: corruption perturbs the loss-based posterior update, whereas drift makes long-horizon posterior memory stale. We address the latter with a restarted variant that temporally localizes the same quasi-Bayesian update. The resulting high-probability bounds decompose into a PAC-Bayesian complexity term, a corruption-sensitive posterior perturbation term, and a dynamic optimal-transport term driven by \(A_T^{\mathrm{OT}}=\sum_{t=2}^T W_2^2(p_{t-1}^*,p_t^*)\). Under bounded support, stable latent geometry, predictive-map regularity, oracle realizability, localized restart windows, sublinear transport action, and sublinear corruption budget, the restarted predictor achieves sublinear cumulative Wasserstein regret. These guarantees require no parametric model for the stream, drift mechanism, or corruption process.

### [163] [Reinforcement Learning Foundation Models Should Already Be A Thing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18812)
*Abdelrahman Zighem,Jill-Jênn Vie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了通过合成马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）预训练强化学习基础模型的思路，利用注意力机制处理MDP的充分统计量，实现了在无需微调的情况下对多种强化学习任务的高效求解，填补了强化学习在基础模型领域的研究空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 利用合成数据作为训练基础，填补了强化学习缺乏大规模互联网数据的空白；2. 识别出MDP具有与片段观察无关的固定大小充分统计量，使其能够直接适配类似于TabPFN的基于注意力机制的架构；3. 将强化学习目标视为序列建模问题，通过以策略头替代监督学习头的方式进行预训练；4. 在完全合成的MDP环境下进行模型训练，并在多个基准测试中验证模型性能。

Abstract: Foundation models for language and vision are powered by internet-scale data, while structured domains (tabular prediction, time-series forecasting, graph learning, reinforcement learning) are not. The substitute is synthetic data, which shifts the burden from collection to prior design. Such priors already exist for many structured tasks: TabPFN and its successors solve tabular classification with a transformer pretrained on a synthetic Bayesian prior.
  We make two points. \textbf{First}, reinforcement learning is the conspicuous gap: sampling a synthetic MDP is as feasible as sampling a synthetic tabular dataset, yet no in-context RL work treats prior design as a primary objective. \textbf{Second}, MDPs admit a fixed-size sufficient statistic, independent of the episodes observed and tabular in shape, which makes them directly amenable to the attention-based architectures used for tabular foundation models, with a policy head replacing the supervised target. Together these define the agenda for an RL foundation model.
  As a proof of concept, we train one model entirely on synthetic MDPs and show that, with no task-specific tuning, it solves held-out tabular benchmarks in context, both online and offline: online, in far fewer episodes than UCB-VI and tabular Q-learning, and offline, competitively with VI-LCB.

### [164] [Maturing Markov Decision Processes: Decision Making under Increasing Information and Shrinking Action Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18820)
*Jiaxi Liu,Aiping Yang,Yuhang Yang,Shuqi Zhang,Zewei Dong,Jiangming Yang,Xuebin Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对顺序决策中信息增加与行动受限的不对称性，本文提出了“成熟马尔可夫决策过程”（MMDP）框架。通过显式建模这种不对称性并采用结构感知学习策略，显著提升了强化学习在复杂、大规模决策场景下的效率与效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）往往将决策过程扁平化处理，导致无法有效捕捉决策周期中“信息随时间丰富”与“可行行动因约束而减少”之间的嵌套不对称性，使得智能体难以区分哪些决策是紧急的、哪些是可以延迟的。

Method: 引入了“成熟马尔可夫决策过程”（MMDP）这一新颖框架，该框架专门针对信息-行动不对称性进行建模。在此基础上，开发了一种结构感知强化学习框架，包括：1. 阶段感知策略设计；2. 到期行动抽象（expiring-action abstraction）；3. 带有蒸馏的搜索增强学习。通过这些方法提取并利用了决策过程中的“到期行动优先原则”。

Result: 在受控的多供应商补货问题、日益复杂的现金管理环境以及生产规模的仿真实验中，MMDP框架相比传统方法表现出更高的学习效率，且随着问题规模的扩大，其性能优势愈发明显。

Conclusion: 本文提出的MMDP框架成功建模了顺序决策中的信息增长与行动约束不对称性，证明了显式地将这种结构融入强化学习模型可以显著提升学习效率与决策性能，特别是在复杂、大规模的决策任务中具有重要价值。

Abstract: Sequential decision problems often exhibit an asymmetric evolution of information and decision flexibility: as a decision cycle unfolds, the agent receives richer information while feasible actions expire due to operational cutoffs, commitments, or resource constraints. Standard MDP formulations typically flatten this structure into stage-dependent state descriptions and action masks, thereby obscuring the nested information--action asymmetry that determines which decisions are urgent and which can be deferred. We introduce Maturing Markov Decision Processes (MMDPs), a formulation built around this information--action asymmetry. We characterize one of its key consequences through an expiring-action priority principle, which identifies the actions that must be resolved before the next stage. Motivated by this structure, we develop a structure-aware reinforcement learning framework with stage-aware policy design, expiring-action abstraction, and search-augmented learning with distillation. Experiments on a controlled multi-supplier replenishment problem, simplified cash-management environments of increasing complexity, and a production-scale simulator show that explicitly modeling this asymmetry improves learning efficiency and becomes increasingly valuable as decision problems scale.

</details>


### [165] [STARE: Surprisal-Guided Token-Level Advantage Reweighting for Policy Entropy Stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19236)
*Haipeng Luo,Qingfeng Sun,Songli Wu,Can Xu,Wenfeng Deng,Han Hu,Yansong Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 LLM 强化学习中常见的策略熵坍缩问题，本文提出了 STARE 算法。通过分析发现 token 级信用分配错配是根本原因，该方法通过重加权关键 token 的优势并利用闭环门控机制维持熵稳定性，显著提升了复杂推理任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模语言模型（LLM）在使用 GRPO 等可验证奖励强化学习（RL）进行后训练时，常会出现策略熵坍缩（Policy Entropy Collapse）问题，导致模型过早收敛并失去探索能力。研究旨在分析该现象的机制并提出解决方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 STARE 的方法。首先通过一阶梯度分析识别出导致熵坍缩的 token 级信用分配错配，利用 batch 内部的 surprisal 分位数识别熵关键 token 子集，对其有效优势进行选择性重加权，并引入目标熵闭环门控机制进行稳定性调节。

Result: STARE 在 1.5B 到 32B 的多种模型规模及 Short CoT、Long CoT、多轮工具使用等任务上，实现了数千步的稳定 RL 训练；在 AIME24 和 AIME25 基准测试中，平均准确率较 DAPO 等基线提升了 4%-8%。

Conclusion: STARE 证明了通过对基于 surprisal 的关键 token 子集进行优势重加权并结合闭环熵门控机制，可以有效解决 GRPO 等算法中的策略熵坍缩问题，在保持探索与利用平衡的同时提升了模型推理性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards algorithms like GRPO have emerged as the dominant post-training paradigm for complex reasoning in LLMs, yet commonly suffer from policy entropy collapse during training. We conduct a first-order gradient analysis of token-level entropy dynamics under GRPO and identify a token-level credit assignment mismatch: the per-token entropy variation decomposes into the product of the trajectory-level advantage and an entropy sensitivity function over the next-token distribution, yielding an advantage-surprisal four-quadrant structure and a near-criticality property. Motivated by it, we propose STARE (Surprisal-guided Token-level Advantage Reweighting for policy Entropy stability), which identifies entropy-critical token subsets via batch-internal surprisal quantiles, selectively reweights their effective advantages, and incorporates a target-entropy closed-loop gate for stable entropy regulation. Across model scales from 1.5B to 32B and three task families (Short CoT, Long CoT, and Multi-Turn Tool Use), STARE sustains stable RL training over thousands of steps while maintaining policy entropy within the target band. On AIME24 and AIME25, STARE outperforms DAPO and other competitive baselines by 4%-8% in average accuracy, with reflection tokens and response length growing in tandem, indicating sustained exploration-exploitation balance that further unlocks RL training potential.Code is available at https://github.com/hp-luo/STARE.

</details>


### [166] [Target-confidence Recourse Using tSeTlin machines: TRUST](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18832)
*K. Darshana Abeyrathna,Sara El Mekkaoui,Nils Enric Canut Taugbøl,Anuja Vats*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TRUST 是一种能够显式控制预测置信度的反事实解释框架。它利用概率 Tsetlin 机直接搜索满足置信度要求的最小改动，从而生成比传统方法更稳健、更具可解释性的算法补救方案，特别适用于高风险决策场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的反事实解释方法多以跨越决策边界为唯一目标，导致生成的解释在噪声或模型变动下极其脆弱。在高风险决策中，用户不仅需要获得“正确”的决策，还需要该决策具有足够的置信度和风险保障，因此需要一种能直接控制预测置信度的补救生成框架。

Method: 该研究提出了 TRUST（Target-confidence Recourse Using tSeTlin machines）框架，核心方法包括：1. 利用概率 Tsetlin 机（PTM）建立预测结果与规则稳定性之间的联系；2. 结合贝叶斯优化直接搜索满足用户预设置信度阈值的最小改动，而非仅跨越决策边界；3. 通过评估规则激活的稳定性来区分反事实解释的可靠性。

Result: 实验结果表明，与传统的基于边界的方法相比，TRUST 生成的方案在保持低改动成本的同时，显著提升了补救的稳健性。在多个数据集上的测试显示其能够达到极高的稳健性（如 Haberman 数据集在 0.92 置信度下 L2 距离仅为 0.10），同时为决策过程提供了更透明的规则级稳定性信息。

Conclusion: TRUST 框架通过将预测置信度作为显式约束纳入反事实解释的生成过程，不仅提升了算法补救（Recourse）的稳健性，还通过 Tsetlin Machine 的规则机制提供了更高的可解释性。研究表明，控制置信度是实现高风险决策场景下可靠补救的关键。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations are widely used to provide algorithmic recourse in high-stakes decision-making systems. Most existing methods seek the smallest change to an input that flips a model's decision. However, decision-makers often rely not only on predicted labels but also on confidence thresholds and risk margins. Counterfactuals that barely cross a decision boundary can be fragile and unstable under noise or model variation.
  In this paper, we propose Target-confidence Recourse Using tSeTlin machines (TRUST), a framework in which users explicitly specify the desired prediction confidence for recourse. Rather than generating counterfactuals and evaluating confidence afterward, TRUST directly searches for minimal changes that satisfy a user-defined confidence target, enabling comparison of recourse options in terms of cost, confidence, and robustness.
  We instantiate TRUST using a Probabilistic Tsetlin Machine (PTM) combined with Bayesian optimization. The probabilistic clause-based structure of PTM links prediction confidence to the stability of decision rules. We show that counterfactuals satisfying the same rules can still differ substantially in reliability depending on how securely they satisfy those rules, revealing whether decisions are supported by robust or fragile clause activations.
  Experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that target-confidence counterfactuals produce more robust and interpretable recourse than conventional boundary-based approaches. Across multiple benchmarks, TRUST achieves perfect robustness while maintaining low recourse cost, including an L2 distance of 0.10 on the Haberman dataset at 0.92 confidence. By explicitly controlling confidence and exposing rule-level stability, TRUST provides actionable recourse for high-stakes decision support.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型中蕴含的知识虽然可用于复杂世界的结构化推理，但如何以概率论上一致的方式提取和使用这些知识是一个具有挑战性的难题。现有的单次自回归生成方法容易产生偏差，难以实现严谨的结构化概率推断。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Large Language Gibbs”的方案，将大语言模型的条件分布作为马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）算法中的转移算子。该方法通过迭代地重采样单个变量（基于其他变量的条件概率），而非单次自回归生成，从而消除生成顺序带来的偏见并逼近全局一致的平稳分布。

Result: 实验证明，该方法在合成概率分布采样、一致性推理任务以及贝叶斯结构学习中表现良好，能够比传统的单次生成方法更有效地获取结构化概率信息。

Conclusion: LLM Gibbs 采样提供了一种实用的替代方案，能够利用大模型作为概率推断的算子，在无需单次自回归生成的情况下，更有效地处理结构化概率推断和复杂的推理任务。

Abstract: The knowledge encoded in large language models (LLMs) can serve as a substrate for structured reasoning over variables describing a complex world, but accessing this knowledge in a probabilistically coherent manner poses a difficult inference problem. We propose Large Language Gibbs, a scheme for structured probabilistic inference that uses conditional distributions of an LLM as transition operators. Rather than sampling structured objects through single-pass autoregressive generation, we iteratively resample individual variables conditioned on others using an LLM's next-token conditionals. This approach avoids order-dependent biases and produces a stationary distribution that reflects a compromise between all local conditionals. We apply this approach to sampling from synthetic distributions, consistent reasoning tasks, and Bayesian structure learning. The results suggest that the use of LLM conditionals in MCMC is a practical alternative to one-pass generation for structured probabilistic inference under a world prior accessible through noisy LLM conditionals.

In production, anchor ambiguity and labeled-unlabeled mismatch can amplify systematic pseudo-label errors, leading to spurious triggers. We propose a stabilized MF-SSL framework with (i) Noise-Aware Decoupling, which removes ambiguity-prone anchors from the teacher's supervised update path, and (ii) kinematics-gated pseudo-labeling with a teacher conflict penalty to suppress mismatch-induced risk hallucinations on unlabeled data while maintaining broad coverage. *Nassir Mohammad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于统计对偶性的半监督聚类框架，通过将“聚类”视为“异常检测”的对偶问题，利用基于期望阈值的排除法自动识别噪声，从而在无需手动调参的情况下实现鲁棒的聚类，并在低标签需求下展现了优秀的性能与扩展性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 基于“a-contrario”统计推理和格式塔邻近原则，将聚类定义为满足零假设（均匀随机分布）且不包含异常点的最大子集；2. 采用Perception算法，利用期望阈值（E < 1）自动识别异常点，无需手动调整参数；3. 采用“以排除法进行聚类”（clustering-by-exclusion）的迭代机制，通过少量种子标签引导初始化，并逐步纳入非异常点以扩展簇群。

Abstract: This paper introduces a semi-supervised clustering framework grounded in the statistical duality between grouping principles and anomaly detection. We address the challenge of robust cluster definition in noisy environments -- a task where partitioning algorithms often over-assign outliers and density-based methods remain sensitive to heuristic global parameters. Drawing on \textit{a-contrario} statistical reasoning and Gestalt proximity principles, we define a cluster as a maximal subset of data points containing no anomalies relative to a null hypothesis of uniform randomness. Central to this approach is the Perception algorithm, which utilises a principled expectation-based threshold ($\mathbb{E} < 1$) to identify outliers without manual parameter tuning. By treating clustering as the dual of anomaly detection, we employ an iterative ``clustering-by-exclusion'' mechanism. The algorithm is seed-guided, leveraging minimal user-provided labels to initialise robust cluster medians and form initial groups, which are subsequently expanded by admitting non-anomalous points. This approach naturally isolates fringe points, isolated noise, and emerging unknown clusters. We evaluate the method on synthetic and real-world benchmarks, including image and text datasets represented through raw, linear-reduced, and neighbourhood-preserving embeddings. Results demonstrate that with as few as 10--30 seeds per cluster, the proposed method achieves competitive and often very strong performance under a practical low-tuning benchmarking protocol, while maintaining linear scalability with respect to both observations and dimensionality for a fixed number of seeded clusters and iterations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Causal discovery methods commonly assume that all data is independently and identically distributed (i.i.d.) and that there are no unmeasured variables affecting the system. In practice, these assumptions are often violated, leading to inaccurate inference. In this paper, we study how to identify hidden confounding and selection biases from causal mechanism shifts. In particular, we show that structural biases lead to dependent mechanism shifts. That is, by considering for which variables the mechanisms change given data from different environments, we can tell which variables are unbiased, which are subject to hidden confounding, and which are undergoing selection bias. We formalize this into an empirically testable criterion based on mutual information, and show under which conditions it identifies structural biases. To tell which nodes are subject to what kind of bias, we introduce the StruBI algorithm. *Peiyu Yang,Paul Montague,Feng Liu,Andrew C. Cullen,Amardeep Kaur,Christopher Leckie,Sarah M. Erfani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种首创的视觉语言模型（VLM）语义鲁棒性认证框架，通过文本提示模拟语义变化，无需额外训练数据即可定量计算模型预测的稳健区间，显著提升了VLM在应对语义变异时的可靠性评估能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的鲁棒性认证框架主要关注几何或像素级别的变换，而真实场景中VLM常面临由形状、大小、风格等语义变异引起的分布偏移。因此，需要一种能够针对语义层面变换进行鲁棒性认证的框架，以确保VLM在复杂实际应用中的可靠性。

Method: 利用视觉语言模型（VLM）的开放词汇能力，将文本提示作为语义变化的代理，构建由参数控制的语义变换。通过闭式解（closed-form）刻画VLM的决策边界，定量计算并认证在特定语义变换程度范围内预测结果保持不变的区间。

Result: 在合成数据和真实世界数据上的实验表明，该框架能够有效地对多种语义变化场景进行鲁棒性认证，且无需为每种变换获取额外数据，验证了其在实际应用中的实用性和有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功提出了一种针对视觉语言模型（VLM）在语义层面变换下的鲁棒性认证框架。通过利用VLM的开放词汇能力，该方法无需额外数据即可有效评估模型在不同语义变化程度下的预测稳定性，为提升VLM在真实世界应用中的可靠性提供了重要的理论与实践基础。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are now widely used in downstream tasks. However, real-world applications often expose VLMs to distribution shifts induced by semantic variation (e.g., shape, size, and style). Robustness certification determines if a model's prediction changes when transformations are applied to its input. While most certification frameworks study geometric or pixel-level transformations over inputs, this work proposes a novel framework that enables certifying VLM robustness under semantic-level transformations. Leveraging the open-vocabulary capability of VLMs, we use text prompts as semantic proxies to construct transformations parameterized by an extent that controls the degree of semantic variation. By characterizing the VLM decision boundary in closed form, our framework quantitatively certifies extent intervals for which the predicted class remains unchanged under the semantic transformation. Our framework is the first to certify VLM robustness under semantic-level variations without requiring additional data for each variation, making it practical to apply. Experiments on both synthetic and real-world data show that our framework enables certifying robustness under diverse semantic variations across scenarios.

### [173] [A Controlled Benchmark of Quantum-Latent GAN Augmentation for Brain MRI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18970)
*Syed Mujtaba Haider,Silvia Figini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过严格的基准测试发现，在医学影像增强任务中，量子生成器并未展现出比经典生成器更优越的性能或多样性，现有的性能增益更多是一种被动的正则化效应，而非实质性的数据生成优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管量子生成模型在医学影像分类任务中被宣称能提升准确率，但现有的相关研究缺乏严谨的对比基准（如未匹配参数规模、缺乏多次实验验证、未明确数据边界条件）。研究者旨在通过受控实验，剥离并评估量子生成器在医学影像数据增强中的实际贡献。

Method: 研究者构建了一个受控基准测试框架，在医学脑MRI数据上进行实验。他们利用KL正则化隐空间，训练条件Wasserstein GAN（含梯度惩罚），对比了具有近乎相同参数规模（1648个量子参数 vs 1632个经典参数）的量子生成器和经典生成器。通过在5%到100%的不同标签数据比例下进行多次随机种子实验，并结合配对显著性检验、多重比较校正、多样性评估及隐空间分布分析来评估模型表现。

Result: 实验结果表明，在所有标签数据比例下，使用量子生成器或经典生成器进行增强，均未能显著优于仅使用真实数据的训练效果。此外，量子生成器与经典生成器在统计上无显著差异。分析显示，合成样本存在严重的模式坍塌（mode collapse）和分布外偏移，其作用本质上更接近于一种正则化手段，而非有效的数据扩展。

Conclusion: 在医学影像数据增强任务中，现有的量子生成模型并未表现出优于经典模型的性能，且目前所谓的“性能提升”更倾向于是一种隐式的正则化效果，而非真正的数据扩展。该研究强调了在量子机器学习研究中进行严谨、可控的基准测试的必要性。

Abstract: Medical image classification is often constrained by limited labeled data, motivating generative augmentation; recently, quantum generative models have been proposed for this purpose, frequently reporting accuracy gains. However, such claims are typically based on single training runs, do not match the parameter budgets of the quantum and classical generators, and do not characterize the data regime in which any benefit appears. We present a controlled benchmark that isolates the contribution of a quantum generator to brain-MRI augmentation. Images are encoded into a KL-regularized latent space in which a conditional Wasserstein GAN with gradient penalty is trained using either a variational quantum generator or a classical generator of near-identical parameter count (1648 vs. 1632). Synthetic samples are decoded and used to augment a pretrained classifier across labeled data fractions from 5% to 100%, evaluated over eight random seeds with paired significance testing (with multiple-comparison correction) and with intraset diversity and latent-distribution analyses. Across all fractions, no augmentation variant significantly outperforms real-data-only training, and the quantum and classical generators are statistically indistinguishable. Any low-data benefit behaves as regularization rather than faithful data expansion:synthetic samples are off distribution and severely mode collapsed precisely where data is scarce, and the quantum generator is no more diverse thanits classical counterpart. We release the protocol as a testbed for rigorous evaluation of quantum generative augmentation in medical imaging.

</details>


### [174] [Learning from Your Own Mistakes: Constructing Learnable Micro-Reflective Trajectories for Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18844)
*Zhilin Huang,Hang Gao,Ziqiang Dong,Yuan Chen,Yifeng Luo,Chujun Qin,Jingyi Wang,Yang Yang,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TAPO 是一种通过对比正负样本并插入显式诊断与纠正逻辑来改进模型自蒸馏的方法，相较于传统的 KL 对齐，它能更精准地指导模型修正推理错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型自蒸馏方法通常依赖隐式的 KL 散度对齐，缺乏对特定错误模式的诊断能力和针对性的纠正引导，导致模型只是模仿分布而非真正理解错误逻辑。

Method: 提出轨迹增强策略优化（TAPO），核心包括：1. 对比结构：利用同一查询产生的正确与错误路径进行对比；2. 微观反射纠正：在错误发生点插入自然语言诊断与正确推理步骤；3. 难度感知候选选择：在能力边界处进行数据筛选；4. 解耦优势估计：防止梯度污染。

Result: 在 AIME 2024、AIME 2025 和 HMMT 2025 基准测试中，TAPO 在同等训练步数下表现均优于 GRPO，并有效增强了模型的首轮推理准确率及错误纠正能力。

Conclusion: TAPO 通过显式的轨迹构建替代了传统的隐式 KL 散度对齐，证明了针对推理错误进行微观反射式纠正能显著提升大模型的推理能力。这种方法有效地利用了模型自身的对比数据，为大模型的自我训练提供了更精准的优化方向。

Abstract: Self-distillation improves reasoning in large language models by using the model's own rollouts as training signal, typically through implicit logit-level alignment that minimizes KL divergence toward a privileged target distribution. However, because this supervision is generated via uncontrolled sampling, it provides no diagnostic insight into the model's specific errors or corrective guidance for its individual failure patterns. Consequently, the model learns to imitate a privileged distribution rather than receiving fine-grained corrections that pinpoint where and why its reasoning fails. In this paper, we propose Trajectory-Augmented Policy Optimization (TAPO), which advances self-distillation from implicit distributional alignment to explicit trajectory construction. During RL training, the model produces both correct and incorrect rollouts to the same query, and TAPO leverages this contrastive structure to construct micro-reflective corrections, new training trajectories that retain the model's erroneous reasoning up to the point of failure, then insert a natural-language diagnosis and corrected reasoning guided by a correct reference from the same sampling group. Since each trajectory is anchored in the learner's own prefix and solutions, the corrective signal preserves the model's on-policy distribution to a greater extent than the position-wise alignment imposed by KL-based methods. To integrate these trajectories, TAPO introduces difficulty-aware candidate selection at the model's capability boundary and decoupled advantage estimation to prevent gradient contamination. Experiments on AIME 2024, AIME 2025, and HMMT 2025 show that TAPO achieves consistent improvements over GRPO under the same number of training steps. Further analysis demonstrates that TAPO strengthens both first-pass reasoning and error-correction effectiveness.

</details>

*Oskar Bohn Lassen,Simon Driscoll,Stephen I. Thomson,Sebastian Schemm,Francisco C. Pereira*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者使用理想化的 Isca 模型生成了包含平流层爆发性增温（SSW）动力学的配对模拟数据，并对比评估了三种不同的机器学习架构：卷积神经网络（CNN）、Transformer 和图神经网络（GNN）。研究通过 Eliassen-Palm 通量诊断分析了模型的预测能力及物理一致性。

Result: 在平流层动力环境静稳时，各架构表现差异微小；但在 SSW 事件活跃期间，性能差距显著拉大。尽管模型表现出了较低的预测误差，但在分析波流相互作用时，发现模型在平流层波动驱动结构方面仍存在严重的物理一致性问题。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在模拟平流层动力学时，显式的三维垂直耦合结构是机器学习模型必需的关键归纳偏置。此外，低预测误差并不等同于物理上的真实性，模型仍可能在波流相互作用的结构上存在系统性偏差。

Abstract: Machine-learning emulators are increasingly used for weather prediction and have the potential to extend skill on subseasonal-to-seasonal timescales by learning dynamically important sources of predictability. A key challenge is whether the models can exploit predictability anchors, such as stratospheric variability, that influence tropospheric circulation beyond short lead times. We test how architectural inductive bias affects emulation of sudden stratospheric warming (SSW) dynamics using paired idealised Isca simulations that differ only in an imposed wave-2 heating perturbation. Across convolutional, transformer, and graph-based architectures trained for one-step prediction, model differences are modest when the stratosphere is dynamically quiet but widen substantially when SSW-like variability is active. Our results identify explicit three-dimensional vertical coupling as a key inductive bias for machine-learning emulation of stratospheric dynamics. However, Eliassen-Palm flux diagnostics show that low forecast error does not guarantee physically faithful wave-mean-flow interaction, with coherent errors remaining in stratospheric wave-driving structure.

### [176] [FoMoE: Breaking the Full-Replica Barrier with a Federation of MoEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19025)
*Lorenzo Sani,Zeyu Cao,Meghdad Kurmanji,Alex Iacob,Andrej Jovanovic,Yan Gao,Wanru Zhao,Nicholas D. Lane*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FoMoE 是一种新型的分布式训练系统，通过跨节点切分专家层而非复制全量模型，有效解决了地理分布环境下大模型训练的内存瓶颈与通信开销问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型训练通常依赖单数据中心内的高速互联。尽管现有的 DiLoCo 等方法尝试在地理分散、弱连接的中心进行训练，但它们仍需每个站点存储完整模型，导致内存占用过高且通信开销巨大。因此，需要一种能够打破“全副本”范式的新型分布式架构。

Method: 提出了 FoMoE 系统，核心创新在于通过“部分专家复制”（Partial Expert Replication）策略，不再要求所有工作节点存储完整的模型，而是将专家层跨节点分区存储。此外，引入了一种新颖的“跳过令牌”（Skip-token）机制来提高分布式环境下的吞吐量。

Result: 实验表明，FoMoE 在受限环境下相比高效基线降低了高达 1.42 倍的通信成本（相比 DDP 降低 45.44 倍），通过跳过令牌机制实现了最高 1.4 倍的吞吐量提升，并通过建模验证了其在 100B 参数规模下扩展的潜力。

Conclusion: FoMoE 通过在地理分布的计算节点间划分专家层，成功打破了传统 MoE 模型必须在每个站点保留完整副本的限制。该方法在显著降低通信开销的同时，保持了模型训练的稳定性和效率，为在受限带宽和分布式环境下训练超大规模模型提供了一种可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Pre-training Large Language Models (LLMs) typically demands large-scale infrastructure with tightly coupled hardware accelerators. While increasing model and dataset scale remains the dominant driver of performance, Mixture-of-Experts (MoEs) architectures have recently achieved state-of-the-art results by decoupling parameter count from computational cost. This efficiency enables training massive models on constrained compute budgets, yet it typically requires the high-speed interconnects of a single datacenter. To overcome these physical limits, recent approaches such as DiLoCo and Photon use low-communication data-parallel methods to enable scaling across geographically distributed, weakly connected data centers. However, these methods suffer from a fundamental inefficiency: they require full model replicas at every site, which imposes prohibitive memory constraints and communication overheads. In this work, we introduce FoMoE, a system that breaks the full-replica paradigm by partitioning expert layers across workers. We demonstrate that FoMoE: (I) reduces communication costs by up to 1.42x over efficient baselines and 45.44x over DDP via partial expert replication in the studied regimes; (II) achieves empirical throughput speedups of up to 1.4x through a novel skip-token mechanism; and (III) shows stable routing in the trained proxy regimes and projects the communication/memory benefits to 100B-scale configurations through system modelling.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: When algorithmic predictors inform resource allocation in high-stakes domains such as healthcare, these predictors must account for strategic manipulation of input features. The typical solution is to redesign the predictor itself to explicitly account for strategic interactions. In practice, however, decision makers are often constrained to adjusting coarser levers within existing prediction pipelines. For example, healthcare organizations often select which features to exclude based on perceived manipulability, while using standard regularization procedures to shrink the coefficients of retained features. In this work, we initiate a formal study of strategic classification through feature selection and its interaction with ridge regularization. Our main finding is that excluding individual features based on their manipulability alone is generally suboptimal. We provide a fine-grained characterization of the performance of a feature subset under optimal regularization, yielding new insights for policy design. Motivated by this characterization, we develop a practical algorithm for jointly choosing the feature set and the level of ridge regularization. Through a real-world case study on a healthcare payments benchmark, we illustrate how our algorithm can guide the design of coarse policy levers in practice. Our results provide a principled, practical framework for mitigating the effects of strategic behavior in algorithmic decision-making systems.

### [178] [A Hybrid LSTM--Vision Transformer Architecture for Predicting HRRR Forecast Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19026)
*David Aaron Evans,Jay C. Rothenberger,Kara J. Sulia,Nick P. Bassill,Chris D. Thorncroft*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合 LSTM-ViT 框架，通过融合地面观测的时间序列与垂直大气剖面信息，有效提升了对高分辨率数值天气预报模型误差的预测能力，尤其在处理降水等复杂对流过程时表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究开发了一个混合型 LSTM-Vision Transformer (LSTM-ViT) 架构。该模型利用 LSTM 处理地面观测站的时间序列数据，同时利用 Vision Transformer 处理来自垂直剖面观测网的大气剖面数据，以捕捉复杂的大气垂直演变过程，进而预测 HRRR 模型在降水、风速和温度方面的预报误差。

Previous work demonstrated that Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) networks can successfully predict forecast errors in the High-Resolution Rapid Refresh (HRRR) model using mesonet observations, but we believe performance degradation is linked to periods of complex vertical atmospheric evolution. To address this limitation, we develop a hybrid LSTM-Vision Transformer (LSTM-ViT) framework that combines temporal sequence learning from surface observations with atmospheric profiles from the New York State Mesonet profiler network. The LSTM-ViT framework is trained to predict HRRR hourly precipitation, 10 m wind speed, and 2 m temperature forecast errors at individual mesonet stations. Across all three predictors, incorporation of profiler-derived atmospheric structure improves forecast error prediction skill relative to the baseline LSTM architecture, with the largest gains occurring at shorter forecast lead times and during periods of enhanced PBL activity. Improvements are particularly pronounced for precipitation forecast error, where the LSTM-ViT framework achieves approximately a twofold increase in predictive skill relative to the baseline LSTM while better capturing convectively driven error evolution and reducing degradation associated with PBL processes. These results demonstrate that combining temporal sequence learning with vertically informed attention mechanisms provides a physically meaningful pathway for improving forecast error prediction in operational NWP systems. Our research offers forecasters enhanced guidance regarding model bias and forecast confidence.

### [179] [Anomaly Detection for Sparse and Irregular Multivariate Time Series with Latent SDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18898)
*Martin Uray,Dominik Geng,Florian Graf,Stefan Huber,Roland Kwitt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现实世界中时间序列不规则采样和数据缺失的问题，提出了一种基于潜变量随机微分方程（Latent SDEs）的异常检测方法，该方法在处理不规则数据时表现出比传统方法更优的性能和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多元时间序列异常检测方法大多假设数据是均匀采样的，这与现实世界中数据常存在稀疏、不规则采样或部分观测的情况不符，导致现有模型在处理真实场景数据时受限。

Method: 提出了一种基于潜变量随机微分方程（Latent SDEs）的生成式模型。该方法将观测到的时间序列投影到连续时间的随机动力系统中，从而直接处理稀疏、不规则采样或部分观测的数据，并能自然地捕捉时间序列中的周期性行为。

Result: 在六个异常检测基准数据集上的实验表明，该方法在性能上优于当前最先进的基准模型。特别是在面对严重的数据稀疏性时，该方法仍保持稳健，而对比基准模型性能则显著下降。

Conclusion: 潜变量随机微分方程（Latent SDEs）为多元时间序列异常检测提供了一种极其自然的归纳偏置，特别是在应对现实世界中数据不规则和缺失的挑战时，表现出极强的稳健性和优越性。

Abstract: Multivariate time series anomaly detection (MTSAD) is critical for a wide range of application areas, such as industrial monitoring, cybersecurity, or healthcare. Real-world data is often sparse, irregularly sampled or partially observed, yet existing methods assume uniformly sampled time series. We propose a generative approach based on Latent SDEs that projects the observed time series on a continuous-time stochastic dynamical system, directly being able to handle missing observations and irregular sampling, while also naturally capturing possible cyclic behavior that many real-world use cases inherently possess. Experiments on six anomaly benchmark datasets show that our proposed method ranks first among state-of-the-art baselines. We further demonstrate that our method remains robust under severe data sparsity, while performance significantly degrades for the tested baseline methods. These results highlight latent SDEs as a natural inductive bias for anomaly detection in multivariate time series, especially in presence of real-world irregularities.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present Pareto Q-Learning with Reward Machines (PQLRM), a multi-objective reinforcement learning algorithm for tasks whose reward structure is specified by a set of reward machines (RMs). PQLRM combines Pareto Q-Learning (PQL), which maintains sets of vector-valued Q-estimates to approximate the Pareto front, with enhancements from Q-Learning with Reward Machines (QRM), which exploits the factored automaton structure of the reward signal. This yields a multi-policy algorithm that remains sample-efficient under non-Markovian, RM-encoded rewards. Experimental trials show that PQLRM converges faster than a naive PQL baseline applied to the cross-product MDP and can synthesize Pareto-optimal policies that QRM cannot.

### [181] [OrthoReg: Orthogonal Regularization for Hybrid Symbolic-Neural Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19145)
*Till Richter,Niki Kilbertus*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对混合建模中神经网络组件“覆盖”物理符号结构导致模型不可解释的问题，本文提出了一种正交正则化技术（OrthoReg），通过强制物理模型与神经网络组件解耦，提升了模型的符号恢复能力与泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的混合动力系统建模方法（符号模型+神经网络）存在严重的冗余问题：当神经网络具备较强拟合能力时，往往会“吞噬”符号组件中的物理机制，导致模型失去可解释性。传统基于 $L^2$ 的正则化在符号结构通过稀疏发现时会失效，无法有效区分符号部分与神经网络部分。

Method: 作者提出了一种正交正则化方法（OrthoReg）。该方法在训练过程中直接惩罚符号组件与神经网络组件在函数空间上的重叠，确保神经网络只负责拟合符号部分无法解释的残差，从而避免了神经网络“重新学习”已知的物理结构。

Result: 在多个存在部分模型失配的基准动力系统实验中，OrthoReg 均优于现有基准方法，能够更准确地恢复正确的符号表达式，并在面对分布外（out-of-distribution）场景时展现出更好的预测鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OrthoReg 通过显式正则化手段有效解决了混合建模中物理模型与神经网络组件之间的冗余问题，实现了两者功能的正交解耦。这不仅提高了符号回归的恢复精度，还显著增强了模型在分布外数据上的泛化能力。

Abstract: Dynamical systems are fundamental to modeling the natural world, yet modeling them involves a persistent trade-off: manually prescribed mechanistic models are interpretable by design but often overly simplistic and misspecified; in contrast, flexible data-driven neural methods lack physical insight. Hybrid modeling aims for the best of both worlds by combining a prescribed or symbolic, physics-based component with a flexible neural network. A critical challenge, however, is that the neural component may relearn mechanistic parts, yielding redundant and uninterpretable models, especially when the symbolic structure itself is discovered from data. Existing methods based on standard $L^2$ regularization rely on a projection argument that breaks when the symbolic component is learned through sparse discovery, allowing the neural augmentation to overlap with symbolic structure. We introduce \textbf{OrthoReg} (Orthogonal Regularization), which directly penalizes overlap between the symbolic and neural components, preventing symbolic structure from being absorbed by the neural residual. This yields a complementary decomposition: the symbolic part captures what the library can express, and the neural part captures what remains. On benchmark dynamical systems with partial library mismatch, OrthoReg improves symbolic recovery and out-of-distribution behavior.

Conclusion: 本文通过理论分析确立了二值神经网络（BNN）验证问题的计算复杂性边界：对于通用可满足性问题，其计算复杂度为NP完全；但对于特定类型的输入扰动（如均匀遮挡），可以利用其分段常数特性实现多项式时间内的鲁棒性验证。

Abstract: This paper studies the computational complexity of verification problems for Binarized Neural Networks (BNNs), where activations (and sometimes weights) are binary. We analyze two problems: satisfiability and robustness under uniform image occlusion. We show that BNN satisfiability is NP-complete via a reduction from Boolean satisfiability problem (SAT), and that uniform occlusion induces a piecewise-constant structure in the network output, enabling a polynomial-time robustness-checking algorithm.

### [183] [Essential Subspace Merging for Multi-Task Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19164)
*Longhua Li,Lei Qi,Xin Geng,Qi Tian*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型合并方法难以解决源自同一预训练基座的多任务微调模型在参数更新时的相互干扰问题，旨在通过分析任务更新中输出偏移的能量分布，寻找减少干扰并保留知识的融合途径。

Method: 提出本质子空间分解（ESD）方法，通过分析激活偏移的能量分布，识别出携带任务信息的本质子空间；以此为基础，设计了静态融合方法（ESM）对本质组件进行正交化融合，并扩展为动态融合方法（ESM++），利用低秩专家和原型路由进行推理。

Result: 通过在多个任务集和模型规模上的广泛实验证明，ESM和ESM++能够显著降低任务间的干扰，在保持各任务性能的同时实现高质量的多任务模型集成。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的ESD、ESM及ESM++方法通过有效识别并解耦任务更新中的本质子空间，成功解决了模型合并中多任务干扰的核心难题，为无需训练的模型融合提供了高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Model merging aims to enable multi-task learning by integrating the capabilities of multiple models fine-tuned from the same pre-trained checkpoint into a single model. Its core challenge is inter-task interference among task-specific parameter updates. In this paper, we analyze the output shifts induced by task updates and observe that their energy is concentrated in a small number of principal directions. We call the subspace spanned by these directions the essential subspace. In contrast, most remaining directions carry little task-relevant energy, but their accumulation across multiple task updates can cause severe interference during merging. Motivated by this observation, we propose Essential Subspace Decomposition (ESD), which decomposes each task update according to the principal components of its activation shift. Based on ESD, we introduce Essential Subspace Merging (ESM), a training-free static merging method that orthogonalizes and fuses essential components into one compact multi-task model. We further extend ESM to ESM++, a training-free dynamic merging method that decomposes task-specific residuals into low-rank experts and selects the most relevant expert through prototype-based routing during forward inference. Extensive experiments across multiple task sets and model scales demonstrate that ESM and ESM++ effectively preserves task knowledge while reducing inter-task interference.

### [184] [GrapNet: A Programmable Dynamic-Architecture Neural Graph Substrate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18923)
*Zirong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GrapNet 是一种将神经网络定义为可编辑“图”的新型架构，允许直接对网络结构进行动态修改（如增删连接、冻结子图），在保持与传统模块兼容的同时，显著提升了模型在持续学习等场景下的可编程性和任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经网络主要基于固定张量结构，缺乏直接的“可编程性”。在需要对网络进行编辑（如审计、冻结子图、更改后端）时，只能进行复杂的参数“手术”，难以维护。研究者希望通过 GrapNet 实现一种以“图”为核心的神经网络表示，使架构编辑成为一种一等公民操作。

Method: 提出了 GrapNet 架构，将神经网络视为一个可执行的图模型。每个节点拥有指向下一层子节点的引用及对应的可训练分配向量。通过对图结构的直接操作（如添加、删除关系、冻结子图）来实现网络架构的重组，并将结构规则与执行策略与计算核心解耦，同时支持与传统神经网络模块的组合使用。

Result: 在可编程性压力测试中，GrapNet 表现优于传统的固定结构网络。在 Split Fashion-MNIST 任务中，GrapNet+ER 达到了 63.16% 的准确率（优于 dense MLP+ER 的 51.08%）；在 Split CIFAR-10 任务中，同样表现出显著的性能提升。

Conclusion: GrapNet 提供了一种具备结构可编程性的神经网络基底，通过将架构视为图，实现了对神经网络的动态编辑和灵活控制，证明了这种结构化方法比传统的固定张量网络在处理持续学习等任务时更具优势。

Abstract: Programmability is a missing first-class interface in fixed-tensor neural networks: editing a relation, freezing a subgraph, auditing a local function, or changing the execution backend should be an operation on the neural program rather than ad-hoc parameter surgery. GrapNet studies this graph-as-network setting. The graph is the architecture and executable program, not an input data graph. Each compute node owns its next-layer child references and a trainable allocation vector aligned with those references; deleting a relation physically removes both the child reference and the corresponding allocation coordinate. Structural rules and execution policies live outside the node core, so the same child-owned graph can be grown, frozen, structurally edited, grouped into trainable family blocks, routed by attention over active relations, or lowered to dense snapshots after topology stabilizes. GrapNet composes with conventional modules through a vector-valued parent interface: dense layers, CNN encoders, ResNet feature extractors, attention blocks, and transformer representations can all feed one sensory GrapNode per coordinate. The evaluation is organized as a programmability stress suite rather than as a new replay benchmark. In a matched ten-seed Split Fashion-MNIST study, a plastic GrapNet+ER head reaches 63.16 percent seen-class accuracy versus 51.08 percent for a parameter-larger dense MLP+ER under the same seen-class loss and replay memory, with paired delta 12.08 points and p=1.3e-5. On Split CIFAR-10 with a frozen ImageNet ResNet-18 encoder, the same substrate improves the online head over MLP-256 by 3.81 points, with p=0.0026. These results support GrapNet as an editable neural graph substrate whose core value is structural programmability with faithful execution views.

</details>


### [185] [Compute Efficiency and Serial Runtime Tradeoffs for Stochastic Momentum Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19179)
*Depen Morwani,Alexandru Meterez,Pranav Nair,Sham Kakade*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文量化分析了动量优化器（HB与ASGD）在大批次训练中“序列运行时间”与“计算效率”之间的权衡，揭示了动量如何通过扩大有效批次窗口来加速训练，并指出其性能表现高度依赖于数据特征谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机动量方法（如HB和ASGD）在现代深度学习训练中被广泛应用，但其在“序列运行时间”与“计算效率（CE）”之间的权衡机制尚不明确，尤其是大批次训练对计算效率的具体影响及其与动量机制的关系需要深入理论探讨。

Method: 通过对具有高斯协变量的相容线性回归问题进行建模，对随机重球法（HB）和加速随机梯度下降（ASGD）进行了有限维离散时间的批次大小权衡下界分析。并通过合成线性回归实验对理论结果进行了验证。

Result: 证明了HB方法不会改变SGD的CE前沿，而是扩大了能够维持SGD级别计算效率的批次窗口（可达 $\sqrt{\kappa}$ 倍）；ASGD在谱衰减较快时具有性能优势，但存在明显的计算效率与序列运行时间之间的权衡关系。

Conclusion: 研究表明，重球法（HB）在保持计算效率（CE）的同时，能通过增加批次大小来减少序列运行时间，其适用窗口比随机梯度下降（SGD）更大；而Nesterov动量（ASGD）的性能高度依赖于数据谱特征，在快速衰减的幂律谱下具有小批次优势，但会随着批次增大而牺牲计算效率以换取更快的序列收敛。

Abstract: Stochastic momentum methods such as heavy ball (HB), Nesterov momentum, and variants of Accelerated SGD (ASGD) [Kidambi et al., 2018] are widely used in modern training, but their stochastic benefits depend on two distinct quantities: serial runtime, the number of iterations needed to reach a target accuracy, and compute efficiency (CE), the inverse total gradient-query or FLOP cost. Larger batches reduce serial runtime without hurting CE only when the contraction gap grows linearly with batch size.
  We study stochastic HB and ASGD for consistent linear regression with Gaussian covariates and prove finite-dimensional, discrete-time lower bounds on their batch-size tradeoffs. Our first result shows that HB does not improve the CE frontier over SGD for arbitrary spectra; rather, it preserves SGD-level CE over a larger batch-size window, allowing larger batches to reduce serial runtime until HB reaches its deterministic accelerated scale. This window can be a factor $\sqrtκ$ larger than the SGD critical batch size. For ASGD, the picture is more spectrum-dependent: for rapidly decaying power-law spectra, ASGD improves small-batch CE over HB/SGD, but as batch size grows it trades this CE advantage for improved serial runtime. Synthetic linear-regression experiments verify these qualitative regimes, including near-overlap of ASGD and HB for slowly decaying spectra and the predicted CE--serial tradeoff for rapidly decaying spectra.

Our key insight is that task-agnostic rewards, which combine intrinsic model uncertainty with extrinsic semantic consistency informed by protein representation models, exhibit strong correlation with controllability measures across base models and temperature regimes. Moreover, PLMs fine-tuned with unsupervised rewards can achieve consistently higher coverage compared to their base model in pass@k evaluations. Motivation: 电动汽车普及给电力系统带来压力，基于强化学习的智能充电调度虽能有效缓解问题，但在现实中常面临关键特征（如离店时间）缺失的挑战。现有的两阶段方法（先预测后决策）中，预测模型通常仅关注预测精度，导致误差累积并限制了决策质量。因此，需要一种方法来优化预测以适配决策需求。

Method: 提出了一种决策导向的强化学习（DF-RL）框架。该方法采用端到端的训练方式，将预测器（用于估计缺失的离店时间等关键特征）与强化学习控制器进行联合优化，使预测器的训练目标直接与后续决策的质量挂钩，从而减少了预测误差对控制策略的负面传播。

Result: 实验结果表明，该DF-RL方法优于传统基线模型，在总奖励方面提升了最高14%，并将未供能电量（即因离店导致的充电失败）减少了55%。

Conclusion: 决策导向的强化学习（DF-RL）框架通过实现预测模型与决策模型的端到端联合训练，能够有效弥补关键特征缺失带来的不确定性，显著提升电动汽车充电调度的整体性能，证明了在特定决策任务中，优化预测模型以提升决策效果优于单纯优化预测准确率。

Abstract: The recent growth of EV adoption poses challenges for power systems, including increased peak demand and potential grid instability. Smart control of EV charging -- e.g., based on reinforcement learning (RL) -- can alleviate these issues by learning temporal and contextual patterns from historical data. Yet, in real-world scenarios, key features, such as departure time, often are unavailable. This, in turn, makes it harder for an RL agent to learn and execute an effective charging policy. To mitigate this uncertainty, a trained forecaster can approximate the unknown features from available data. However, since these forecasting models are typically trained for accuracy (rather than their impact on a downstream agent's decision quality), their errors may propagate and hinder the overall performance of a controller that is using the forecasts. To avoid this, we propose a decision-focused RL (DF-RL) framework in which the forecaster is trained end-to-end, i.e., with feedback from the charging policy actions taken by the RL agent. Such joint training of both the forecaster and controller ultimately results in higher-quality actions: our proposed DF-RL method yields superior charging decisions compared to other baselines, achieving up to a 14% improvement in total reward and a 55% reduction of unsupplied energy (i.e., charging that failed to happen because the EV already left), relative to the RL method without departure time forecasting.

</details>


### [188] [Online Reward-Punishment Learning from Fixed-Channel Perceptual Event Streams without Environment Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18963)
*Zirong Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种无需外部奖励的在线学习框架（OHIRL），通过内部评估机制和残差动态建模，让智能体在仅有感知数据的情况下，自主推断环境价值并实现最优决策，解决了奖励稀疏或缺失环境下的学习难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强化学习高度依赖外部标量奖励或评估标签，但在许多现实场景中，这些信号往往缺失。本研究旨在探讨智能体如何在没有外部奖励、仅有原始感知数据输入的情况下，通过环境交互自主推断出感知维度（如疼痛、能量等）的价值（正向或负向），并基于此习得有效的行为策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为OHIRL的在线奖励-惩罚学习框架，该框架包含四个核心模块：M_psi负责下一时刻感知包预测，D_omega负责建模残差动力学，C_eta作为固定的内部评估器（基于恢复正向、持续/增长负向的残差调节准则），B_xi负责利用价值证据进行策略更新和动作评分。通过条件误差分解来分离证据估计误差与策略优化误差。

Result: 在2x2-XOR任务中，B_xi达到了0.952的奖励符号准确率；在全在线交错审计中，M_psi的R2预测值为0.907，B_xi的符号准确率为0.940，最优动作准确率高达0.979。对比实验显示，即时感知分数、预测误差奖励等基准方法在这些任务上均失效。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在缺乏外部显式奖励的情况下，智能体可以通过对感知维度的残差动态和转换后果进行推理，从而成功习得价值导向和最优策略。该框架验证了感知包的价值不是固定的，而是取决于上下文和环境后果，且该方法在各种复杂任务中表现出极高的鲁棒性和准确性。

Abstract: We study online reward-punishment learning when the environment provides no scalar reward or evaluative label. At each step the agent receives only a fixed-channel perceptual packet, and quantities such as pain, energy, contact, damage, or cognitive error are treated as perceptual dimensions whose valence must be inferred from transition consequences. OHIRL separates four roles: M_psi learns next-packet prediction, D_omega models residual dynamics, C_eta is a fixed internal post-transition trajectory evaluator, and B_xi learns to use the resulting value evidence for later policy updates and action scoring. C_eta uses a recovery-positive and persistence/growth-negative residual-regulation orientation; a coefficient-origin audit shows that equal-unit, raw-equal, and random monotone variants preserve more than 92% of the released top-action rankings, while sign inversion preserves 0%.
  The reward-free protocol exposes observation transitions while withholding environment rewards, delayed external evaluators, success labels, and action-goodness labels. A conditional error decomposition separates B_xi evidence-estimation error from residual policy-optimization error. In a 2x2-XOR packet task, medicine and chili acquire opposite value under visual XOR contexts, and the same pain or spice increase can be positive or negative depending on consequence structure; B_xi reaches 0.952 balanced reward-sign accuracy. In a full online-interleaved audit, M_psi reaches holdout R2=0.907, B_xi reaches 0.940 sign accuracy, and the policy reaches 0.979 optimal-action accuracy, while immediate packet scores, prediction-error rewards, shuffled targets, zero reward, and error-reduction controls collapse. Hidden-reward CartPole and Taxi controls, public-context no-leakage audits, and module-role ablations further test information boundaries and component necessity.

### [190] [EfficientRollout: System-Aware Self-Speculative Decoding for RL Rollouts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18967)
*Minseo Kim,Minjae Lee,Seunghyuk Oh,Kevin Galim,Donghoon Kim,Coleman Hooper,Harman Singh,Amir Gholami,Hyung Il Koo,Wonjun Kang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EfficientRollout 是一种针对 LLM 强化学习训练的加速框架，通过自推测解码和系统感知的动态策略，解决了策略演进导致的推测失效和计算资源浪费问题，显著降低了训练延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大型语言模型（LLM）的强化学习训练中，序列化的推测生成成为主要的延迟瓶颈。现有的推测解码技术在 RL 场景中效果不佳，原因在于：策略的不断演进导致固定草稿模型逐渐失效，且强化学习过程中动态变化的批处理大小使得系统在计算密集型和内存密集型之间波动，导致传统的并行验证机制难以发挥最大效益。

Method: 提出了一种名为 EfficientRollout 的系统感知型自推测解码框架。该方法主要包含两个核心策略：1. 利用目标模型的量化版本作为“自我”草稿模型（无需额外的预训练或在线适配），确保草稿与演进中的策略保持同步；2. 设计了一种系统感知的切换策略与接受率感知的草稿长度动态调整机制，仅在有利的计算区间进行推测，并根据草稿质量实时调整推测规模。

Result: 实验结果显示，EfficientRollout 在加速自回归（AR）生成基线的基础上，将强化学习 Rollout 阶段的延迟降低了最多 19.6%，端到端训练延迟降低了 12.7%，且完全保留了最终模型的生成质量。

Conclusion: EfficientRollout 通过自推测解码（Self-SD）机制，有效克服了强化学习（RL）训练中因策略演进导致的推理延迟瓶颈，在保持模型性能的同时显著提升了训练效率，为大语言模型的强化学习后训练提供了一种系统级的加速解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a representative post-training paradigm for LLMs, enabling strong reasoning and agentic capabilities. However, rollout generation remains a dominant latency bottleneck because autoregressive sampling decodes responses sequentially and a small number of long-tailed generations often determine completion time. Speculative decoding (SD) offers a natural way to address this bottleneck, as it is a well-established technique for serving fixed LLMs that reduces latency by rapidly drafting tokens and accepting them through parallel verification while preserving the target-model distribution. However, its practical speedups do not directly carry over to RL rollouts: (i) the evolving target policy makes any fixed drafter increasingly mismatched with the policy's output distribution; and (ii) active batch sizes shrink throughout rollout decoding, shifting decoding from compute-bound to memory-bound regimes where parallel verification can exploit underutilized compute. Therefore, accelerating RL rollouts requires both a drafter that remains effective under long, high-temperature generations from an evolving policy and system-aware use of SD that avoids compute-bound regimes. We present EfficientRollout, a system-aware self-SD framework designed to address this gap for RL rollouts. EfficientRollout induces a quantized drafter from the target model (i.e. self-speculative decoding), keeping it coupled to the evolving policy without separate drafter pretraining or online adaptation. It further coordinates a system-aware SD toggle policy with acceptance-aware draft-length adaptation, enabling speculation only in beneficial regimes while matching the drafting budget to evolving drafter quality. EfficientRollout reduces rollout and end-to-end latency by up to 19.6% and 12.7%, respectively, over an accelerated AR rollout baseline, while preserving final model quality.

</details>

*Chenyu Zhou,Qiliang Jiang,Shuning Wu,Xu Zhou*

TL;DR: 本文提出了MAST方法，通过精准定位并选择性更新模型中的关键注意力投影张量，实现了在遗忘特定推理能力的同时，极大地保护了模型在其他任务上的原有性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的全参数梯度上升方法在实现机器遗忘时会导致严重的附带损害（即遗忘目标的同时损害了模型在其他基准测试上的表现），因此需要一种更具选择性和机制导向的遗忘方法。

Method: MAST（机制对齐选择性目标定位）：通过计算注意力投影张量的“离主能量”（off-principal energy）、更新幅度和遗忘梯度耦合度进行排名，仅更新排名靠前的张量子集，而非进行全参数更新。

Result: 实验表明，MAST在Qwen2.5-Math和Qwen3模型上均能实现统计学意义上的目标遗忘（如MATH测试集成绩下降），同时保持或仅轻微影响GSM8K及其他保留集的性能，相比全参数更新具有显著优势。

Conclusion: MAST是一种高效的机器遗忘方法，能够通过对注意力投影张量进行机制导向的选择性更新，在实现特定推理能力遗忘的同时，最大限度地减少对模型其他任务能力的附带损害。

Abstract: We propose MAST (Mechanism-Aligned Selective Targeting), a mechanism-guided method for unlearning RLVR-induced reasoning with substantially lower collateral damage than standard full-parameter updates. In matched SFT/RLVR checkpoints on Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B and Qwen3-1.7B-Base, the SFT-to-RLVR increment differs sharply from the SFT update in token-level delta-log-probability, and full-parameter gradient ascent forgets only by damaging retain MATH and GSM8K. MAST ranks attention-projection tensors by off-principal energy, update magnitude, and forget-gradient coupling magnitude, then updates only the top-ranked subset. On the primary model, MAST induces statistically significant target forgetting (MATH forget 45/150 to 37/150; McNemar p=0.0078) while preserving GSM8K (+0.8 pp) and MATH retain (-0.5 pp). The advantage reproduces across seeds, NPO/SimNPO objectives, and Qwen3, where MAST preserves GSM8K while full-parameter unlearning collapses it.

### [192] [DIPHINE: Diffusion-based $Φ$-ID Neural Estimator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18997)
*Simon Pedro Galeano Munoz,Mustapha Bounoua,Giulio Franzese,Pietro Michiardi,Maurizio Filippone*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 DIPHINE，一种基于扩散模型的新型神经估计器，解决了 ΦID 在非高斯连续复杂系统中的应用难题，实现了对系统冗余、唯一和协同信息的高效分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的集成信息分解（ΦID）计算方法主要局限于高斯或离散系统，无法处理复杂的连续非高斯动力学系统。为了揭示真实世界复杂系统的潜在信息架构（如如何存储、共享和整合信息），需要一种能够处理更广泛数据类型的通用评估框架。

Method: 作者提出了 DIPHINE（基于扩散的 Φ-ID 神经估计器），利用基于分数的扩散模型来共同估计 ΦID 所需的所有互信息项。该方法通过单个摊销神经网络（amortized network）进行学习，并通过莫比乌斯反演（Möbius inversion）恢复十六个基本原子，从而无需预先假设系统的数据分布。

Result: 实验结果表明，DIPHINE 在合成基准测试中能够准确恢复真实的信息原子，在处理互信息估计方面优于现有方法。此外，该方法成功应用于真实生理数据，在无需分布假设的前提下提取出了具有生理意义的信息动力学结构。

Conclusion: DIPHINE 填补了非高斯连续系统在集成信息分解（ΦID）研究中的空白。该方法通过扩散模型克服了分布假设的限制，为复杂系统的信息动力学分析提供了一个通用且可扩展的评估框架。研究还揭示了ΦID原子估计中的误差传播规律，特别是确认了协同原子（synergy-to-synergy）在计算上的挑战性。

Abstract: Uncovering the true informational architecture of real-world complex systems requires disentangling how their components uniquely store, redundantly share, and synergistically integrate information over time. Integrated Information Decomposition ($Φ$ID) is a framework for decomposing the information dynamics of multivariate systems into sixteen non-overlapping atoms that characterize redundant, unique, and synergistic modes of information storage, transfer, and integration. Existing methods to compute $Φ$ID are restricted to Gaussian or discrete systems, preventing its application to continuous non-Gaussian dynamical systems. We address this limitation by proposing DIPHINE (Diffusion-based $Φ$-ID Neural Estimator), the first neural estimator that leverages score-based diffusion models to jointly estimate all the mutual information terms required by $Φ$ID from a single amortized network, recovering the sixteen atoms through Möbius inversion. We provide a theoretical analysis of error propagation through the inversion, showing that the Jacobian of the mapping from mutual informations to atoms is integer-valued and that the synergy-to-synergy atom is provably the hardest to estimate. We demonstrate accurate recovery of ground-truth atoms on synthetic benchmarks, superior performance compared to established mutual information estimators, and the ability to extract physiologically interpretable information-dynamic structure on an application involving real data without any distributional assumptions.

</details>


### [193] [Explaining Attention with Program Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19317)
*Amiri Hayes,Belinda Li,Jacob Andreas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将Transformer模型中的注意力头“代码化”的方法，利用语言模型生成可执行的Python程序来拟合注意力模式。实验证明，这些程序不仅能高度还原注意力行为，还能在保持模型性能的同时有效替代神经注意力头，实现了模型行为的符号化解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决深度学习中“黑盒”模型缺乏可解释性的问题，试图用人类可理解的符号描述（如可执行的Python程序）来替代不透明的神经计算，以增强模型行为的透明度和可控性。

Method: 该方法通过以下步骤实现：1. 计算注意力头在样本上的注意力矩阵；2. 利用预训练语言模型将矩阵信息总结并生成可重现注意力模式的Python程序；3. 在保留数据集上对生成的程序进行重排序和验证。最终，通过将表现最好的程序替换原有的神经网络注意力头，评估其对模型整体性能的影响。

Result: 研究表明，使用不到1000个生成的Python程序即可重现GPT-2、TinyLlama-1.1B和Llama-3B中注意力头的行为，在TinyStories数据集上实现超过75%的平均IoU相似度。此外，将25%的注意力头替换为程序替代品后，模型困惑度（perplexity）平均仅增加16%，且在多个下游问答基准测试中保持了原有性能。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种可扩展的管道，通过人类可读的可执行代码对Transformer模型中的注意力头进行逆向工程，成功将神经网络的隐式计算转化为显式的符号描述，为实现神经模型的可解释性和符号透明度提供了重要途径。

Abstract: A longstanding goal of research on interpretable deep learning is to replace opaque neural computations with human-meaningful symbolic descriptions. In this paper, we propose an approach for approximating the behavior of components of deep networks with executable programs. We focus on attention heads in transformer language models. For a given head, we first compute its associated attention matrices on a collection of randomly selected training examples. Next, we prompt a pre-trained language model with a summary of these matrices, and instruct it to generate a set of Python programs that can reproduce the associated attention patterns given only text from the input sentence. Finally, we re-rank programs according to how well our final set of programs predict behavior on held-out inputs. We demonstrate that a set of fewer than 1,000 such generated programs can reproduce the attention patterns of heads in GPT-2, TinyLlama-1.1B, and Llama-3B, achieving an average Intersection-over-Union similarity above 75% on TinyStories. Moreover, the best-fit programs can replace neural attention heads without substantially affecting model behavior: replacing 25% of attention heads with programmatic surrogates across the three models incurs only a 16% average perplexity increase, while maintaining performance on a variety of downstream question answering benchmarks. This work contributes a scalable pipeline for reverse-engineering attention heads in transformer models using human-readable, executable code, advancing a path toward symbolic transparency in neural models.
