### [194] [UBP2: Uncertainty-Balanced Preference Planning for Efficient Preference-based Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19328)
*Mohamed Nabail,Leo Cheng,Jingmin Wang,Nicholas Rhinehart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对基于偏好的强化学习中样本效率低的问题，提出了一种基于模型的探索算法 UBP2，通过联合建模奖励、动力学和价值函数的不确定性，实现了高效的主动探索与规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于偏好的强化学习方法多依赖被动数据收集，导致样本效率低下，特别是在学习初期阶段。缺乏一种有效的主动探索机制来协调奖励学习与行为策略优化。

Method: 提出了一种名为“不确定性平衡偏好规划”（UBP2）的基于模型的强化学习方法。该方法利用奖励模型、动力学模型和价值函数的集成（ensemble）来量化认识论不确定性，并通过统一的得分函数（结合预期奖励、终端价值和不确定性）指导主动探索与规划。

Result: 实验结果表明，在 Meta-World 基准测试中，UBP2 的样本效率显著优于现有的无模型偏好学习方法以及非乐观的基于模型的基准方法。此外，该方法在理论上满足有限和无限时域下的次线性遗憾（sublinear regret）保证。

Conclusion: UBP2 提供了一种在基于偏好的强化学习中平衡开发与探索的有效框架，通过理论保证和实验验证，证明了在模型环境下利用多维不确定性评估能够显著提升学习效率。

Abstract: Preference-based RL provides an approach to learning reward models from pairwise comparisons of behaviors, bypassing the need for explicit reward design. However, existing methods typically rely on passive data collection and suffer from poor sample efficiency, especially during the early stages of learning. We introduce a model-based approach that actively directs exploration by jointly reasoning over uncertainties in the reward, dynamics, and value functions. Our method, Uncertainty-Balanced Preference Planning (UBP2), uses ensembles of reward, dynamics, and value function models to evaluate candidate trajectories according to a unified score that combines expected reward, terminal value, and epistemic uncertainty. Planning under this objective yields an explicit tradeoff between exploitation and information acquisition without requiring ad hoc exploration heuristics. Under standard regularity assumptions, we establish sublinear regret guarantees for both finite-horizon and infinite-horizon settings. Empirically, experiments on the Meta-World benchmark show UBP2 achieves substantially higher sample efficiency than model-free preference-based methods and non-optimistic model-based baselines.

</details>


### [195] [Geometric and Stochastic Analysis of Discontinuities in Sparse Mixture-of-Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19036)
*Tho Tran Huu,Huu-Tuan Nguyen,Thien-Hai Nguyen,Nhat-Tri Ho,Viet-Hoang Tran,Tho Quan,Tan Minh Nguyen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究从几何和随机角度揭示了SMoE模型中不连续性的分布规律，指出一阶不连续性是影响模型性能的主要因素，并提出了一种低开销的平滑策略以提升模型的稳定性和预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏专家混合模型（SMoE）通过Top-k路由实现规模化，但这种路由机制引入了内在的不连续性。在不连续面附近，极小的输入扰动会导致激活专家集剧烈波动，进而引发输出的不稳定性。研究旨在从理论上剖析这些不连续性的几何结构和随机行为，并寻求缓解方案。

Method: 1. 几何分析：利用测度论切片（measure-theoretic slicing）论证不连续表面的渐进体积估计；2. 随机分析：利用扩散过程建模输入扰动，分析随机路径触及不连续面的概率及停留时间（occupation-time）；3. 改进算法：提出一种针对不连续区域的轻量化平滑机制，通过在不连续点附近软化专家选择来提升模型表现。

Result: 研究证明了高阶不连续集合在输入空间中体积几乎为零，低阶（一阶）不连续性占据主导地位。此外，实验表明提出的平滑机制不仅增强了模型的连续性，还在多项语言和视觉任务中实现了性能提升。

Conclusion: 本文通过几何与随机分析揭示了SMoE模型中不连续性表面的本质，证明了一阶不连续性在输入空间中占据主导地位。基于此，提出的轻量级平滑机制在不显著增加计算开销的前提下，有效改善了模型的连续性并提升了在语言和视觉任务上的经验性能。

Abstract: Sparse Mixture-of-Experts (SMoE) architectures are now widely deployed in state-of-the-art language and vision models, where conditional routing allows scaling to very large networks. However, this very Top-$k$ expert selection that enables conditional routing also renders the SMoE map inherently discontinuous. In the vicinity of these discontinuity surfaces, even inputs that are arbitrarily close may activate substantially different sets of experts resulting in significantly different outputs. In this work we give a rigorous geometric and stochastic analysis of these discontinuities. We first classify them by order, determined by the number of tied experts at a switching event. Using measure-theoretic slicing arguments, we establish asymptotic volume estimates for the thickened discontinuity surfaces, showing that lower-order discontinuity sets dominate, whereas higher-order ones occupy a vanishingly small relative volume. Next, modeling random perturbations in the input space via a diffusion process, we prove that the path eventually encounter a discontinuity, and moreover that the first hit almost surely occurs on an order-1 discontinuity with explicit finite-time probability bounds. We further derive occupation-time bounds that quantify the duration the random path spend in the neighborhoods of each discontinuity order. These theoretical results imply that inputs are more likely to lie near lower order discontinuities. Motivated by this insight, we propose a simple smoothing mechanism that can be directly applied to existing SMoEs, softly incorporating experts near discontinuities; our analysis guarantees that the added computational overhead remains small while providing localized smoothing near discontinuities, and experiments across language and vision tasks show that smoothing not only enforces continuity of the SMoE map but also enhances empirical performance.

</details>


### [196] [Smoothness-Based Derandomization of PAC-Bayes Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19105)
*Alexandre Lemire Paquin,Brahim Chaib-Draa,Philippe Giguère*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了平滑损失函数下的PAC-Bayes去随机化问题，提出了一种基于参数平滑性（雅可比和海森矩阵）的泛化边界，并将该理论转化为实用的神经网络正则化方法，有效改善了模型在CIFAR-10上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PAC-Bayes理论通常侧重于随机预测器（Gibbs预测器），但实际应用中通常使用确定性预测器。现有的理论框架在处理平滑损失函数时，缺乏将随机预测器的泛化保证转化为确定性预测器时精确代价的量化分析，本文旨在弥补这一理论空白并将其应用于神经网络的正则化设计。

Method: 本文提出了一种利用损失函数和预测器类的平滑性质，通过分析Jensen差类（Jensen gap class）的Rademacher复杂度，将Gibbs预测器的泛化界推广到确定性预测器的方法。文中利用参数的雅可比矩阵（Jacobians）和海森矩阵（Hessians）来刻画预测器的“平滑度”（flatness），并将其转化为一种可计算的正则化项，特别针对BatchNorm神经网络进行了优化计算。

Result: 研究证明了从Gibbs预测器切换到后验均值预测器的泛化差距由Jensen差类的Rademacher复杂度决定。所得理论边界揭示了参数平滑度（通过雅可比和海森量度量）对泛化误差的影响，并将该结果成功应用于线性预测器和神经网络。在CIFAR-10数据集上的实验表明，基于该理论导出的正则化器能够有效提升模型性能，且对不同批处理大小具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过量化从Gibbs预测器转换到确定性预测器（后验均值）的代价，建立了平滑损失函数下的PAC-Bayes泛化界。这种基于雅可比矩阵和海森矩阵的平滑性度量不仅为理解神经网络的泛化性能提供了理论视角，还导出了有效的正则化策略，实验证明该方法在处理具有BatchNorm的网络时具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: We study PAC-Bayes derandomization for smooth loss functions. Our goal is to obtain generalization bounds that hold with high probability for deterministic predictors by exploiting smoothness properties of both the loss and the predictor class. We show that passing from the Gibbs predictor to the deterministic predictor at the posterior mean has a precise cost, given by the generalization gap of the Jensen gap class. We control this class through its Rademacher complexity, leading to bounds for deterministic predictors that involve flatness quantities expressed in terms of parameter Jacobians and Hessians of the score map. The framework applies to both bounded and unbounded smooth loss functions, and we specialize the results to linear predictors and smooth neural networks. Finally, the Jacobian and Hessian quantities appearing in the theory motivate a practical regularizer. For BatchNorm networks, we compute this regularizer with respect to effective BatchNorm weights obtained by folding the BatchNorm transformation into the adjacent affine weights. Experiments on CIFAR-10 illustrate the behavior of this regularizer under different batch sizes.

Abstract: Sequence modeling has become increasingly popular in recommendation and ranking algorithms, owing to its capacity to model users' historical behaviors and infer user intentions. For example, in Airbnb, guest sequences are often long, exploratory and complex, and we focus on booking labels, which are sparse. As such, we are often required to make various design decisions regarding data and modeling to strike a balance between effectiveness and scalability. This work delved into these production challenges and deployed JourneyFormer, a sequence modeling solution for search ranking at Airbnb. We detail crucial design considerations, covering aspects such as guest event selection, ID embeddings, model architecture, and label attribution. Additionally, we describe several tailored strategies to accelerate model training and inference. JourneyFormer has been successfully deployed within Airbnb's production, where its effectiveness and impact have been evidenced not only by improved offline ranking metrics but also by significant gains in key business metrics through online A/B testing across 2 production surfaces.

### [198] [Seeing Before Reasoning: Decoupling Perception and Reasoning for Shortcut-Resilient Multimodal On-Policy Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19120)
*Sihan Wang,Xiyao Liu,Lianqing Liu,Zhi Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ViGOS 是一种针对多模态大模型的视觉接地自我蒸馏框架，通过引入视觉描述任务并配合多层级教师监督机制，有效克服了传统蒸馏方法中模型过度依赖文本而忽视图像信息的“捷径”问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型领域表现优异的“在线策略自我蒸馏”（OPSD）方法直接迁移至多模态模型（MLLM）时，存在严重的“文本捷径”风险，即模型往往更倾向于根据文本参考答案预测 Token，而非真正结合图像信息进行推理。为了解决这一制约多模态模型视觉接地能力的瓶颈，作者提出了 ViGOS 框架。

Method: ViGOS 框架提出了“先视觉描述，后逻辑推理”的两阶段生成模式。其核心在于采用了分层级的监督策略：1. 对于高质量的输出，引入一个仅依赖图像的感知教师来监督视觉描述，确保信息对齐；2. 使用特权推理教师监督推理过程和最终答案；3. 仅在模型输出无效时，才引入参考教师进行格式修复。这种方式有效阻断了模型直接依赖文本标签而忽略图像信息的捷径学习。

Result: 实验结果表明，ViGOS 在广泛的视觉-语言任务（包括通用视觉语言理解、专家推理、视觉数学、空间接地以及视觉先验评估）中，不仅保留了自我蒸馏带来的推理性能优势，还显著提升了模型对图像信息的依赖度和视觉接地精度，在容易产生“文本偏置捷径”的任务设置中表现尤为突出。

Conclusion: ViGOS 框架有效地解决了多模态大模型在自我蒸馏过程中存在的文本偏置捷径问题。通过分离视觉描述感知与逻辑推理任务，并结合多层级的教师监督策略，该方法显著增强了模型在处理视觉信息时的接地能力（grounding），在多个视觉-语言推理基准测试中均表现出优于现有方法的性能，验证了其在提升多模态推理能力方面的有效性。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) trains a model on its own rollouts and uses a frozen copy to provide dense token-level targets conditioned on a reference target. This works well for LLM reasoning, but a direct extension to multimodal large language models (MLLMs) can create a shortcut: the privileged target may guide tokens mainly based on the text reference target rather than the image. We propose ViGOS, a visually grounded OPSD framework for MLLM post-training. The student first writes a visual description and then reasons toward the final answer. For valid rollouts, an image-only perception teacher supervises the description, while a privileged reasoning teacher supervises the reasoning and final answer on the same student prefix. A reference teacher is used only for invalid rollouts to recover the output format. Across general vision-language, expert reasoning, visual math, spatial grounding, and visual-language-prior benchmarks, ViGOS keeps the main benefits of OPSD and improves image-grounded behavior in shortcut-prone settings.

### [199] [INDEQS: Informed Neural controlled Differential EQuationS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19138)
*Michael Detzel,Gabriel Nobis,Kristiyan Blagov,Juri Schubert,Jackie Ma,Wojciech Samek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有图神经网络在时序预测中忽略已知拓扑结构的问题，本文提出了INDEQS框架，通过在NCDE中嵌入有向图先验，显著提升了预测精度与模型效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于图的神经控制微分方程（NCDE）方法通常仅从数据中学习空间结构，忽略了许多现实场景中已知的有向图先验知识。为了解决这一局限性，作者旨在构建一种能够有效利用已知图结构来增强连续时间序列预测能力的方法。

Method: 提出了Informed Neural Controlled Differential Equations (INDEQS)框架，将先验有向图知识融入NCDE的两个关键架构位置：一是“内部混合”（inner mixing），即在隐藏状态传播时施加图约束；二是“外部混合”（outer mixing），即在向量场与控制输入之间引入图结构信息。同时，提供了轻量级的图约束变体和通过自适应图卷积学习补充连接的扩展变体。

Result: 在合成的平流模拟数据集及河流流量预测、交通流预测（PeMS08）等真实世界任务中，INDEQS在参数量相当的情况下，其外部信息整合方式显著降低了平均绝对误差（MAE），证明了在模型中显式引入图先验知识的有效性。

Conclusion: INDEQS通过在NCDE架构中整合已知的有向图结构，显著提升了时序预测的准确性和参数效率。研究表明，在预测任务中显式利用图先验知识（即informedness）优于纯数据驱动的结构学习，特别是在复杂网络场景中。此外，连续时间解码器在处理时间序列时表现出比离散解码器更强的灵活性和准确性。

Abstract: Neural Controlled Differential Equations (NCDE) provide a powerful continuous-time framework for forecasting time series, but standard graph-based extensions typically learn spatial structure purely from data, even in settings where a directed graph structure is known a priori. We introduce Informed Neural controlled Differential EQuationS (INDEQS), a graph-based NCDE forecasting method that incorporates prior knowledge of a directed graph at distinct architectural positions. INDEQS separates inner mixing of hidden states across graph nodes from outer mixing between vector field and control, and offers both a lightweight graph-constrained variant and a more expressive variant, learning additional graph connections from data via adaptive graph convolutions. To systematically study when graph informedness is beneficial in forecasting, we devise a continuous advection simulation on directed graphs, yielding synthetic spatio-temporal datasets with known ground-truth flow structure. We then evaluate INDEQS on two real-world tasks: river discharge forecasting on a hydrological network and traffic flow prediction on PeMS08. Across these synthetic and real-world benchmarks, outer informedness consistently improves mean absolute error over an uninformed NCDE with comparable parameter count, particularly on larger graphs, while inner informedness offers a more parameter-efficient alternative when strict adherence to a known adjacency is desired. A comparison of discrete convolutional and continuous-time decoders further shows that continuous decoders yield better accuracy and greater temporal flexibility on real-world tasks. An implementation of INDEQS and the advection simulation is available at https://github.com/Mitchi1/indeqs.

</details>

In this work, we propose ChronoSurv, a heterogeneous hierarchical directed graph framework for multimodal survival analysis. ChronoSurv represents patient care as a progression-aware clinical trajectory using directed graphs aligned with key diagnostic steps. A hierarchical topology incorporates fine-grained, coarse, and global representations, further supporting flexible adaptation to missing modalities, while heterogeneous message passing models complex and asymmetric relationships across modalities and clinical steps. Experimental results on two public datasets demonstrate that ChronoSurv achieves state-of-the-art discriminative performance while maintaining statistically reliable calibration. ### [201] [Complementary Attention Head Pruning for Efficient Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19150)
*Yaniv Livertovsky,Shahar Somin,Gonen Singer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Transformer模型压缩，本文提出了一种无需梯度、基于图论的自动剪枝框架CAHP，通过互补性分析保留模型关键注意力头，在提升压缩效果的同时解决了传统剪枝方法中结构退化和超参数依赖的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型参数量巨大，限制了其在资源受限环境下的部署。现有的结构化剪枝方法通常依赖梯度或随机门控，存在训练不稳定、结构退化及需要繁琐超参数调优等缺陷。因此，研究人员寻求一种更稳定、无需手动调优且能更好保留模型关键结构的剪枝框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为CAHP（互补注意力头剪枝）的后处理框架。该方法将注意力头的选择定义为全局图论问题，通过基于图的聚类算法结合信息论距离度量，自动识别并保留具有拓扑多样性的互补注意力头集合，且无需预设剪枝比例，通过识别性能下降曲线的边际递减点来自动决定保留的头数。

Result: 在SST-5和MNLI基准测试中，CAHP在不同规模的Transformer模型上均优于现有的竞争基线方法，特别是在高压缩比场景下效果显著。结构分析显示，CAHP有效地规避了梯度类方法倾向于仅保留靠近输出层头的缺陷，从而保留了模型中间层的关键功能注意力头。

Conclusion: CAHP提供了一种无需梯度信息、自动且稳定的Transformer注意力头剪枝方案。通过将剪枝建模为图论问题，该方法不仅在压缩率较高时表现优异，且能有效规避梯度剪枝方法中常见的“邻近偏差”问题，保留了对模型功能至关重要的中间层注意力头，从而实现了更高效的模型压缩。

Abstract: The remarkable success of Transformer-based models in natural language processing stems from architectural scaling, which leads to a large number of parameters and hinders deployment in resource-constrained environments. While structured pruning offers a pathway to compression, existing state-of-the-art methods often rely on gradient-based importance ranking or stochastic gating, which suffer from instability, structural degeneration, and the need for extensive manual hyperparameter tuning. In this paper, we introduce CAHP (Complementary Attention Head Pruning), a novel post-hoc framework that redefines head selection as a global graph-theoretical problem. Rather than evaluating heads in isolation, CAHP utilizes graph-based clustering combined with information-theoretic distance measures to identify and preserve a topologically diverse subset of complementary attention heads. Without requiring a predefined sparsity level or pruning ratio, the framework automatically determines the number of selected attention heads across layers by identifying a diminishing marginal performance curve, where pruning additional heads leads to a sharp degradation in performance, as determined by the chosen polynomial degree. Extensive evaluations on the SST-5 and MNLI benchmarks, across different Transformer model scales, demonstrate that CAHP consistently outperforms competitive baselines, particularly in high-compression regimes. Furthermore, our structural analysis shows that CAHP avoids the "proximity bias" of gradient-based pruning methods, which tend to preserve heads mainly in layers close to the output, and instead retains a functionally critical set of attention heads in the model's intermediate layers.

</details>


### [202] [The Reward Was in Your Data All Along: Correcting Flow Matching with Discriminator-Guided RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19162)
*Nicolas Beltran-Velez,Felix Friedrich,Zhang Xiaofeng,Reyhane Askari-Hemmat,Xiaochuang Han,Adriana Romero-Soriano,Michal Drozdzal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对生成模型在训练损失与感知质量间的结构失配问题，本文提出了一种判别器引导的强化学习（DRL）方法，通过利用预训练特征空间的判别器引导模型向真实数据分布对齐，在无需人类反馈的情况下显著提升了图像生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评分模型和流匹配模型在训练时依赖于均方误差（L2）的回归损失，这与推理时的视觉质量和语义连贯性之间存在结构性偏差。而依赖人类偏好的强化学习虽能缓解此偏差，但成本高昂且受主观因素干扰。因此，作者旨在寻找一种无需人工反馈、直接对齐数据分布的有效优化方案。

Method: 提出判别器引导强化学习（DRL）。该方法训练一个在预训练表征空间中区分真实数据与模型样本的判别器，利用其Logit值作为KL正则化强化学习的奖励函数，直接优化模型以匹配数据分布。

Result: 在多个模型（如SiT, JiT等）上取得了显著效果，无引导下的FID值大幅下降（如SiT从9.38降至2.62），语义空间FD值显著改善，并在无需人工偏好数据的情况下提升了图像质量与偏好奖励。

Conclusion: DRL提供了一种无需人类反馈的高效对齐方法，通过结合预训练判别器与强化学习，既优化了图像保真度，又改善了后续偏好对齐的帕累托前沿，为生成模型性能提升提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: Score- and flow-matching models often rely on preference-based reinforcement learning for two purposes: aligning with subjective preferences and, surprisingly, recovering properties such as visual realism and coherent object structure that matching-based training is intended to learn from the data itself. We argue that this reflects a structural mismatch. Matching losses measure $\ell_2$ regression error on the velocity or score field under training-time marginals, a proxy poorly aligned with the visual and semantic properties that determine sample quality at inference. Given a reward aligned with these properties, RL sidesteps the mismatch by evaluating the model on its own samples and following the reward landscape directly. The challenge is to obtain such a reward without relying on human preferences, which are expensive and conflate data realism with annotator inclinations.
  We propose Discriminator-Guided RL (DRL). DRL trains a discriminator to separate data from base-model samples in a pretrained representation space and uses its logit as the reward in KL-regularized RL. The pretrained space restricts the discriminator to perceptually meaningful directions, and the logit estimates the log-likelihood ratio between data and model, which is the optimal reward for targeting the data distribution. Across SiT, JiT, REPA, and RAE, DRL reduces guidance-free FID (e.g., $9.38 \to 2.62$ on SiT) and semantic-space FD (e.g., $88.2 \to 19.3$ on DINOv3 for SiT), with consistent gains across all backbones, and improves human-preference rewards without training on them. It also yields a better Pareto frontier between preference reward and image fidelity under subsequent preference-based post-training, increasing alignment while reducing low-level artifacts such as oversaturation and excessive brightness.

</details>


### [203] [AGDN: Learning to Solve Traveling Salesman Problem with Anisotropic Graph Diffusion Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19185)
*Bolin Shen,Ziwei Huang,Zhiguang Cao,Yushun Dong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 AGDN 的新型图神经网络框架，通过 MixScore 矩阵和各向异性图扩散策略，有效增强了对 TSP 问题图结构的建模能力，实现了求解性能与泛化性的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决现有基于图学习的旅行商问题（TSP）求解器中存在的两个核心难点：一是全连接 TSP 图缺乏足够的信息化拓扑先验；二是常用的图稀疏化技术会导致最优解中的关键连接被过早丢弃。

Method: 提出各向异性图扩散网络（AGDN），主要包括：1. 构建 MixScore 转移矩阵，融合了节点相似度和成对距离，以提供更优的拓扑先验；2. 开发各向异性图扩散策略，支持在多跳邻域间进行高效的信息交换，避免了传统图稀疏化方法导致的信息丢失。

Result: 在多种规模和分布的 TSP 实例上，AGDN 均取得了优于现有基准方法的求解结果，且在未见过的实例规模和数据分布上展现出良好的泛化性能，同时保持了具有竞争力的计算时间。

Conclusion: AGDN 通过各向异性图扩散机制，有效解决了 TSP 问题中图结构利用率不足的挑战，不仅在性能上超越了现有方法，还表现出极强的泛化能力和计算效率，为组合优化问题的神经求解提供了一种高效的新框架。

Abstract: The Traveling Salesman Problem (TSP) is a cornerstone of combinatorial optimization and arises in many practical scenarios. Although graph-based learning approaches have been explored for TSP, the question of how to exploit graph structure more effectively remains open. We present the Anisotropic Graph Diffusion Network (AGDN), a new Graph Neural Network framework designed to solve TSP. Our method tackles two central difficulties: (1) the lack of informative topological prior in fully connected TSP graphs, and (2) losing connected nodes in the optimal solution after the commonly used graph sparsification techniques. To overcome these issues, we construct a MixScore transition matrix that merges node similarity with pairwise distance, and we develop an anisotropic graph diffusion strategy that supports efficient information exchange across multiple hops. Comprehensive experiments spanning diverse instance sizes and node distributions show that AGDN consistently outperforms existing methods while keeping computation time competitive. Furthermore, AGDN generalizes well to problem sizes and distributions beyond those seen during training. The implementation is publicly available at: https://github.com/LabRAI/AGDN.

### [204] [A Human-in-the-Loop Bayesian Optimization Framework for Constraint-Aware Bioprocess Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19230)
*Samuel Stricker,Claus Wirnsperger,Alessandro Butté,Laura Helleckes,Gonzalo Guillén Gosálbez,Antonio del Rio Chanona,Mehmet Mercangöz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的贝叶斯优化通常仅提供单一自动化建议，难以处理复杂工程场景下包含约束条件、鲁棒性要求以及专家主观偏好的多目标折衷问题，因此需要开发一种支持人机交互、能同时考虑性能、约束和鲁棒性的优化框架。

Method: 1. 约束处理：将满足输出规格限制的后验概率作为帕累托目标，通过高斯过程（GP）后验分布进行解析计算。
2. 鲁棒性优化：采用蒙特卡洛采样策略，在用户定义的输入扰动范围内估计预期的置信下限性能。
3. 交互式可视化：通过交互式仪表盘，以成对的二维投影形式展示性能、不确定性、约束和鲁棒性之间的多维权衡。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将约束优化和鲁棒性纳入多目标帕累托框架，显著增强了人机交互贝叶斯优化（HitL-BO）的实用性。通过可视化工具使专家能够直观地权衡性能、不确定性、约束满足度和鲁棒性，从而在复杂工程任务（如生物工艺开发）中实现更科学、高效的资源配置和决策过程。

Abstract: This work presents an extension to Pareto Front Guided Sampling (PFGS), a Human-in-the-Loop (HitL) Bayesian Optimization (BO) framework in which Gaussian process (GP) surrogate-derived quantities are reformulated as objectives of a multi-objective optimization problem, and the resulting Pareto front is exposed to a domain expert for interactive candidate selection rather than returning a single automated recommendation. The framework is extended in two directions: constrained optimization is addressed by incorporating the posterior probability of satisfying output specification limits as an explicit Pareto objective, computed analytically from the GP posterior distribution; robust optimization is addressed by a Monte Carlo sampling strategy that estimates expected lower-confidence performance over a user-defined variability of input perturbations, capturing performance degradation under likely implementation deviations. The resulting multi-dimensional Pareto representation renders trade-offs between predicted performance, model uncertainty, probabilistic constraint satisfaction, and input robustness simultaneously visible through pairwise two-dimensional projections on an interactive dashboard, enabling selection criteria to be iteratively refined as the surrogate model improves and development objectives evolve. The framework is showcased on an eight-dimensional fed-batch Chinese Hamster Ovary (CHO) cell culture simulator demonstrating systematic identification of high-performing, feasibility-compliant, and perturbation-resilient operating conditions, and illustrating how expert-defined requirements provide a principled stopping criterion and support informed allocation of experimental resources.

*Xingze Zheng,Hanyin Cheng,Siyuan Wang,Yiting Hao,Peng Chen,Yuan Jun,Yang Shu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于重建的时间序列异常检测方法普遍面临“过拟合”与“欠拟合”之间的平衡难题（即过度泛化或泛化能力不足），导致难以精确识别异常。

Method: 提出了一种名为SCAN的框架：1. 在表征层引入多尺度聚类，利用正常模式的聚类中心来约束重建过程，防止模型过度拟合或泛化；2. 在异常判定层，结合聚类归属概率与重建误差，构建双重异常得分指标；3. 通过提取邻域中心表征进行多视图聚类，进一步优化聚类效果。

Result: 在多个真实世界的应用数据集上进行了广泛实验，结果表明SCAN模型在多领域时间序列异常检测任务中达到了最先进（State-of-the-Art）的性能水平。

Conclusion: 本文提出的SCAN模型通过多尺度聚类机制，有效解决了时间序列异常检测中重建模型存在的泛化能力失衡问题，通过表征约束和双重异常判定准则，显著提升了检测的鲁棒性和准确性。

Abstract: Time series anomaly detection plays a crucial role in a wide range of real-world applications. Reconstruction-based methods have become the mainstream paradigm, but they suffer from over-generalization and under-generalization problems, which are challenging to balance. To address this, we introduce multi-scale clustering to enhance reconstruction-based methods. At the representation level, we integrate the cluster center representations of normal patterns to constrain the model to target representative normal patterns for reconstruction, preventing dominance of powerful capacity and representation capability. At the anomaly criterion level, we derive anomaly confidence score based on cluster membership probability and combine it with reconstruction error, providing dual criteria for detection. Furthermore, the effectiveness of the cluster center representations and anomaly confidence score depends on the clustering performance. Accordingly, we extract neighborhood-centered representations for multi-view clustering to improve clustering performance. Extensive experiments on multiple real-world datasets from diverse application domains demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of SCAN.

Conclusion: 利用NVML遥测技术构建的GPU工作负载分类器具有很强的鲁棒性。尽管存在对抗性攻击，但该方法仍能保持较高的识别率，证明了在不访问敏感模型信息的情况下，通过物理特征监控GPU计算行为是可行且有效的AI治理手段。

We evaluate the adversarial robustness of GPU workload classification using only zero-overhead, privacy-preserving NVML telemetry: content-agnostic signals that observe physical effects of computation without accessing model weights, training data, or hyperparameters. Across 5 rounds of monitor-evader iteration, we evaluate 20 evasion strategy families on 9 GPU models spanning 4 architecture generations. We develop a classifier that achieves 98.2% binary accuracy at identifying training workloads across the whole corpus, and 43-87% accuracy against the most challenging unexpected workloads even when they are adversarially disguised.

### [208] [Does VLA Even Know the Basics? Measuring Commonsense and World Knowledge Retention in Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19297)
*Nikita Kachaev,Andrey Moskalenko,Matvey Skripkin,Nikita Kurlaev,Daria Pugacheva,Albina Burlova,Mikhail Kolosov,Denis Shepelev,Andrey Kuznetsov,Elena Tutubalina,Aleksandr I. Panov,Alexey K. Kovalev,Vlad Shakhuro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Act2Answer评估协议，将常识问答任务转化为具身动作任务，旨在明确区分VLA模型在知识保留与运动控制方面的缺陷，揭示了VLA模型在复杂知识上的性能损耗及其内部特征的分布规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型通常由预训练VLM微调而来，但微调过程对模型原有常识和事实知识保留的影响尚不明确。现有评估方法难以区分模型失败是归因于知识缺失还是低级控制能力的泛化不足。

Method: 提出了Act2Answer评估协议：将知识问答转化为桌面场景下的动作选择任务，通过物体放置动作来体现回答。构建了覆盖多样化常识和世界知识的测试套件，并结合分层意图探测（layerwise intent probing）技术，追踪VLM主干网络及动作头中与回答相关的信息流。

Result: 通过对7个VLA模型和9个VLM基线的对比评估发现：VLA在简单概念上表现较好，但在丰富语义类别上性能下降明显；VQA协同训练能有效提升模型知识保留率；通过探测发现，与答案相关的信号在VLA模型中间层最强，而在顶层有所衰减。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了Act2Answer作为评估具身VLA模型知识保留能力的有效方法。结果表明，VLA模型在简单概念上表现稳健，但在复杂语义知识上与原VLM存在显著差距。此外，VQA联合训练对知识保留有正向作用，且关键语义信息主要分布在模型的中层。

Abstract: Embodied Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are typically obtained by fine-tuning powerful pretrained VLMs on robotics data, yet it is unclear how much commonsense and factual knowledge they retain after adaptation. Failures on knowledge-sensitive tasks are ambiguous, conflating missing knowledge with poor generalization of low-level control. We introduce Act2Answer, a lightweight protocol that adapts VLM knowledge benchmarks to VLA evaluation by requiring agents to answer through action. Each question becomes a short tabletop episode where the agent performs a single object-placement action to select among candidate answers, yielding an action-grounded success rate with reduced control confounds. We curate a test suite of such environments across diverse commonsense and world-knowledge categories and introduce layerwise intent probing to localize answer-relevant information across the VLM backbone and action head. In a large-scale study of 7 VLA models and 9 VLM baselines, we systematically rank models across categories, finding that VLAs show solid performance on simple concepts while exhibiting larger gaps on richer semantic categories relative to their source VLMs, that VQA co-training is associated with better knowledge retention, and that answer-relevant signals peak in middle VLA layers but attenuate in upper layers. Act2Answer is available at https://tttonyalpha.github.io/act2answer/.

</details>


### [209] [P-K-GCN: Physics-augmented Koopman-enhanced Graph Convolutional Network for Deep Spatiotemporal Super-resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19303)
*Xizhuo,Zhang,Zekai Wang,Fei Liu,Bing Yao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对非规则几何结构的时空超分辨率难题，本文提出了一种物理增强的Koopman图卷积网络（P-K-GCN），通过结合动力学算子理论与物理约束损失，在保证计算效率的同时显著提升了重建的物理准确性与泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时空超分辨率方法在处理非规则几何结构时表现不佳，且纯数据驱动模型往往缺乏物理一致性，难以在计算成本受限的情况下实现高精度的时空动力学重建。

Method: 提出了一种名为P-K-GCN的物理增强Koopman算子图卷积网络。核心方法包括：1.利用基于连续样条的图卷积网络（GCN）处理非规则几何空间依赖；2.引入Koopman算子理论将非线性动力学映射至线性演化的潜在空间；3.通过物理约束损失函数优化模型，并从理论上证明了该方法通过降低Rademacher复杂度及收紧泛化界限来减少重建误差。

Result: 在心脏电生理学等非规则三维几何结构的实验中，P-K-GCN模型在超分辨率任务上的预测精度显著优于现有的基准模型，验证了其物理增强机制和Koopman算子对提升重建保真度的有效性。

Conclusion: P-K-GCN提供了一种将物理先验与动力学算子理论相结合的有效框架，通过图神经网络解决非规则几何问题，显著提升了时空超分辨率重建的准确性、鲁棒性及泛化能力。

Abstract: High-fidelity simulation of spatiotemporal dynamics is computationally prohibitive, necessitating efficient super-resolution techniques to reconstruct high-resolution data from coarse-grained inputs. Traditional data-driven methods often lack physical constraints, and simple physics-informed learning struggles with irregular spatial geometries and intricately evolving temporal dynamics. To tackle these challenges, we propose a Physics-augmented Koopman-enhanced Graph Convolutional Network (P-K-GCN) for spatiotemporal super-resolution on irregular geometries. Specifically, a continuous spline-based GCN is first designed to extract spatial dependencies directly from coarse graph, and Koopman operator theory is incorporated to project the nonlinear dynamics into a compact latent space where temporal progression is linearized. Second, we augment the optimization objective with a physics-based loss to force the data-driven reconstructions to adhere to physical laws for improving predictive fidelity and robustness. Finally, we provide a rigorous theoretical analysis, establishing that the physics augmentation and Koopman regularization mathematically guarantees a reduction in super-resolution error by diminishing Rademacher complexity and tightening generalization bounds. We evaluate our framework on reconstructing spatially high-resolution cardiac electrodynamics across a 3D heart geometry from sparse low-resolution measurements. Numerical experiments demonstrate that our method achieves superior accuracy compared to baseline models.

</details>


### [210] [Diffusion-Proof: Recipe for Formal Theorem Proving Beyond Auto-Regressive Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19315)
*Ruida Wang,Rui Pan,Pengcheng Wang,Shizhe Diao,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了首个用于形式化定理证明的扩散模型框架 Diffusion-Proof，通过全证明生成和基于扩散的局部修正模型，有效克服了传统自回归模型在长程推理上的缺陷，显著提升了数学证明任务的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自回归语言模型（AR LLMs）在形式化定理证明中存在长程连贯性差、误差累积等局限，而扩散模型（dLLMs）通过多标记块的迭代去噪生成，有望克服这些问题，但在形式化数学领域的应用尚处于起步阶段。

Method: 提出 Diffusion-Proof 框架：包括 dLLM-Prover-7B（用于全证明生成，具备长程连贯性）和 dLLM-Corrector-7B（利用扩散模型的填充能力进行局部证明修正，结合双向信息进行迭代去噪）。

Result: 实验结果显示，Diffusion-Proof 在 ProofNet-Test 和 MiniF2F-Test 基准测试中分别取得了 1.61% 和 6.14% 的绝对性能提升，并成功解决了一个 DeepSeek-Prover-V2-7B 无法攻克的 IMO 题目。

Conclusion: Diffusion-Proof 框架证明了扩散模型在形式化数学证明领域具有超越传统自回归模型（AR LLMs）的潜力，特别是在长期连贯性和错误修正方面表现出独特的优势，为形式化证明提供了一种新的研究范式。

Abstract: Enhancing the formal math reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) has become a key focus in both mathematical and computer science communities in recent years. While significant progress has been made in using state-of-the-art Auto-Regressive (AR) LLMs for formal theorem proving, these models suffer from inherent limitations. Their next-token prediction generation methods may yield suboptimal performance due to the challenges of long-range coherence and the compounding of errors over long sequences. Recent advancements in diffusion LLMs (dLLMs), which generate text through iterative denoising of a multi-token block, offer a promising alternative. However, the application of dLLMs to formal mathematics, where maintaining long-range coherence is critical, remains largely understudied. To address the challenges above, we propose **Diffusion-Proof**, to the best of our knowledge, the first framework to train and apply dLLMs for formal theorem proving. Our frameworks contain training and inference methods for two models. The first one is *dLLM-Prover-7B*, which performs whole-proof writing with long-range coherent tactic usage. The second one is *dLLM-Corrector-7B*, which is a novel large block diffusion-based correction model. It leverages the in-filling capabilities of dLLMs to perform local proof correction using bi-directional information. Extensive experiments demonstrate that **Diffusion-Proof** relatively significantly outperforms the AR LLM baseline trained under the same dataset. **Diffusion-Proof** achieves an absolute improvement of **1.61%** on ProofNet-Test and **6.14%** on MiniF2F-Test benchmarks compare to the baseline. Notably, **Diffusion-Proof** successfully resolves one IMO problem that more advanced thinking model DeepSeek-Prover-V2-7B could not solve, showcasing the unique advantage of dLLMs in formal theorem proving.

</details>
